
-----title
曲江 (出生地)

-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0a15abae8ff846febe201dcfe383433f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0a15abae8ff846febe201dcfe383433f");'><span id='0a15abae8ff846febe201dcfe383433f_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年</a>　秋间，九龄应韶州赴广州应乡试。乡试中举后，旋被选贡入京应户部试。本次赴试途中疑作有诗。作品：《初发道中寄远》<div id='poem_22741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22741' class='poemTitle gray;'>▪</span>道经广州，有使至广州诗，并辟周子谅充岭南按察判官。作品：《使至广州》《送广州周判官》<div id='poem_22748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22748?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_22785'>海郡雄蛮落，津亭壮越台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22785_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22785'>城隅百雉映，水曲万家开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22785_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22785'>里树桄榔出，时禽翡翠来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22785_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22785'>观风犹未尽，早晚使车回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22785_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22785'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22785_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7cd755329b2747efae070a35c392410c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7cd755329b2747efae070a35c392410c");'><span id='7cd755329b2747efae070a35c392410c_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　春应进士考，考功郎沈佺期尤所激扬，使其一举高第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='265e2b3ac69c43d6b05009b2b400845c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("265e2b3ac69c43d6b05009b2b400845c");'><span id='265e2b3ac69c43d6b05009b2b400845c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=708')">706-708年</a>，29-31岁</div><div id='265e2b3ac69c43d6b05009b2b400845c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　秋，九龄赴西京应吏部重试及第，主持者李峤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年</a>　中材堪经邦科，授秘书省校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年</a>　在秘书省任校书郎。是年秋，修文馆学士宋之问、李适等同作诗送许州宋思马赴任，九龄为之作序。作品：《饯宋（一作“送”）司马序》<div id='poem_1365926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饯宋司马序</a><span class='authorDate'>（708年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365926")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365926'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365926'>宋司马才通命塞。云翼泥蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365926_comment'></div>蔡邕朔方。不废琴书之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365926_comment'></div>贾谊宣室。欲言鬼神之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365926_comment'></div>既而出宿南浦。与鸿雁而同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365926_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365926", 1365926, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>追饯</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365926", 1365926, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>北梁</span>。对江山而不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365926_comment'></div>是日渚云欲霁。林鸟将春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365926_comment'></div>惜时物之方华。重情人之自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365926_comment'></div>群公有感。中座无欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365926_comment'></div>他日清风。自当元度之夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365926_comment'></div>兹辰零雨。得无子荆之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365926_comment'></div>遂相与援翰。赋诗赠行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365926_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365926_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a8dcd5205c9f44ae9ecf7fe98fc98ab2_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年1月</a>　在秘书省任校书郎。正月，因宫中赐彩盛事，九龄有诗。作品：《剪彩》<div id='poem_22797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_allusion_22797'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1245, "poem_allusion_22797")'>姹女</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22797'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22797'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1245, "poem_sentence_0_22797")'>姹女</span>矜容色，为花不让春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22797'>既争芳意早，谁待物华真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22797'>叶作参差发，枝从点缀新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22797'>自然无限态，长在艳阳晨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作人）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22797'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年</a>　在秘书省任校书郎。六月前，干谒李让侍御史，一者求其提拂；再者欲随其赴岭南理铨选事，乘便归宁。不料被拒，遂上书，剖白己之心迹。作品：《与李让侍御书》<div id='poem_1365920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李让侍御书</a><span class='authorDate'>（710年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365920")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365920'>李公足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365920_comment'></div>夫心以义持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365920_comment'></div>公为时出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365920_comment'></div>虽冥冥入穷神之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365920_comment'></div>鬼莫我窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365920_comment'></div>而恟恟自众人之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365920_comment'></div>通者谁惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365920_comment'></div>何则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365920_comment'></div>我有独见之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365920_comment'></div>物无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365920", 1365920, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>浮言</span>之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365920_comment'></div>亦犹太阿之剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365920_comment'></div>犀角不足齿其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365920_comment'></div>高山之松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365920_comment'></div>霜霰不能渝其操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365920_comment'></div>斯岂非爱恶则物之相背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365920_comment'></div>而终始则我之不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365920_comment'></div>且如明公义贯心灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365920_comment'></div>人推正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365920_comment'></div>遂乃雄飞清宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365920_comment'></div>高步等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365920_comment'></div>向若见不决于明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365920_comment'></div>济不兼于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365920_comment'></div>终然独善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365920_comment'></div>何自致之若是乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365920_comment'></div>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365920_comment'></div>则明公独运之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365920_comment'></div>以获当仁之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365920_comment'></div>固人情之可恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365920_comment'></div>何横议之能干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365920_comment'></div>昨所造次下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365920_comment'></div>求为从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365920_comment'></div>亦望心与道合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365920_comment'></div>申一言而取容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365920_comment'></div>人以义图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365920_comment'></div>轻干驷如脱屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365920_comment'></div>则不意制以形骸之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365920_comment'></div>拘于牙齿之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365920_comment'></div>盖下慎闭门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365920_comment'></div>而公奚措意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365920_comment'></div>夫国家所以历试官序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365920_comment'></div>推择士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365920_comment'></div>虽因时买利之夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365920_comment'></div>犹能变节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365920_comment'></div>而服义亡躯之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365920_comment'></div>奚遽生疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365920_comment'></div>此亦人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365920_comment'></div>亦何害岁寒之取效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365920_comment'></div>然明公所以不容左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365920_comment'></div>诚非克堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365920_comment'></div>固当别有嘤鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365920_comment'></div>如为蛇足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365920_comment'></div>而以为家属在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365920_comment'></div>用防未然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365920_comment'></div>既明公之虑极精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365920_comment'></div>亦下官之心怀感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365920_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365920_comment'></div>至如中朝著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365920_comment'></div>连姻华族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365920_comment'></div>及夫委以钧轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365920_comment'></div>综其条流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365920_comment'></div>而朝廷岂可南求儋耳之酋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365920_comment'></div>北取旄头之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365920_comment'></div>必伫异方之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365920_comment'></div>乃无内顾之私者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365920_comment'></div>故知事有是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365920_comment'></div>公无远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365920_comment'></div>昔如祁奚之举子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365920_comment'></div>不避其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365920_comment'></div>齐人之为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365920_comment'></div>固在于楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365920_comment'></div>是以为善在已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365920_comment'></div>执一心之既定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365920_comment'></div>诡道从时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365920_comment'></div>乃千人之所指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365920_comment'></div>然下官所以勤勤自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365920_comment'></div>其功靡他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365920_comment'></div>正以居本海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365920_comment'></div>始无朝望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365920_comment'></div>昔遇光华启旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365920_comment'></div>朝制旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365920_comment'></div>误登射策之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365920_comment'></div>忝职藏书之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365920_comment'></div>又属朝廷尚义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365920_comment'></div>端士相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365920_comment'></div>复以无依见容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365920_comment'></div>不时弃置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365920_comment'></div>所以迟回城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365920_comment'></div>感激身名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365920_comment'></div>未甘田里之平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365920_comment'></div>所慕君亲之大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365920_comment'></div>而才能不急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365920_comment'></div>时用无施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365920_comment'></div>俸犹拟于侏儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365920_comment'></div>举未优于储偫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365920_comment'></div>所以饥寒在虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365920_comment'></div>扶侍增遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365920_comment'></div>而慈亲在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365920_comment'></div>如日将暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365920_comment'></div>遂乃甘心<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1365920", 1365920, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>附丽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365920_comment'></div>乘便归宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365920_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365920_comment'></div>则命非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1365920", 1365920, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>饮冰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365920_comment'></div>幸安中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365920_comment'></div>又安能崎岖执事之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365920_comment'></div>还无一级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365920_comment'></div>去且二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365920_comment'></div>愿明公审图彼人向者何为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365920_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365920_comment'></div>忠信获戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365920_comment'></div>古人之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365920_comment'></div>惟教义之所矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365920_comment'></div>乃讥嫌之见及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365920_comment'></div>恨不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1365920", 1365920, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>隳肝尝胆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365920_comment'></div>徇知己以求申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365920_comment'></div>而饮气吞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365920_comment'></div>负当年而叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365920_comment'></div>庭闱眷恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365920_comment'></div>行路屏营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365920_comment'></div>斯薄宦之所婴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365920_comment'></div>念劳生之有役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365920_comment'></div>望美高传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365920_comment'></div>何嗟及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365920_comment'></div>炯炯式微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365920_comment'></div>心为谁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365920_comment'></div>转当侧听妙选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365920_comment'></div>用息鄙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365920_comment'></div>心之有怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365920_comment'></div>言不能尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365920_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_128_1365920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22854", 22854, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>下流</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22746'>更愁征戍客，容鬓老边尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22746'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22746_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_22889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>青荧</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22889'>此中楚王梦，梦得神女灵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22889'>神女去已久，云雨空冥冥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22889'>唯有巴猿啸，哀音不可听。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22889'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22889_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_5341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_5341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/5341?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_5341'>思君如满月，夜夜减清辉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_5341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_5341'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_5341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_5341'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(5341)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=711&endYear=711')">711年</a>　在秘书省任校书郎任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年</a>　是年经嗣鲁王李道坚所举，对策三道高第，迁左拾遗。作品：《对嗣鲁王道坚所举道侔伊吕科》<div id='poem_1365915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应道侔伊吕科对策第一道<span class='inlineComment2'>（并问）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（712年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365915")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365915'>问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365915_comment'></div>兴化致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365915_comment'></div>必俟得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365915_comment'></div>求贤审官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365915_comment'></div>莫先慎举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365915_comment'></div>圣朝受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365915_comment'></div>于今百龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365915_comment'></div>尧封比屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365915_comment'></div>魏网斯顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365915_comment'></div>史曹之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365915_comment'></div>衡镜攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365915_comment'></div>岁时调集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365915_comment'></div>士踰累万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365915_comment'></div>借使崔毛重起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365915_comment'></div>裴乐复存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365915_comment'></div>观貌察言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365915_comment'></div>且犹未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365915_comment'></div>考行徵实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365915_comment'></div>其可得乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365915_comment'></div>若远循汉魏之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365915_comment'></div>复存州郡之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365915_comment'></div>即务辞会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365915_comment'></div>权归外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365915_comment'></div>牧守之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365915_comment'></div>何法能鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365915_comment'></div>变通之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365915_comment'></div>厥路奚由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365915_comment'></div>文武之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365915_comment'></div>并用无偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365915_comment'></div>军旅之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365915_comment'></div>事宜经远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365915_comment'></div>而越骑佽飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365915_comment'></div>皆出畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365915_comment'></div>丁年负甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365915_comment'></div>耆日释戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365915_comment'></div>亡殁盖多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365915_comment'></div>军容每阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365915_comment'></div>今欲均井田于要服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365915_comment'></div>遵兵赋于革车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365915_comment'></div>恐习俗滋深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365915_comment'></div>虑始难就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365915_comment'></div>揆今酌古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365915_comment'></div>其衷若何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365915_comment'></div>且惠在安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365915_comment'></div>政惟重谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365915_comment'></div>顷承平既久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365915_comment'></div>居泰易盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365915_comment'></div>编户流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365915_comment'></div>农桑莫赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365915_comment'></div>精求良吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365915_comment'></div>未之能补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365915_comment'></div>遂其宽施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365915_comment'></div>则莫惩游食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365915_comment'></div>峻其科禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365915_comment'></div>则虑扰疲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365915_comment'></div>革弊适时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365915_comment'></div>应有良术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365915_comment'></div>子等并明于国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365915_comment'></div>允应于旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365915_comment'></div>式陈开物之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365915_comment'></div>无效循常之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365915_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_1365915'>对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365915_comment'></div>嗣鲁王道坚所举道侔伊吕科徵仕郎行秘书省校书郎张九龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365915_comment'></div>伏览睿问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365915_comment'></div>大哉国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365915_comment'></div>九品流弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365915_comment'></div>尝所懵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365915_comment'></div>幸因对扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365915_comment'></div>庶言其可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365915_comment'></div>古者诸侯贡士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365915_comment'></div>司徒论士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365915_comment'></div>必讲礼观能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365915_comment'></div>乡举里选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365915_comment'></div>故十五十八之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365915_comment'></div>大学小学之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365915_comment'></div>诵习以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365915_comment'></div>教化以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365915_comment'></div>则孝悌之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365915_comment'></div>可知于乡曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365915_comment'></div>政事之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365915_comment'></div>可升于国朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365915_comment'></div>先王务教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365915_comment'></div>此其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365915_comment'></div>及周道既衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365915_comment'></div>斯文将丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365915_comment'></div>秦氏灭学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365915_comment'></div>唯力是亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365915_comment'></div>仁义大坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365915_comment'></div>俊造亦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365915_comment'></div>汉高以马上非礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365915_comment'></div>复修三代之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365915_comment'></div>魏武以军中是务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365915_comment'></div>权立九品之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365915_comment'></div>后代因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365915_comment'></div>莫能改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365915_comment'></div>纷纷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_95_1365915", 1365915, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>横调</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365915_comment'></div>滔滔皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365915_comment'></div>天下公器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365915_comment'></div>可谓伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365915_comment'></div>伏惟陛下神启睿图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365915_comment'></div>天佑明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365915_comment'></div>物不终否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365915_comment'></div>故受之以泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365915_comment'></div>弊不遂极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365915_comment'></div>乃鼎之以新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365915_comment'></div>涤瑕荡秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365915_comment'></div>今其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365915_comment'></div>伏愿图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365915_comment'></div>夫正其本者万事理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365915_comment'></div>劳于求者逸于使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365915_comment'></div>岂有大明御宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365915_comment'></div>虑此假权之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365915_comment'></div>循良择人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365915_comment'></div>安得谢恩之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365915_comment'></div>是则外台会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365915_comment'></div>真若满于贮中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365915_comment'></div>济理适时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365915_comment'></div>复何殊于掌上者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365915_comment'></div>且有备无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365915_comment'></div>亡战必危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365915_comment'></div>是以振旅茇舍之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365915_comment'></div>羽林佽飞之卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365915_comment'></div>汉家徵选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365915_comment'></div>咸出五陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365915_comment'></div>周制供王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365915_comment'></div>不踰千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365915_comment'></div>此以均其远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365915_comment'></div>会其中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365915_comment'></div>王者之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365915_comment'></div>岂虚乎哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365915_comment'></div>必开井赋于要服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365915_comment'></div>俾裒益于畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365915_comment'></div>虽经始之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365915_comment'></div>何施不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365915_comment'></div>而图远之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365915_comment'></div>犹愿勿遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365915_comment'></div>且将振九品之颓纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365915_comment'></div>维百王之绝略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365915_comment'></div>使官有位次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365915_comment'></div>资有等衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365915_comment'></div>才苟不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365915_comment'></div>时所勿取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365915_comment'></div>使夫能者代上帝之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365915_comment'></div>议者息高门之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365915_comment'></div>吏精其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365915_comment'></div>人享其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365915_comment'></div>流庸不日而来复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365915_comment'></div>耕桑何忧乎不稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365915_comment'></div>动之斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365915_comment'></div>绥之斯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365915_comment'></div>若惟作法于末途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365915_comment'></div>非救弊之本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365915_comment'></div>盛德大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365915_comment'></div>孰与归乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365915_comment'></div>某怖慄尘埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365915_comment'></div>栖栖非得言之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365915_comment'></div>慷慨禾莠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365915_comment'></div>惓惓因献策之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365915_comment'></div>何敢望焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365915_comment'></div>尽心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365915_comment'></div>谨对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_160_1365915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年9月</a>　九月，谏玄宗幸温汤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年4月</a>　在左拾遗任。四月，获见苏州司功参军武平一寄赠的诗，感而酬答。作品：《武司功初有幽庭春暄见贻夏首获见以诗报焉》<div id='poem_22835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武司功初有幽庭春暄见贻夏首获见以诗报焉</a><span class='authorDate'>（713年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22835")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22835_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22835'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1629, "poem_allusion_22835")'>二鲤鱼</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2730, "poem_allusion_22835")'>求莺</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22835'>芳月尽离居，幽怀重起予。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22835'>虽言春事晚，尚想物华初。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22835'>迟日皦方照，高斋澹复虚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22835'>笋成林向密，花落树应疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22835'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_22835", 22835, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>赠鲤</span>情无间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2730, "poem_sentence_4_22835")'>求莺</span>思有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22835'>暄妍不相待，含叹欲焉如。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年</a>　在左拾遗任。是年秋，与吏部尚书崔日用有诗唱和。作品：《奉和吏部崔尚书雨后大明朝堂望南山》<div id='poem_22834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和吏部崔尚书雨后大明朝堂望南山</a><span class='authorDate'>（713年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22834")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22834_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22834'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3383, "poem_allusion_22834")'>山公启事</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7568, "poem_allusion_22834")'>商君阡陌</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22834'>迢递终南顶，朝朝阊阖前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22834'>朅来青绮外，高在翠微先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22834'>双凤褰为阙，群龙俨若仙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22834'>还知到玄圃，更是谒甘泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22834'>夜雨尘初灭，秋空月正悬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22834'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_22834", 22834, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>诡容</span>纷入望，霁色宛成妍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22834'>东极华阴践，西弥嶓冢连。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22834'>奔峰出岭外，瀑水落云边。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22834'>汉帝宫将苑，商君陌与阡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22834'>林华铺近甸，烟霭绕晴川。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22834'>既庶仁斯及，分忧政已宣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22834'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3383, "poem_sentence_11_22834")'>山公启事</span>罢，吉甫颂声传。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22834'>济济<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_22834", 22834, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>金门步</span>，洋洋玉树篇。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22834'>徒歌虽有属，清越岂同年。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_22834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年12月</a>　在左拾遗任。本月，上书姚崇，劝其远诌躁，进纯厚，任人当才，无溺缘情。作品：《上姚令公书》<div id='poem_1365918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上姚令公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（713年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365918")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365918'>月日。左拾遗张九龄谨奏记紫微令梁公阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365918_comment'></div>公登庙堂运天下者久矣。人之情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365918_comment'></div>事之得失。所更多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365918_comment'></div>非曲学之说。小子之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365918_comment'></div>所能损益。亦已明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365918_comment'></div>然而意有不尽未可息。区区之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365918_comment'></div>或以见容。亦犹用九九之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365918_comment'></div>以此道也。忍弃之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365918_comment'></div>今君侯秉天下之钧。为圣朝之佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365918_comment'></div>大见信用。渴日太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365918_comment'></div>千载一时。胡可遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365918_comment'></div>而君侯既遇非常之主。已践难得之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365918_comment'></div>加以明若镜中。运如掌上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365918_comment'></div>有形必察。无往不臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365918_comment'></div>朝暮羲轩之时。何云伊吕而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365918_comment'></div>际会易失。功业垂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365918_comment'></div>而举朝之众倾心。前人之弊未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365918_comment'></div>往往拟议。愚用惜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365918_comment'></div>何者。任人当才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365918_comment'></div>为政大体。与之共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365918_comment'></div>无出此途。而曩之用才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365918_comment'></div>非无知人之鉴。其所以失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365918_comment'></div>溺在缘情之举。夫见势则附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365918_comment'></div>俗人之所能也。与不妄受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365918_comment'></div>志士之所难也。君侯察其苟附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365918_comment'></div>及不轻受。就而厚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365918_comment'></div>因而用之。则禽息之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365918_comment'></div>为知巳而必碎。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1365918", 1365918, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>豫让</span>之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365918_comment'></div>感国士而能漆。至于合如市道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365918_comment'></div>廉公之门客<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1365918", 1365918, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>虚盈</span>。势比雀罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365918_comment'></div>廷尉之交情贵贱。初则许之以死殉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365918_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1365918", 1365918, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>体面</span>俱柔。终乃背之而饱飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365918_comment'></div>身名巳遂。小人恒态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365918_comment'></div>不可不察。自君侯职相国之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365918_comment'></div>持用人之权。而浅中弱植之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365918_comment'></div>巳延颈企踵而至。谄亲戚以求誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365918_comment'></div>媚宾客以取容。情结笑言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365918_comment'></div>谈生羽翼。万事至广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365918_comment'></div>千变难知。其閒岂不有才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365918_comment'></div>所失在于无耻。君侯或弃其所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365918_comment'></div>收其所长。人且不知深旨之若斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365918_comment'></div>便谓尽私于此辈。其有议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365918_comment'></div>则曰不识宰相。无以得迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365918_comment'></div>不因交游。无以求进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365918_comment'></div>明主在上。君侯为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365918_comment'></div>安得此言。犹出其口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365918_comment'></div>某所以为君侯至惜也。且人可诚感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365918_comment'></div>难可户说。为君侯之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365918_comment'></div>谢媒介之徒。即虽有所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365918_comment'></div>一皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1365918", 1365918, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>沮抑</span>。专谋选众之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365918_comment'></div>息彼讪上之失。祸生有胎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365918_comment'></div>亦不可忽。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365918_comment'></div>古人有言。御寒莫若重裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365918_comment'></div>止谤莫如自修。修之至极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365918_comment'></div>何谤不息。勿曰无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365918_comment'></div>其祸将大。夫长才广度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365918_comment'></div>珠潜璧匿。无先容以求达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365918_comment'></div>虽后时而自宁。今岂无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365918_comment'></div>何近何远。但问于其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365918_comment'></div>人焉廋哉。虽不识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365918_comment'></div>有何不可。是知女不私人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365918_comment'></div>可以为妇矣。士不苟进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365918_comment'></div>可以为臣矣。此君侯之度内耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365918_comment'></div>安用小人之说为。固知山藏海纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365918_comment'></div>言之无咎。下情上通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365918_comment'></div>气用和洽。是以不敢默默而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365918_comment'></div>愿无以人故而废其言。以伤君侯之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365918_comment'></div>此至愿也。幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365918_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1365918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=714')">713-714年</a>　在左拾遗任。是年有诗。作品：《送苏主簿赴偃师》《别乡人南还》《和崔尚书喜雨》<div id='poem_22789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年闰2月</a>　在左拾遗任。此月与众王公卿同赋《龙池篇》作品：《奉和圣制龙池篇》<div id='poem_22756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年</a>　在左拾遗任。是年春夏间，又有送密县高赞府等诗文。作品：《景龙观山亭送密县高赞府序》<div id='poem_1365924' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365924' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365924?labeling=true' target='_blank'>景龙观山亭集送密县高赞府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（714年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365924")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365924_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365924'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365924'>景龙。东山初主第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365924_comment'></div>始其置金榜。筑凤台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365924_comment'></div>穷土木之功。极冈峦之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365924_comment'></div>议与磐石同体。造化较力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365924_comment'></div>何其壮哉。自吾君茅茨不剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365924_comment'></div>采椽不斲。既抑华而务实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365924_comment'></div>将设教以垂范。以故平阳化焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365924_comment'></div>罢歌舞于其地。麻姑见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365924_comment'></div>变桑田于此时。所谓长女之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365924_comment'></div>郁为列仙之馆。其后尝有好事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365924_comment'></div>以为胜游。令日芳辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365924_comment'></div>携手接袂。往往而在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365924_comment'></div>祗取乐焉。高十官雌伏都畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365924_comment'></div>星言至止。闻殊庭之可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365924_comment'></div>召嘉客以相欢。徒观其匠幽奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365924_comment'></div>宅爽垲。十里九版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365924_comment'></div>岂惟梁氏之作。千岩万壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365924_comment'></div>宛是吴中之事。青林修耸而垂䌽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365924_comment'></div>绿萝蒙笼以结阴。清流若镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365924_comment'></div>下照金沙之底。杂花如锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365924_comment'></div>傍缘石菌之崖。则可以藻饰形神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365924_comment'></div>挥斥氛滓。相顾风尘之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365924_comment'></div>无负云霄之槩。既而东主西宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365924_comment'></div>酒酣乐阕。聚必有散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365924_comment'></div>匪伊麋鹿之群。往而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365924_comment'></div>固亦山林之弊。高公乃振衣而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365924_comment'></div>举杯有属。却计送人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365924_comment'></div>出长安之东道。退思征马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365924_comment'></div>向洛阳之南阡。虽暂劳于州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365924_comment'></div>迫于簿领。方欲厌于承明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365924_comment'></div>资其骞跃。夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365924_comment'></div>相知意气。何恨仳离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365924_comment'></div>盍赋诗焉。以赠行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365924_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1365924_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年9月</a>　在左拾遗任。九月，与黄门侍郎卢怀慎有诗唱和，以竹之“高节人相重，虚心世所知”而喻人自勉。作品：《和黄门卢侍郎咏竹》<div id='poem_22754' class='_poem'><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365858_comment'></div>纵两县检括。有所阿容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365858_comment'></div>即愿宣付宪司。纠摘其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365858_comment'></div>今便收捕入内。别加推逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365858_comment'></div>道路有云。何急于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365858_comment'></div>若在外勘当。虑以相宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365858_comment'></div>其馀法狱。岂皆应就内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365858_comment'></div>始可以杜其请托。方益威严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365858_comment'></div>便是法不肃而吏不惧。其弊尤重于别宅者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365858_comment'></div>昔汉丞相府尚不按吏。诚以务在尊崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365858_comment'></div>体不可失。况天子中禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365858_comment'></div>而有此名。丞尉极微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365858_comment'></div>所缘至小。固不足以尘黩圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365858_comment'></div>虽在内曹。外议切切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365858_comment'></div>未为得所。即有闻知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365858_comment'></div>不敢不奏。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365858_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365858_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=715&endYear=715')">715年5月20日</a>　是日，有书，奏请朝廷重刺史、县令之选及行辟举之法，玄宗嘉纳之。作品：《上封事书》<div id='poem_1365852' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365852' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365852?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上封事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（715年5月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365852")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365852_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365852'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365852'>五月二十日。宣义郎左拾遗内供奉臣张九龄谨再拜死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365852_comment'></div>上书开元神武皇帝陛下。臣所以上事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365852_comment'></div>以臣愚见。并当时尤切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365852_comment'></div>不敢饰词。伏愿陛下亲览可否之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365852_comment'></div>幸甚幸甚。臣伏以陛下自克清内难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365852_comment'></div>光宅天下。常欲跻人于富寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365852_comment'></div>致国于太平。圣虑每勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365852_comment'></div>德音屡发。然犹黎人未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365852_comment'></div>水旱为忧。臣窃伏思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365852_comment'></div>有由然矣。臣闻乖政之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365852_comment'></div>发为水旱。天道虽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365852_comment'></div>其应甚速。昔者东海枉杀孝妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365852_comment'></div>旱者久之。一吏不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365852_comment'></div>匹妇非命。则天为之旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365852_comment'></div>以昭其冤。况今六合之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365852_comment'></div>元元之众。莫不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>悬命</span>于县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365852_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>宅生</span>于刺史。陛下所与共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365852_comment'></div>此尤亲于人者也。多非其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365852_comment'></div>徒有其名。致旱之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365852_comment'></div>岂惟孝妇一事而已。是以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>亲人</span>之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365852_comment'></div>宜得其贤。用才之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365852_comment'></div>宜重其选。而今刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365852_comment'></div>除京辅近处<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>雄望</span>之州。刺史犹择其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365852_comment'></div>县令或备员而已。其馀江淮陇蜀三河诸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365852_comment'></div>除大府之外。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>稍稍</span>非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365852_comment'></div>但于京官之中。出为州县者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365852_comment'></div>或是缘身有累。在职无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365852_comment'></div>用于牧宰之閒。以为斥逐之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365852_comment'></div>或因势<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>附会</span>。遂忝高班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365852_comment'></div>比其势衰。且无他责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365852_comment'></div>又谓之不称京职。亦乃出为刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365852_comment'></div>至于武夫流外。积资而得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365852_comment'></div>官成于经久。不计于有才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365852_comment'></div>诸若此流。尽为刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365852_comment'></div>其馀县令已下。固不可胜言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365852_comment'></div>盖氓庶所系。国家之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>本务</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365852_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>本务</span>之职。反为好进者所轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365852_comment'></div>承弊之人。每遭非才者所扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365852_comment'></div>陛下圣化。从此不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365852_comment'></div>皆由不重<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>亲人</span>之选。以成其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365852_comment'></div>而欲天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>和洽</span>。固不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365852_comment'></div>古者刺史入为三公。郎官出宰百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365852_comment'></div>莫不于其所重。劝其所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365852_comment'></div>臣窃怪近俗。偏轻此任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365852_comment'></div>今朝廷卿士。入而不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365852_comment'></div>于其私情。遂自得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365852_comment'></div>何则。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>京华</span>之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365852_comment'></div>衣冠所聚。子弟之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365852_comment'></div>身名所出。从容<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>附会</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365852_comment'></div>不劳而成。一出外藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365852_comment'></div>有异于此。人情进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365852_comment'></div>岂忘于私。但立法制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365852_comment'></div>不敢违耳。原其本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365852_comment'></div>固私是欲。今大利在于京职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365852_comment'></div>而不在于外郡。如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365852_comment'></div>则智能之士。欲利之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365852_comment'></div>日夜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>营营</span>。宁有复出为刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365852_comment'></div>而陛下国家之利。方赖智能之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365852_comment'></div>此辈既自固而不行。在外者又技痒而求入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365852_comment'></div>如此。则智能之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365852_comment'></div>常无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>亲人</span>之责。陛下又未格之以法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365852_comment'></div>无乃甚不可乎。故臣愚以为欲理之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365852_comment'></div>莫若重刺史县令。此官诚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365852_comment'></div>智能者可行。正宜悬以科条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365852_comment'></div>定其资历。凡不历都督刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365852_comment'></div>虽有高第者。不得入为侍郎列卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365852_comment'></div>不历县令有善政者。亦不得入为台郎给舍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365852_comment'></div>虽远处都督刺史。至于县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365852_comment'></div>以次差降。以为出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365852_comment'></div>亦不得十年频任京职。又不得十年尽任外官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365852_comment'></div>如此设科。以救其失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365852_comment'></div>则内外通理。万姓获宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365852_comment'></div>如积习为常。遂其私计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365852_comment'></div>陛下独宵衣旰食。天下亦未之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365852_comment'></div>又古之选用贤良。取其称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365852_comment'></div>或遥闻而辟召。或一见而任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365852_comment'></div>是以士修<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>素行</span>。不图侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365852_comment'></div>群小不逮。亦用息心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365852_comment'></div>以故奸伪自止。流品不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365852_comment'></div>今天下未必理于上古。而事务日倍于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365852_comment'></div>诚为不正其本。而设巧于末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365852_comment'></div>所谓末者。吏部条章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365852_comment'></div>动盈千百。刀笔之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365852_comment'></div>辨析毫釐。节制抢攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365852_comment'></div>溺于文墨。胥徒之猾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365852_comment'></div>又缘隙而起。臣以为始造簿书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365852_comment'></div>以备用人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_86_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/172/Comments/0")'>遗亡</span>耳。今反求精于案牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365852_comment'></div>不急于人才。亦何异遗剑中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365852_comment'></div>而刻舟以纪。去之弥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365852_comment'></div>可为伤心。凡有称吏部之能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365852_comment'></div>则曰从县尉与主簿。从主簿与县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365852_comment'></div>斯选曹执文而善知官次者也。惟据其合与不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365852_comment'></div>不论贤与不肖。大略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365852_comment'></div>岂不谬哉。陛下若不以吏部尚书侍郎为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365852_comment'></div>必不授以职事。尚书侍郎既以贤而受委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365852_comment'></div>岂复不能知人。知人之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365852_comment'></div>虽自古所慎。而拔十得五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365852_comment'></div>其道可行。今则执以格条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365852_comment'></div>贵于谨守。幸其心能自觉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365852_comment'></div>每选于所拔亦有三人五人。若又专固者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365852_comment'></div>则亦一人不拔。据资配职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365852_comment'></div>自以为能。为官择人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365852_comment'></div>初无此意。故使时人有平配之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365852_comment'></div>官曹无得贤之实。朱紫同色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365852_comment'></div>清浊不分。是于圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365852_comment'></div>有何裨益。故臣以为选部之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365852_comment'></div>弊于不变。变法之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365852_comment'></div>在陛下焕然行之。假如今之铨衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365852_comment'></div>欲自为意。亦限行之已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365852_comment'></div>动必见疑。遂用因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365852_comment'></div>益为浮薄。今若刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365852_comment'></div>精覈其人。即每年当管之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365852_comment'></div>应有合选之色。先委考其才行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365852_comment'></div>堪入品流。然后送台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365852_comment'></div>台又推择。据所用之多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365852_comment'></div>为州县之殿最。一则州县慎于所举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365852_comment'></div>必取入官之才。二则吏部因其有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365852_comment'></div>无多庸人之数。纵有不在送者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365852_comment'></div>妄起怨端。且犹分谤于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365852_comment'></div>不至喧哗于南省。今则每岁选者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365852_comment'></div>动以万计。京师米物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365852_comment'></div>为之空虚。岂多士若斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365852_comment'></div>盖渝滥至此。而欲仍旧致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365852_comment'></div>难于改制。祗益文法烦碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365852_comment'></div>贤愚浑杂。就中以一诗一判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365852_comment'></div>定其是非。适使贤人君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365852_comment'></div>从此遗逸。斯亦明代之缺政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365852_comment'></div>有识者之所叹息也。夫天下虽广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365852_comment'></div>朝廷虽众。而士之名贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365852_comment'></div>诚可知也。若使毁誉相乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365852_comment'></div>听受不明。事将已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365852_comment'></div>无复可说。如知其贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365852_comment'></div>各有品第。每一官缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365852_comment'></div>而不以次用之。则是知而不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365852_comment'></div>焉用彼相。借如诸司清要之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365852_comment'></div>当用第一之人。及其要官阙时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365852_comment'></div>或以下等叨进。以故时议无高无下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365852_comment'></div>惟论得与不得。自然清议不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365852_comment'></div>名节不修。上善则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1365852", 1365852, "Clauses/277/Comments/0")'>守志</span>而后时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365852_comment'></div>中人则躁求而易操。其故何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365852_comment'></div>朝廷若以令名而进人。士子亦以修名而获利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365852_comment'></div>而利之所出。众则趋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365852_comment'></div>已而名利不出于清修。所趣多归于人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365852_comment'></div>其小者苟求辄得。一变而至阿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365852_comment'></div>其大者许以分义。再变而成朋党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365852_comment'></div>斯并教化渐渍。使之必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365852_comment'></div>故于用人之际。不可不第高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365852_comment'></div>若高下有次。不可妄干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365852_comment'></div>天下士流。必刻意修饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365852_comment'></div>思齐日众。刑政日清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365852_comment'></div>此皆兴衰之大端。焉可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365852_comment'></div>易曰。履霜坚冰至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365852_comment'></div>言圣人之见。终始之徵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365852_comment'></div>臣今所言上刺史县令等事。一皆指实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365852_comment'></div>纵臣所欲变法。不合时宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365852_comment'></div>伏望更发睿图。及询于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365852_comment'></div>作为长算。振此颓风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365852_comment'></div>使官修其方。人受其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365852_comment'></div>天下幸甚。伏惟陛下聪明神武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365852_comment'></div>动以圣断。正当可为之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365852_comment'></div>未行反本之法。微臣企竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365852_comment'></div>窃有所望。伏愿少留宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365852_comment'></div>稍览愚诚。必无可施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365852_comment'></div>弃之非晚。不胜尘露裨补之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365852_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_164_1365852_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=715&endYear=715')">715年</a>　春夏间，在紫微省与紫微侍郎苏颋等雅集赏花，得赋芍药诗。作品：《苏侍郎紫薇庭各赋一物得芍药》<div id='poem_22747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22747' id='poem_sentence_3_22916'>花间直城路，草际曲江流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22916'><span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=718&endYear=718')">718年</a>　登朝后，曾献状。作品：《论教皇太子状》<div id='poem_1365857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论教皇太子状</a><span class='authorDate'>（718年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365857")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365857'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365857_comment'></div>臣伏以皇太子是天下之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365857_comment'></div>为国之贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365857_comment'></div>今则睿质渐长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365857_comment'></div>犹在深宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365857_comment'></div>所与近习者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365857_comment'></div>未必皆正人端士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365857_comment'></div>安于逸乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365857_comment'></div>久则性成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365857_comment'></div>是以古者明王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365857_comment'></div>恐其若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365857_comment'></div>虽在赤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365857_comment'></div>先之以教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365857_comment'></div>必使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1365857", 1365857, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>耆儒硕德</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365857_comment'></div>为之师保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365857_comment'></div>故大戴礼云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365857_comment'></div>周成王在襁褓之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365857_comment'></div>太公为之太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365857_comment'></div>教之顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365857_comment'></div>周公为之太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365857_comment'></div>傅其德义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365857_comment'></div>召公为之太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365857_comment'></div>保其身体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365857_comment'></div>是故成王能圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365857_comment'></div>周道用康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365857_comment'></div>秦始皇使赵高傅其太子胡亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365857_comment'></div>因教之以狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365857_comment'></div>所习者非斩劓人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365857_comment'></div>则夷人之三族也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365857_comment'></div>胡亥即位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365857_comment'></div>秦氏以亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365857_comment'></div>则明人之性情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365857_comment'></div>莫不由习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365857_comment'></div>若近正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365857_comment'></div>闻正事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365857_comment'></div>虽欲为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365857_comment'></div>固已不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365857_comment'></div>若亲近细人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365857_comment'></div>不闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1365857", 1365857, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>教谕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365857_comment'></div>纵欲行善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365857_comment'></div>犹未知所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365857_comment'></div>此必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365857_comment'></div>胡越之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365857_comment'></div>生则声同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365857_comment'></div>长则语异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365857_comment'></div>盖声者天然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365857_comment'></div>语者所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365857_comment'></div>习于胡则胡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365857_comment'></div>习于越则越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365857_comment'></div>故知成于所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365857_comment'></div>不可不慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365857_comment'></div>臣伏愿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1365857", 1365857, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>详择</span>典故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365857_comment'></div>徵用名贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365857_comment'></div>执经劝学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365857_comment'></div>朝夕从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365857_comment'></div>俾皇太子得于所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365857_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365857_comment'></div>谨奉状以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365857_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1365857_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=718&endYear=718')">718年10月</a>　十月，应王昊、王旻兄弟之请，为其父故太仆卿王希隽撰写墓志。作品：《故太仆卿上柱国华容县男王府君墓志》<div id='poem_1365950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故太仆卿上柱国华容县男王府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（718年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365950")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365950_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365950'>公讳某。琅琊临沂人。盖王氏所由远矣。然其自汉至今。上下千载。海沂为颂。始壮厥猷。淮水作桢。克昌其后。继迹台衮。联华牧伯。君子韪其立言。史官褒其行事。则巳系无违德。人以嘉闻。图牒粲然。宜为冠族。乃祖某。梁侍中尚书左右仆射安东亭侯。高祖某。陈度支尚书。曾祖某。太子中书舍人。祖某。皇朝吏部郎中。赠润州刺史。父某。官至洪州都督。公践修范业。雅有名器。性开敏而达于从事。才果断而长于御下。至于学以知古。义以随时。虚巳存诚。离经合道。异焉而不伤于物。同焉而不害于政。咸自得之。务其大者。仪凤中。初以门子选为孝敬皇帝挽郎。解巾相王府参军。授豫王府参军。历太子通事舍人蒲州司法参军。丁洪州府君忧去职。丧踰于戚。行过于礼。时其在疚。哀能感邻。服阕。授相州邺县令。施于政也。挥干镆之锋。截无不断。展骐骥之足。行无不至。以故言出有孚。岂止于百里。教行无类。俄浃于四封。邑人是宜。舆颂乃作。御史中丞张仁愿表公尤异。帝用嘉焉。迁洛州陆浑县令。加朝散大夫。宠其能也。再有仲由之善。益闻考父之恭。薄理我畿。有加于邺。识者观政。许其以后图。时辈推多。验之于晚节。稍迁蒲州司马洛州长史蒲州长史。三为郡佐。一以贯之。执心有恒。厥声以茂。虽巴祗之体素。顾和之理识。异代同官。齐名比义。固无愧也。俄迁随州刺史。赵始大。列于诸侯。张敞有名。擢为刺史。贤明独断。政教宏宣。始于汉东之美。继以巴中之异。郡历数四。课尝第一。再领遂绵二州刺史。先是俗多梗弊。人尽流庸。公亦来思。抚之如子。彼得攸塈。归之如市。行有馀力。用不尽才。骤迁大都督。乃拜相州刺史。先是景云岁。我唐虽旧。仪制维新。置连率之官。增监郡之秩。于是历选列辟。专谋用贤。且有后命。而公为称首。遂作越州都督。同京官正三品连率。统察杭婺衢睦温抚台闽八州长吏巳下。率由部按。事虽竟寝。议者终荣。仍守越州都督。加银青光禄大夫。公素有盛名。兼之宠数。闻望而草风必偃。至止而蓬麻自直。与夫任贤坐啸。劳心行部。彼有因而至此。我无为而巳然。政之行焉。有若神者。徵拜雍州司马。顷之。又正名为京兆少尹。京兆者。本公之乐土。居巳重世。买臣还郡。无矜于出绶。张既本州。是荣于衣绣。公虽作贰。我亦为光。开元二年。始封华容县男。昭有德也。其明年。有制以公检校太仆卿。训以六驺。正于君仆。日加数马之慎。岁有展軨之勤。无何即真。可谓贵矣。然公思报所受。逾励所行。神明未衰。志业不究。春秋六十有一。开元六年秋八月乙亥。寝疾薨于洛阳之陶化里第。呜呼哀哉。朝廷伤焉。赙赠以礼。夫人范阳卢氏。不享偕老。先时在殡。其年冬十月乙酉。合葬于偃师之某原。却倚首阳。前瞻洛汭。岂伊瑕邱之乐。盖取邢山之兆。有子曰昊。次子曰旻。泣血苫●(FB57)。哀缠于远日。勒铭金石。仪叶于吉时。假以斯文。为之实录。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365950'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365950'>有周之裔，居海之沂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365950'>绪业为永，德音罔违。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365950'>贻厥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365950", 1365950, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>谋翼</span>，俾其翰飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365950'>宜哉世祀，亦曰家肥<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365950'>今也则亡，天不可问<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365950_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365950'>神欺永年，礼先远日。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365950'>合如防墓，开彼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1365950", 1365950, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>滕室</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1365950'>鹤吊人悲，龟言地吉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365950_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1365950'>篆石泉户，与山相毕<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365950_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1365950'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=718&endYear=718')">718年12月</a>　十二月，应韦瀚之请，为其父故韶州司马韦府君撰墓志铭。作品：《故韶州司马韦府君墓志铭并序》<div id='poem_1365953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故韶州司马韦府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（718年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365953")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365953_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365953'>君讳某。字某。京兆杜陵人。其先佐夏翼商。赐命为伯。傅楚相汉。继世能贤。休有成烈。庆流于裔。洎曾祖津。仕隋至内史侍郎户部尚书。武德初拜黄门侍郎寿光男。克济美名。以食旧德。大父琨。太子詹事武阳侯。能成休轨。载扬厥问。烈考展。官止少府监主簿。懿业无忝。而大位不充。天爵自高。人伦斯贵。公荷百代之丕搆。传一经之素范。白足以长人。文敏足以敷政。迹不由径。必期乎直。学不为辨。每抑其华。志尚则然。风流自远。斯有万里之望。岂伊百夫之特。始自崇文生明经上第。起家汾州参军。公以为国无小而行无择。苟履忠信。何陋蛮貊。遂求补远郡。从所好焉。于是授泉州司仓参军。历广州都督府法曹参军。轮囷下蟠。弗以屑意。干蛊用誉。将以明道。固已仁焉而不异于远。义焉而不辞于难。潜亦孔昭。允谓君子。秩满。迁韶州司马。在郡数载。检身一德。辅化致理。刑清讼息。宜其奋庸上国。寘乎公卿。而矢志南州。终于参佐。悲夫。享年五十有一。某年月。卒于官舍。粤开元六年冬十二月庚午。葬于少陵原。有子曰某。欲报罔极。思传不朽。勒石泉户。式昭德音。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365953'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365953'>皇矣鼻祖，时维大彭。<div class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1349, "poem_sentence_0_22778")'>相如</span>只谢病，子敬忽云亡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22778'>岂悟瑶台雪，分彫玉树行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22778'>清规留草议，故事在封章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22778'>本谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22778", 22778, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>山公启</span>，而今殁始扬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22778_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_22779' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22779' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22779?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22779'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22779'>返葬长安陌，秋风箫鼓悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22779'>奈何相送者，不是平生时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22779'>寒影催年急，哀歌助晚迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22779'>宁知建旟罢，丹旐向京师。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22779_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22779'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22779_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=719&endYear=719')">719年</a>　本年底，应苏诜太夫人崔氏所请，为“卒哭”而作文。作品：《画天尊像铭并序》<div id='poem_1365936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画天尊像铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（719年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365936")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365936_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365936'>画天尊像者。赠吏部侍郎武功苏公夫人崔氏为公卒哭之所作也。苏公有重名于时。未大用而卒。遭命不遂。当代所悲。况作嫔于公。鞠凶在疚。援诗以誓其节。执礼而哭于昼。哀而能感。感而能通。极希微而不见。中恍惚其如在。于是欲介景福。将祈太清。因心寓象。命工设色。饰金阙。图玉皇。元天不远。真官在列。飘若灵气。烂其神光。彼昭厥诚。允速其应。斯所谓元鉴无昧。当受谒帝之符。幽魂有凭。必署升仙之箓。此固崔氏之至愿也。有足悲者。不其猗欤。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365936'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365936'>至哉天京，灾劫不及。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365936'>上有灵府，圣真所集。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365936'>彼美孟姜，闻斯洞彰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365936'>仙道贵度，我君则亡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365936'>猗欤我君，蔚为人杰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365936'>命屈金铉，神传玉诀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365936'>游魂大素，介福上清。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365936'>式图元象，永观厥成。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365936'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年1月</a>　为礼部员外郎。正月，有文。作品：《奉和圣制瑞雪篇》<div id='poem_22899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22899")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_2_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22899'>信宿婵娟飞雪度，能使玉人俱掩嫭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22899'>皓皓楼前月初白，纷纷陌上尘皆素。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22899'>昨讶骄阳积数旬，始知和气待迎新。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22899'>匪惟在人利，曾是扶<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作占）</span>天意。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22899'>天意岂云遥，雪下不崇朝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22899'>皇情玩无斁，雪委方盈尺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22899'>草树纷早荣，京坻宛先积。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22899'>君恩诚谓何，岁稔复人和。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_22899", 22899, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>籉笠</span>兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_22899", 22899, "Clauses/26/Comments/1")'>农节</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22899'>倚瑶琴兮或歌，续薰风兮瑞雪。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年4月</a>　为礼部员外郎。夏四月，与起居舍人蔡孚、万年主簿韩朝宗出游长安南郊杜曲，欢聚于故韦司马别业，受到主人韦澣的热情款待，因序其事。作品：《贺给事尝诣蔡起居郊馆有诗因命同作》《韦司马别业集序》<div id='poem_22845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺给事尝诣蔡起居郊馆有诗因命同作</a><span class='authorDate'>（720年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365928?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韦司马别业集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（720年4月）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365928'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365928'>杜城南曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365928_comment'></div>斯近郊之美者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365928_comment'></div>背原面川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365928_comment'></div>前峙太一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365928_comment'></div>清渠修竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365928_comment'></div>左并宜春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365928_comment'></div>山霭下连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365928_comment'></div>溪气中绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365928_comment'></div>此皆韦公之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365928_comment'></div>余固己闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365928_comment'></div>开元岁夏四月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365928_comment'></div>猥忝散职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365928_comment'></div>居多放情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365928_comment'></div>跂彼一行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365928_comment'></div>无忘于夙尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365928_comment'></div>时其七召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365928_comment'></div>果获于前期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365928_comment'></div>乃与起居舍人蔡公万年主簿韩公惠而得朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365928_comment'></div>欣然命驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365928_comment'></div>韦公方拭席见待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365928_comment'></div>羞以药物之滋。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1365928_comment'></div>清言移景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365928_comment'></div>閒步周林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365928_comment'></div>翻飞自情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365928_comment'></div>俯仰为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365928_comment'></div>斯亦吾侪之乐事。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365928_comment'></div>岂一邱而一壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365928_comment'></div>二三君子。<div class='inline'
