/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年</a>　春夏间，又有和贺给事郊游诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年</a>　本年前后，秋与给事中许景先唱和，有诗。作品：《和许给事直夜简诸公》<div id='poem_22819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_8_22819'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_22819_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年11月</a>　为赵令言、赵令则之父故许州长史赵庆逸撰墓志铭并序。作品：《故许州长史赵公墓志铭并序》<div id='poem_1365952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故许州长史赵公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（720年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365952")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365952_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365952'>公讳某。天水陇城人。其先受赐于周。所食者赵。下逮襄子。大为诸侯。贻子谋孙。克用保国。有功有伐。无代无之。曾祖某。隋尚书左右仆射淮宁郡公。祖某。金紫光禄大夫殿中监。赠工部尚书武强公。父某。符宝郎。皆发闻馨香。系祚蕃衍。不高位者。则人望焉。公惇师旧业。允迪渊懿。包君子大雅之量。有古人获心之赏。修词以达其道。则质文相半。履行以顾其言。则刚柔并克。弱冠以门子调补湖州参军。转相州司兵参军。学以入官。思不出位。格言清论。始诵今行。属太上皇养德在藩。择贤为吏。公首其举。王曰尔谐。于是引为相王府户曹参军。转法曹参军。及龙德既亨。鹤鸣有应。往而利见。縻以好爵。乃授朝散大夫雍州录事参军。纲领诸曹。罔有不率。秩满。除洛州伊阙县令。事举其中。敛从其薄。惠小镇大。徇公灭私。政之在人。今而遗爱。俄迁徐州司马。未几。转陕州司马许州长史。千里将骋。六辔斯柔。得之自心。动而中节。故其四参州事。再入府寮。一宰畿邑。三为郡佐。莫不所居而绩宣其用。所去而颂因其迹。岂伊苟然。厥繇尚矣。开元八年春二月。疾作革。乙丑。终于官舍。春秋若干。某年冬十有一月庚午。归葬。夫人崔氏祔焉。公自然淡泊。不屑势利。守道贞固。与命推迁。故历年多所。移官数四。不过参佐而巳。岂亦直道之云乎。然而卑以自牧。约而能济。推厚居薄。内居其仁。急病让夷。外多其义。不曰君子。其能尔乎。有子曰令言。次曰令则。泣血加人。抑情就礼。哀愬窀穸之事。恭惟先君之德。验之所履。附之斯文。以传无穷。以慰罔极。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365952'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365952'>猗嗟令德，宽仁合道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365952'>景行行止，风流肆好。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365952'>名取公器，善为身宝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365952'>志所以立，政所以宣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365952'>入官惟允，莅事其然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365952'>是仪是式，不忘不愆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365952'>今也终古，后之克祚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365952'>子孙禋祀，春秋霜露。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365952_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=721&endYear=721')">721年5月</a>　在司勋员外郎任。五月，拟处分举人敕。作品：《敕处分举人》<div id='poem_1365733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕处分举人</a><span class='authorDate'>（721年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365733")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365733'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365733'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365733_comment'></div>求贤济理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365733_comment'></div>询事考言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365733_comment'></div>务取由衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365733_comment'></div>以观深识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365733_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365733", 1365733, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>顷年</span>策试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365733_comment'></div>颇成弊风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365733_comment'></div>所问既不切于时宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365733_comment'></div>所对亦何关于政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365733_comment'></div>徒徵隐僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365733_comment'></div>莫见才明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365733_comment'></div>以此择贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365733_comment'></div>良未得所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365733_comment'></div>卿等各膺推荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365733_comment'></div>副朕虚求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365733_comment'></div>宜其悉心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365733_comment'></div>各尽所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365733_comment'></div>勿复仍旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365733_comment'></div>空载游词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365733_comment'></div>各宜就食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365733_comment'></div>食讫就试。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1365733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=721&endYear=721')">721年10月14日</a>　在司勋员外郎任。此日，加朝散大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=721&endYear=721')">721年11月</a>　在司勋员外郎任。此日，为故河南少尹窦敬宾撰碑铭。作品：《故河南少府窦府君墓碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1365947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故河南少尹窦府君墓碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（721年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365947")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365947_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365947'>序曰。正其身。君子所以慎德。敏于行。吉人所以寡辞。或道之。或处之。是亦正命。命之将行。利有攸往。则行不家至而人劝。言不面命而事济。不为迹而实以阜蕃。不沽名而声以遹骏。夫如是者。存乎其人。故河南少尹窦公。盖有之矣。公讳某。扶风平陵人。自后魏大将军侍中永富公至烈考瀛州刺史赠刑部尚书莘国公六叶矣。皆增华卿族。见重公朝。四国于藩。四方于宣。龙旂承祀。六辔耳耳。公所谓盛德必祀。承子之始大。积善馀庆。是哀伯之有后。故生则灵知。长而纯固。既白而受采。亦黄以通中。天假不器之性。人服自然之理。而况于文雅缘饰。志业孔修。引伸足以长人。动用足以利物。既学从政。其归易。形有方殊。道以一贯。人致一意而巳。我乃万目尽张。故其始也。以明经上第。授彭州参军事。询谋郡将。器异甚厚。所遇森然。其言固矣。如山之为。始于覆篑。如江之导。终以方舟。于是累迁至于辥王友赞善大夫。燕王筑馆以待士。汉储立苑以招宾。当其推择。莫匪贤俊。议者惟允。而公在焉。然由韫椟隋和。十城空其价。蜷跼骥騄。千里未之骋。及其用也。再入尚书郎。遂为洛阳令。三台雅望。一时精选。旧章资以弥纶。利器呈于盘错。出宰百里。实推三河。其赋政则必反于其身。亦既诚信被之于物。是为惠怀。故虽二州馀弊。憸巧而难理。五郡尤剧。权倾而多奸。莫不可使由之。令自求之。善处中于下鞲。能合契于游刃。至于釐举风俗之谬。裁正人伦之经。务劝衣食之原。调均徭赋之事。本为巳任。无间人言。故视事踰四年。通而不倦。遗德在百姓。久而益彰。非夫明允宣和。优柔博约。自我之不忒。为人之攸暨。亦曷由臻兹。厥有洛阳所谓贤令者。则周纡王涣孔翊祝良。公实续之。谁其似之。属天子建中都。营新邑。资尔亚尹。伊其董司。朝选其人。公首斯举。以故稍迁河中少尹。且有后命。废府而复迁河南焉。以公之归。从人之望。官则改次。政无易方。以佐理王都。以表则天下。而年不克祚。位不光宠。遇暴疾而卒。悲夫。是岁有唐开元之九年。春秋五十有六。公以孝友为体。一变而迪忠信。以明恕为用。再变而致循良。故所行无择。所事无巧。有恒其德。终且温温。不伐其功。昭然赫赫。所以遗爱固结。必在何武之去。称诵斯深。惟恐子产之死。巳而神道欺而不福。物情丧其所赖。人之不幸。今也云亡。及丧之西归。则人吏致哀。道路相属。得人心如此。其旨可知。冬十一月。葬于北原。后之人或者将游于斯。叹于斯。彼其与归。我乃不朽矣。其子八人。长曰某。次曰某。家有太邱之德。里以高阳之名。夙构闵凶。能哀伤以殆灭。匪革其道。惧功伐之不传。俾予为文。以叙孝子之志。铭曰。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=722&endYear=722')">722年</a>　为司勋员外郎。时张说秉政，对九龄尤亲重之，许为后出词人之冠，并予推奖超拔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=722&endYear=722')">722年2月17日</a>　此日，转中书舍人内供奉。为吏部侍郎姜晦撰祭故人文一篇。作品：《为吏部侍郎祭故人文》<div id='poem_1365956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为吏部侍郎祭故人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（722年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365956")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365956'>维开元十年岁次壬戌二月癸酉朔十七日巳丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365956_comment'></div>吏部侍郎某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365956_comment'></div>谨以清酌脯醢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365956_comment'></div>敬祭故某公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365956_comment'></div>闻夫仁必寿考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365956_comment'></div>所谓神道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365956_comment'></div>善亦庆延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365956_comment'></div>以为信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365956_comment'></div>今夫子之不福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365956_comment'></div>而圣谟之是愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365956_comment'></div>孝友纯固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365956_comment'></div>礼让周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365956_comment'></div>行所以直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365956_comment'></div>业所以专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365956_comment'></div>诚公才而天假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365956_comment'></div>故官政以日宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365956_comment'></div>节使是式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365956_comment'></div>朝宿既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365956_comment'></div>十部称贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365956_comment'></div>一人思媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365956_comment'></div>凤凰于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365956_comment'></div>云霄以冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365956_comment'></div>胡然明灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365956_comment'></div>歼我良懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365956_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365956_comment'></div>夫子之逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365956_comment'></div>平生之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365956_comment'></div>襟抱素合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365956_comment'></div>游处常偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365956_comment'></div>清风对禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365956_comment'></div>文石同侪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365956_comment'></div>自兹两掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365956_comment'></div>殆将一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365956_comment'></div>展转清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365956_comment'></div>仳离君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365956_comment'></div>曷其爱而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365956_comment'></div>甫云觏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365956_comment'></div>正司空之扫第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365956_comment'></div>属荆州之罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365956_comment'></div>歘交臂而相失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365956_comment'></div>殷痛心其何巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365956_comment'></div>今卜兆有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365956_comment'></div>祖载在庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365956_comment'></div>飒然象设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365956_comment'></div>寞尔音形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365956_comment'></div>驱白马而何见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365956_comment'></div>瞻素车之巳扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365956_comment'></div>德音不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365956_comment'></div>应甘棠之勿剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365956_comment'></div>交情乃见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365956_comment'></div>伊黍稷之非馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365956_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365956_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1365956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=722&endYear=722')">722年闰5月</a>　本月，与朝臣源乾曜、张嘉贞、宋璟、许景先、袁晖、贺知章、韩休、王翰、崔日用、崔泰之、苏晋、卢从愿、徐知仁、崔禹锡、王光庭、席豫、徐坚、胡皓、王丘等二十人一道，作有奉和圣制送兵部尚书张说赴朔方巡边诗。作品：《奉和圣制送尚书燕国公赴朔方》<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狮子赞序</a><span class='authorDate'>（722年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365930")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365930'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365930'>夫德之所感者深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365930_comment'></div>物之所怀者远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365930_comment'></div>中国有圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365930_comment'></div>占候而自来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365930_comment'></div>四夷不王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365930_comment'></div>征伐而难致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365930_comment'></div>故绝域有来贡没羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365930_comment'></div>诸侯有不入苞茅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365930_comment'></div>举其大凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365930_comment'></div>不在遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365930_comment'></div>顷有至自南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365930_comment'></div>厥繇西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365930_comment'></div>献其方物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365930_comment'></div>而狮子在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365930_comment'></div>尔雅所谓狻麑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365930_comment'></div>如虦猫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365930_comment'></div>食虎豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365930_comment'></div>今之所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365930_comment'></div>信然绝猛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365930_comment'></div>其天骨雄诡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365930_comment'></div>材力杰异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365930_comment'></div>得金精之刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365930_comment'></div>为毛群之特。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365930_comment'></div>仡立不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365930_comment'></div>而九牛相去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365930_comment'></div>眈视且瞋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365930_comment'></div>则百兽皆伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365930_comment'></div>所以肉视犀象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365930_comment'></div>孩抚熊罴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365930_comment'></div>其馀琐细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365930_comment'></div>不置牙齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365930_comment'></div>我天子示柔远之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365930_comment'></div>国无不庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365930_comment'></div>有伏猛之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365930_comment'></div>物无难制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365930_comment'></div>故其受羁绁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365930_comment'></div>伏闲皂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365930_comment'></div>驯而为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365930_comment'></div>锋莫可当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365930_comment'></div>然吾君所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365930_comment'></div>义不谓此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365930_comment'></div>盖蛮夷君长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365930_comment'></div>岁时贡献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365930_comment'></div>或殊琛绝赆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365930_comment'></div>实于内府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365930_comment'></div>或异兽奇禽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365930_comment'></div>扰于外囿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365930_comment'></div>皆其觐礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365930_comment'></div>若中国之贽币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365930_comment'></div>所不辞让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365930_comment'></div>明异方之臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365930_comment'></div>此则非有利物之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365930_comment'></div>充耳目之玩好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365930_comment'></div>以为怀柔之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365930_comment'></div>示天地之含容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365930_comment'></div>不其然欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365930_comment'></div>固无德而称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365930_comment'></div>义异獒犬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365930_comment'></div>岂劳召公之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365930_comment'></div>美同赤豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365930_comment'></div>何关韩侯之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365930_comment'></div>凡我侍臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365930_comment'></div>为之赞云。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年4月29日</a>　为中书舍人。此日，为兵部尚书王晙撰谢平章事表。作品：《为兵部尚书王晙谢平章事表》<div id='poem_1365847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为兵部尚书王晙谢平章事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（723年4月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365847")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365847'>臣晙言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365847_comment'></div>伏奉今月二十九日制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365847_comment'></div>授臣兵部尚书同中书门下三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365847_comment'></div>殊常宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365847_comment'></div>妄集疲朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365847_comment'></div>承恩窃喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365847_comment'></div>任重惟忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365847_comment'></div>臣诚欢诚恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365847_comment'></div>臣伏以虚受之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365847_comment'></div>鲁史诫以量力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365847_comment'></div>满盈之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365847_comment'></div>夏载陈其招损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365847_comment'></div>臣阶缘试吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365847_comment'></div>际会登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365847_comment'></div>遂得入拜尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365847_comment'></div>比天之喉舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365847_comment'></div>出典方镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365847_comment'></div>为王之爪牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365847_comment'></div>虽忠烈之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365847_comment'></div>心知所竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365847_comment'></div>而绩用之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365847_comment'></div>岁久无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365847_comment'></div>今陛下不以为愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365847_comment'></div>寘之庙堂之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365847_comment'></div>委以军国之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365847_comment'></div>实恐鼎足不任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365847_comment'></div>鹈翼为刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365847_comment'></div>退失微臣之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365847_comment'></div>上累陛下之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365847_comment'></div>是以永夕九飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365847_comment'></div>终朝三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365847_comment'></div>泉谷为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365847_comment'></div>冰炭在怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365847_comment'></div>道虽愿于将行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365847_comment'></div>位固惭于幸得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365847_comment'></div>臣已有别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365847_comment'></div>具所让人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365847_comment'></div>犹蒙曲私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365847_comment'></div>未寝严命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365847_comment'></div>方欲俯偻恭命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365847_comment'></div>对扬休光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365847_comment'></div>磨铅效于一割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365847_comment'></div>策蹇同于十驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365847_comment'></div>臣诚惧尘台席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365847_comment'></div>谬齿国华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365847_comment'></div>将何以允答鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365847_comment'></div>弼谐大化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365847_comment'></div>拜命祗惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365847_comment'></div>罔知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365847_comment'></div>臣不胜荷惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365847_comment'></div>谨奉表谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365847_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365847_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1365847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　九月前，有谢赐马状一文。作品：《谢赐马状》<div id='poem_1365912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365912'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365912_comment'></div>今日高力士奉宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年9月</a>　九月，为故驸马都尉观国公杨睿交撰墓志铭并序。作品：《故特进赠兖州都督驸马都尉观国公杨公墓志铭并序》<div id='poem_1365949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故特进赠兖州都督驸马都尉观国公杨公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（723年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365949")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365949_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365949'>公讳慎交。字某。宏农华阴人也。其先食采于杨。因邑为氏。始大于两汉。更盛于周隋。司空观德王士雄。公之高祖也。台阶论道。盟府书勋。利建维城。泽流后嗣。洎右卫将军赠兵部尚书府君讳嘉本。累叶炳灵。六辔承祀。而皆千里一举。逸翰所推。五侯同拜。贵戚莫比。公即尚书之子也。诞保中和。克绍前烈。幼以美秀。兼大叔之文。长而嘉闻。增季友之业。孝弟忠信。蕴乎生知。礼乐诗书。成于时习。弱冠以门子调补晋州参军。中宗之在春宫也。妙才地。将降天孙。兼之实难。而公惟允。以选尚长宁郡主。加朝散大夫。拜通事舍人。累迁右卫郎将。神龙元祀。中兴在运。预闻大策。克树休勋。而贵主宜家。既增汤沐。列侯传国。复锡山川。至是始袭观国公。拜驸马都尉左千牛卫将军。加上柱国。累迁秘书监兼太子宾客。增秩金紫光禄大夫。又特进散骑常侍右千牛将军陕王傅。坐事左出巴州刺史。入为光禄卿。复出为亳襄陈邓四州刺史。左转鄜亳许绛四州别驾。公性明敏。有器韵。不求虚誉。而百行允修。不矜小善。而九能咸事。至于入官从政。东文西武。才既两可。事亦百中。且不恃贵以伤义。不怙宠而废公。奉以周旋。加之撝挹。虽在降出。无他悔吝。此亦公之善自为谋。以道终始者也。开元十二年四月癸卯。遘疾薨于绛郡之官舍。春秋五十。天子悼焉。有制赠使持节都督兖州诸军事兖州刺史。仍遣使吊问。令返葬京师。率礼有加。哀荣异数。其年秋九月甲申。葬于北原。其孤曰某等。煢煢在疚。愿图遗烈。后之人亦知范宣之世禄。岂独臧孙之立言。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365949'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365949'>岩岩太华，作镇西土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365949'>祚我诸杨，降生厥祖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365949'>四代而立，为汉元辅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365949_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365949'>爰及礽裔，克复先古。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365837_comment'></div>顷年已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365837_comment'></div>每思至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365837_comment'></div>或远人不率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365837_comment'></div>克开厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365837_comment'></div>乾坤交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365837_comment'></div>保合太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365837_comment'></div>麟凤龟龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365837_comment'></div>元符黄瑞之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365837_comment'></div>钦谒上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365837_comment'></div>告受命之元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365837_comment'></div>昭严配之成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365837_comment'></div>大典云备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365837_comment'></div>至诚克展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365837_comment'></div>诸侯骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365837_comment'></div>来于穆之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365837_comment'></div>百神受职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365837_comment'></div>率咸秩之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365837_comment'></div>六变已陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365837_comment'></div>三献斯毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365837_comment'></div>盖春秋之大事莫先乎祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365837_comment'></div>王者之盛礼莫重于郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365837_comment'></div>柴燎克终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365837_comment'></div>感庆罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365837_comment'></div>岂予一人之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365837_comment'></div>亦尔万邦之赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365837_comment'></div>宜因咸和之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365837_comment'></div>俾承厚下之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365837_comment'></div>可大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365837_comment'></div>自开元十一年十一月十六日昧爽已前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365837_comment'></div>罪无轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365837_comment'></div>巳发觉未发觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365837_comment'></div>已结正禾结正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365837_comment'></div>系囚见徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365837_comment'></div>大辟罪已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365837_comment'></div>咸赦除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365837_comment'></div>其十恶死罪造伪头首劫贼杀财主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365837_comment'></div>在不赦例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365837_comment'></div>就中仍虑有冤滥者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365837_comment'></div>所司具状送中书门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365837_comment'></div>尽理详覆奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365837_comment'></div>朕将亲览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365837_comment'></div>其有亡命山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365837_comment'></div>挟藏军器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365837_comment'></div>百日不首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365837_comment'></div>复罪如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365837_comment'></div>敢以赦前事相告言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365837_comment'></div>以其罪罪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365837_comment'></div>升坛行事官及供奉官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365837_comment'></div>三品巳上赐爵一级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365837_comment'></div>四品以下加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365837_comment'></div>诸县官并准此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365837_comment'></div>升坛例内外文武官及致仕并前资陪位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365837_comment'></div>赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365837_comment'></div>缘大礼有职掌并押当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365837_comment'></div>更加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365837_comment'></div>斋郎并放出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365837_comment'></div>皇亲诸亲陪位未出身者并放选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365837_comment'></div>已出身者赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365837_comment'></div>亲王公主各与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365837_comment'></div>三品卫监门黄衣长上飞骑万骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365837_comment'></div>并仗内杂色人在斋宫宿卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365837_comment'></div>及诸色人有资劳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365837_comment'></div>缘大礼有职掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365837_comment'></div>并流外行署预见大礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365837_comment'></div>亦赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365837_comment'></div>其充香炉执扇及礼生祝史赞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365837_comment'></div>赐勋外日选优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365837_comment'></div>兵士宿卫斋宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365837_comment'></div>并诸色无资劳缘大礼职掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365837_comment'></div>及京兆府百姓缘南郊祗应者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365837_comment'></div>各免其家一年杂科差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365837_comment'></div>南北卫将军率中郎将宿卫斋宫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365837_comment'></div>并同升坛例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365837_comment'></div>其诸军节度大使及三都留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365837_comment'></div>虽不陪位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365837_comment'></div>委寄既重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365837_comment'></div>特宜同升坛官例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365837_comment'></div>百岁老人赐棉帛五段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365837_comment'></div>粟五石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365837_comment'></div>县令至其家存问给付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365837_comment'></div>孝子顺孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365837_comment'></div>义夫节妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365837_comment'></div>旌表门闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365837_comment'></div>终身勿事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365837_comment'></div>已旌表者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365837_comment'></div>量加优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365837_comment'></div>诸州百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365837_comment'></div>或因逢水旱流寓未安者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365837_comment'></div>宜令所司与朝集使即作赈恤安辑法奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365837_comment'></div>其单贫卫士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365837_comment'></div>番镇久次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365837_comment'></div>令州府长官择灼然者放免番役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365837_comment'></div>征行人家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365837_comment'></div>州县检校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365837_comment'></div>勿使侵欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365837_comment'></div>碛西镇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365837_comment'></div>途路悬邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365837_comment'></div>特宜赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365837_comment'></div>𩻴寡茕独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365837_comment'></div>亦令州县倍加矜恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365837_comment'></div>使得存济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365837_comment'></div>元置义仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365837_comment'></div>救人不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365837_comment'></div>承前贷百姓粮及种子未纳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365837_comment'></div>并放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365837_comment'></div>不得却徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365837_comment'></div>自古圣帝明王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365837_comment'></div>忠臣烈士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365837_comment'></div>名山大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365837_comment'></div>并令所管致祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365837_comment'></div>其已得替官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365837_comment'></div>并轻累未得处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365837_comment'></div>非老弱疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365837_comment'></div>犹堪处事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365837_comment'></div>量加收叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365837_comment'></div>使免失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365837_comment'></div>其左贬官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365837_comment'></div>非逆人五服内亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365837_comment'></div>及犯赃贿名教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365837_comment'></div>所司责勘奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365837_comment'></div>量移近处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365837_comment'></div>其官人有清白政术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365837_comment'></div>堪任刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365837_comment'></div>及抱器怀才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365837_comment'></div>不求闻达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365837_comment'></div>州长官其以名荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365837_comment'></div>宗室中有孝悌才术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365837_comment'></div>为众所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365837_comment'></div>仍在卑任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365837_comment'></div>委宗正具以名奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365837_comment'></div>君臣一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365837_comment'></div>休戚共焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365837_comment'></div>朕钦承天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365837_comment'></div>恭传大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365837_comment'></div>盖凭累祖馀业得一之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365837_comment'></div>亦由群公旧勋不二之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1365837_comment'></div>永言繄赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1365837_comment'></div>其敢忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1365837_comment'></div>自武德已来实封功臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1365837_comment'></div>知政宰辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1365837_comment'></div>有身无大故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1365837_comment'></div>而亡官失爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1365837_comment'></div>子孙沦屈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1365837_comment'></div>所由勘实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1365837_comment'></div>具以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1365837_comment'></div>存者可畴其官荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1365837_comment'></div>逝者当录其允嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1365837_comment'></div>使幽明同庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1365837_comment'></div>知有今辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1365837_comment'></div>亚献邠王守礼终献宁王宪各赐物一千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1365837_comment'></div>捧俎申王撝夹侍岐王范薛王业各赐物七百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1365837_comment'></div>侍中源乾曜中书令张说兵部尚书同中书门下三品王晙各赐物五百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1365837_comment'></div>正衣驸马都尉王守一王繇温曦宗正少卿崔澄各赐物三百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1365837_comment'></div>二王后赐物一百五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1365837_comment'></div>坛场使京兆尹孟温礼赐物二百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1365837_comment'></div>修造羽仪使赐物一百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1365837_comment'></div>修撰仪注官五品已上赐物一百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1365837_comment'></div>六品已下赐物七十段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1365837_comment'></div>自馀陪位预宴官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1365837_comment'></div>一品赐物一百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1365837_comment'></div>二品三品八十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1365837_comment'></div>四品五品六十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1365837_comment'></div>六品七品四十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1365837_comment'></div>八品九品三十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1365837_comment'></div>鸿胪诸蕃使与见大礼及在本蕃王侯大酋长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1365837_comment'></div>并同宴会例给赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1365837_comment'></div>郡主县主各赐物八十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1365837_comment'></div>缘大礼数处有职掌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1365837_comment'></div>任于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_200_1365837", 1365837, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>一头</span>从高叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1365837_comment'></div>天下州府赐酺三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1365837_comment'></div>京城五日。<div id='poem_sentence_204_1365837_comment'></div>其有处分未该者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1365837_comment'></div>令所司及本使比类奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1365837_comment'></div>赦书日行五百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1365837_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1365837_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>　为中书舍人。春，梓州刺史韦抱贞兄弟诗酒宴集于京郊曲江南亭，九龄等与宴并有和诗。作品：《和韦尚书答梓州兄南亭宴集》<div id='poem_22751' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22751' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>　为中书舍人。春末夏初，族叔张敬忠调任益州长史前置酒宴，九龄与宴并赋诗践行。作品：《益州长史叔置酒宴别序》<div id='poem_1365923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州长史叔置酒宴别序</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365923")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365923'>天子建五长。守四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365923_comment'></div>内以承卫京师。外以攘却戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365923_comment'></div>则有持其节制。未十年而历践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365923_comment'></div>抚其封疆。既一行而宁辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365923_comment'></div>尽在我叔父。备闻于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365923_comment'></div>昔者吉甫是钦。仲著孝友之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365923_comment'></div>楚子所畏。趯在诸侯之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365923_comment'></div>世有实绩。今以美济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365923_comment'></div>俾我张氏。郁彼士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365923_comment'></div>以媚于一人。以正于四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365923_comment'></div>岂非德能光大。谋必变通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365923_comment'></div>思古人之获心。施君子之不器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365923_comment'></div>所以前拜小司马。兼拥旄于五命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365923_comment'></div>今为左常侍。仍总戎于三蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365923_comment'></div>轨模素远。绰有先路之风声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365923_comment'></div>车服载驰。光被上军之礼命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365923_comment'></div>莫不文茵畅毂。淑旂绥章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365923_comment'></div>啴啴皇皇。途将出于华阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365923_comment'></div>威己叠乎夜郎。是时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365923_comment'></div>四序鳞次。属当春夏之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365923_comment'></div>千里草长。有怀原隰之往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365923_comment'></div>乃辟轩宇。邀宾寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365923_comment'></div>自髦士而及同姓。由金华而下建礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365923_comment'></div>或交以道合。岂徒肆好之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365923_comment'></div>或情以族亲。所谓宗盟之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365923_comment'></div>龟组交映。肴蓛骈罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365923_comment'></div>而声欲成文。发中堂之弦管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365923_comment'></div>志在击节。感四座之衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365923_comment'></div>必名义而为言。虽聚散而何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365923_comment'></div>酒酣相顾。骊歌乃作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365923_comment'></div>白日西下。求壮士之翻车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365923_comment'></div>青山南登。爱忠臣之叱驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365923_comment'></div>凡我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1365923", 1365923, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>明懿</span>。赋诗饯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365923_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1365923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年7月</a>　为中书舍人。皇后被废，奉拟文。作品：《废王皇后制》<div id='poem_1365720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>废王皇后制</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1365720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365720'>门下。朕承五圣之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365720_comment'></div>为万国之君。敢以私爱而废至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365720_comment'></div>内顾而忘鸿业。皇后王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365720_comment'></div>天命不佑。华而不实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365720_comment'></div>居上畜虎狼之心。御下甚鹰鹯之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365720_comment'></div>造起狱讼。朋扇朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365720_comment'></div>见无将之端。有可讳之恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365720_comment'></div>焉得敬承宗庙。母仪天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365720_comment'></div>可废为庶人。就别院安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365720_comment'></div>刑于家室。有愧昔王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365720_comment'></div>为国大计。盖非获已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365720_comment'></div>布告天下。咸使知闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365720_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365720_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fc91017626dd494db0cb2b8681189f44_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=726')">725-726年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='fc91017626dd494db0cb2b8681189f44' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年</a>　在中书舍人任。本年前后，九龄应少府监、许州刺史李察之托请，为其祖父李仁瞻、父李玄祐撰碑铭并序。作品：《故果州长史李公碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1365943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故果州长史李公碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365943")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365943_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365943'>公讳仁瞻。字某。赵郡房子人。其先自段干木至柏仁侯。皆以醇德茂功。奋于上世。始于藩魏。终而将赵。其名不殒。遂济于今。五代祖后魏中书侍郎始丰懿侯璨。璨生徐州刺史始丰顺侯元茂。元茂生赵郡太守府君讳子云。子云生驸马都尉直阁将军府君讳道宗。道宗生齐尚书兵部郎中府君讳山寿。公即郎中府君之子。仍世济美。在邦攸宜。故我公禀灵中和。履道元吉。以学则探其奥旨。见圣人之心。以行则践其嘉言。合君子之度。以故动为人誉。名乃日宣。义府孔修。德舆云远。固未可量也。隋大业中举孝廉。洎唐兴。调棣州司户参军。凡迁磁相二州总管府户曹参军宜州录事参军。莫不事人以直。反身于诚。处卑能安。敬长则顺。故光辅郡将。周爰咨度。自州徂州。或啸或诺。既而迁金乡晋陵二县令。精诚以庀事。善教以长人。四封用孚。三英以粲。彼蒲与密。独何有焉。以课最迁归州治中郢州司马。加朝散大夫。行果州长史。盘桓参佐。未复公侯。道非吾行。德无必贵。遂以没代。岂命也夫。某年月。卒于官舍。享年若干。及丧至自蜀。而葬不归赵。乃卜宅于许。封树汝坟。子孙遂家。亦既重代。至开元中。公之孙曰察。以古诸侯之禄。奉先大夫之祀。昼游本郡。辉光前烈。非清白以遗。善庆之馀。保艾尔后人。亦何以臻此。于是履霜为感。恭惟春秋之事。刻石是图。俾扬祖宗之业。斯善继者也。叙而志之。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365943'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365943'>长史英英，作为世程。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365943'>动合雅度，绰有令名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365943'>以之入官，从事而升。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365943'>以之佐郡，为政孔明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365943'>悠悠上天，曷不贵德。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365943'>终于参佐，孰云邦国。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365943'>孝孙其昌，馀庆乃彰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365943'>宰树苍苍，徽音不忘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365943'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年4月12日</a>　在中书舍人任。此日，奉拟停张说中书令制。作品：《停燕国中书令制》<div id='poem_1365721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>停张说中书令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（726年4月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365721")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365721'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365721'>特进行尚书右丞相兼中书令燕国公张说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365721_comment'></div>往属艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365721_comment'></div>输诚于履险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365721_comment'></div>及兹辅相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365721_comment'></div>润色于告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365721_comment'></div>而不察细微之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365721_comment'></div>颇乖周慎之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365721_comment'></div>朕略小存大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365721_comment'></div>念旧录功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365721_comment'></div>且法不欲屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365721_comment'></div>宜罢中枢之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365721_comment'></div>义亦有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365721_comment'></div>更崇端揆之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365721_comment'></div>宜停中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365721_comment'></div>可尚书右丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365721_comment'></div>仍将国史于宅修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365721_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365721_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年4月12日</a>　在中书舍人任。曾为何给事进亡父所著书《帝国秘录》上表。作品：《为何给事进亡父所著书表》<div id='poem_1365849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为何给事进亡父所著书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（726年4月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365849")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365849'>臣言。臣父某官某名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365849_comment'></div>往历枢近。志勤忠益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365849_comment'></div>至于霸王大略。军国要务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365849_comment'></div>事关兴替。言涉箴规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365849_comment'></div>因著十篇。名曰帝图秘箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365849_comment'></div>将欲献纳。才加撰次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365849_comment'></div>寻属臣私门殃衅。夙遘闵凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365849_comment'></div>手泽所存。心瞿不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365849_comment'></div>遂未奏御。犹在缄縢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365849_comment'></div>二纪及兹。遗言将坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365849_comment'></div>诚愚臣不克负荷。丕扬休烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365849_comment'></div>俾亡父之业。圣代莫传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365849_comment'></div>虽忝掖垣。若寘冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365849_comment'></div>伏惟陛下听政<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1365849", 1365849, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>中昃</span>。观书乙夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365849_comment'></div>思上皇而合道。恨古人于同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365849_comment'></div>而臣亡父所论君臣之际。必欲验之行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365849_comment'></div>非直垂于空文。诚宜上感宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365849_comment'></div>由<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365849", 1365849, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>没代</span>而匡补。下藏秘府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365849_comment'></div>因圣君以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1365849", 1365849, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>发明</span>。竟未上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365849_comment'></div>伏增悲惧。臣不胜感惕之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365849_comment'></div>谨缮写封进以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365849_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1365849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>　随后，改任太常少卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年6月</a>　本月，有奉和圣制烛龙斋祭诗。作品：《奉和圣制烛龙斋祭》<div id='poem_22933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制烛龙斋祭</a><span class='authorDate'>（726年6月）</span><span class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22933'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22933'>上帝临下，鉴亦有光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22933'>孰云阴骘，惟圣克彰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22933'>六月徂暑，四郊愆阳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22933'>我后其勤，告于坛场。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22933'>精意允溢，群灵鼓舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22933'>蔚兮朝云，沛然时雨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22933'>雨我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_22933", 22933, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>原田</span>，亦既有年。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22933'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_22933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年6月</a>　本月，有奉和圣制喜雨等诗作。作品：《奉和圣制喜雨》<div id='poem_22934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_22934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22934'>艰我稼穑，载育载亭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>　是年冬，赵颐贞赴安西都护任，九龄与张说等有诗送之。作品：《送赵都护赴安西》<div id='poem_22846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>　九龄在太常少卿任，对命相学颇有研究，是年前后，作有《百煞经》等论断及歌诀十八篇。作品：《飞廉煞》《亡神劫煞》《大耗煞歌》《穿心六害歌》《三刑歌》《吞啗煞歌》《流霞煞歌》《返伏吟》《孤辰寡歌》《歌断》《论黄幡豹尾》《红艳煞歌》《阴错阳差歌》《呻吟煞》《总论驾前神煞歌》《总论驾后神煞歌》《地煞赋总断》《百煞经》<br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　抵京后，有祭张燕公文。作品：《祭张燕公文》<div id='poem_1365961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1365961_comment'></div>谨以清酌少牢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365961_comment'></div>敢昭告于燕国公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365961_comment'></div>惟公应有期之运。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365961_comment'></div>精心惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365961_comment'></div>明未眹而先睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365961_comment'></div>听有馀而每黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365961_comment'></div>犹豹变而成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365961_comment'></div>尝凤鸣而中律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365961_comment'></div>故能羽翼圣后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365961_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365961", 1365961, id='poem_sentence_25_1365961_comment'></div>实大我之宗盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365961_comment'></div>与人君之姻娅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365961_comment'></div>天盖福善。<div id='poem_sentence_35_1365961_comment'></div>人亡令则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365961_comment'></div>国失良相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365961_comment'></div>学堕司南。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1365961_comment'></div>何天道之弗谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365961_comment'></div>追惟小子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365961_comment'></div>夙荷深期。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1365961_comment'></div>空匍匐而心断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365961_comment'></div>迹既拘于彝宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365961_comment'></div>情未展于哀款。<div id='poem_sentence_60_1365961_comment'></div>哀乌衣之往集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365961_comment'></div>庶羞虽薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365961_comment'></div>冀享厥诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365961_comment'></div>尊灵斯降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365961_comment'></div>是嘉平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365961_comment'></div>已矣万古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365961_comment'></div>缠绵五情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365961_comment'></div>追悲绪于离筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365961_comment'></div>结巨恨于幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365961_comment'></div>伏惟尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1365961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　抵京后，为信安王李祎献圣真图表。作品：《为信安王献圣真图表》<div id='poem_1365848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为信安王献圣真图表</a><span class='authorDate'>（731年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365848")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365848'>臣言。臣一昨扈从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365848_comment'></div>西狩岐阳。时以有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365848_comment'></div>事因农隙。整六军之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365848_comment'></div>修大田之礼。戎卒是训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365848_comment'></div>威武载扬。属草浅兽肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365848_comment'></div>霜清气杀。诏虞人以即鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365848_comment'></div>命荆州而起鸟。陛下亲御弧矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365848_comment'></div>纡驾林衡。曾不合围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365848_comment'></div>取其背者。虽有逸群之狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365848_comment'></div>走险之捷。而飞黄骋辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365848_comment'></div>萦拂如组。绿沈纵镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365848_comment'></div>宛转若神。必命中于前期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365848_comment'></div>皆应弦而绝倒。其馀变态不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365848_comment'></div>神妙无穷。非臣瞽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365848_comment'></div>所能模状。既而备献禽之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365848_comment'></div>虔荐寝之诚。教人以孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365848_comment'></div>自天作则。此外效获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365848_comment'></div>毕赐懿亲。兼禁羽骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365848_comment'></div>无犯宿麦。是行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365848_comment'></div>典礼斯备。仁恩允洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365848_comment'></div>三令惟肃。七德以宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365848_comment'></div>魏武何阶。亦纪功于猛兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365848_comment'></div>周文差拟。将比义于非熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365848_comment'></div>臣忝籍宗枝。幸陪銮辂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365848_comment'></div>窃观神武。冠绝古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365848_comment'></div>以为载之空言。不若图之绘事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365848_comment'></div>向所述圣。今皆写真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365848_comment'></div>虽天颜不违。而丹青莫拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365848_comment'></div>徒极愚思。庶存万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365848_comment'></div>谨录上陈。伏深战汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365848_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365848_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1365848_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年7月</a>　越大庾岭，有文。作品：《贺祈雨有应状》<div id='poem_1365880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365880'>右。臣一昨面奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365880_comment'></div>缘秋稼有望。时雨暂愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365880_comment'></div>念及黎元。见于颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365880_comment'></div>方躬自祈请。诚勤夙夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365880_comment'></div>上灵昭鉴。嘉瑞必臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365880_comment'></div>昨日申酉之閒。云物果应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365880_comment'></div>初含五色。正覆于坛场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365880_comment'></div>未及终宵。更洒于城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365880_comment'></div>遂使炎埃宿润。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1365880", 1365880, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>虐暑</span>暂消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365880_comment'></div>实冀肤寸之资。毕致普天之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365880_comment'></div>臣等多昧。徒仰于成造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365880_comment'></div>苍生何幸。每及于圣私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365880_comment'></div>无任欣戴忭跃之至。谨奉状陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　九龄有和吏部侍郎李林甫秋夜望月诗。作品：《和吏部李侍郎见示秋夜望月忆诸侍郎之什卒章有前后行之戏因命仆继作》<div id='poem_22818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22818' id='poem_content_1365745'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365745'>敕清夷军使虞灵章。穷寇伤残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365745_comment'></div>寄命无所。犹以遗噍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365745_comment'></div>敢犯塞垣。卿义勇过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365745_comment'></div>临难无苟。亲当矢石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365745_comment'></div>逐此犬羊。略有枭夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365745_comment'></div>足申威武。边寄尽节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365745_comment'></div>朕甚嘉之。仍闻锋镝既交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365745_comment'></div>在卿亦有所损。神道助顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365745_comment'></div>应不为灾。今将药物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365745_comment'></div>可以时疗。所有将士用命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365745_comment'></div>即具状以闻。其不幸阵亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365745_comment'></div>固将深悼惜。亦宜追恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365745_comment'></div>当有加赠。夏末甚热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365745_comment'></div>卿及将士巳下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365745_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　又奉命改作敕渤海王大武艺书，甚合上意。作品：《敕渤海王大武艺书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　转工部侍郎，仍充集贤院学士副知院事，有谢状。作品：《谢工部侍郎集贤院学士状》<div id='poem_1365892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_1365892_comment'></div>擢任集贤。远自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365892", 1365892, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>炎荒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365892_comment'></div>忽至霄汉。秘文副掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365892_comment'></div>浅陋无堪。遽蒙圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365892_comment'></div>反迁华省。<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365892_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年8月20日</a>　此日兼知制诰，亦有谢状。作品：《谢知制诰状》<div id='poem_1365893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰状</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年8月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1365893'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365893'>右。臣忝迹集贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365893_comment'></div>久无成效。幸免咎责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365893_comment'></div>伏用兢惶。忽蒙特恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365893_comment'></div>令知制诰。臣学业既浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365893_comment'></div>识理非长。述宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365893_comment'></div>诚恐不逮。跪受<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365893", 1365893, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>严命</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365893_comment'></div>伏增悚惕。无任戴荷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365893_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1365893_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年8月</a>　本月，或因张说之子中书舍人张均、驸马都尉张垍和符宝郎张埱三兄弟之请，敬撰燕公张说墓志铭。作品：《故开府仪同三司行尚书左丞相燕国公赠太师张公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1365948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故开府仪同三司行尚书左丞相燕国公赠太师张公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365948")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365948_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365948'>大唐有天下一百十三年。开元十有八载。龙集庚午。冬十二月戊申。开府仪同三司行尚书左丞相燕国公薨于位。享年六十四。呜呼哀哉。皇帝悼焉。素服举哀。废朝三日。乃下制赠太师。盖师傅之旧恩。礼有加也。诏葬先远。丧事有日。又特赐御词。表章琬炎。公义有忘身之勇。忠为社稷之卫。文武可宪之政。公侯作捍之勋。皆巳昭昭于天文。虽与日月争光可矣。公讳说。字道济。范阳方城人。晋司空壮武公之裔孙。周通道馆学士讳弋府君之曾孙。庆州都督讳恪府君之孙。赠丹州刺史刑部尚书讳骘府君之季子。自上世积庆。及公而祥发。神明所府。道德为枢。生以宁济。幼而休祥。鹰扬虎视。英伟磊落。越在诸生之中。已有绝云霓之望矣。初天后称制。举郡国贤良。公时大知名。拔乎其萃者也。起家太子校书。迄于左丞相。官政四十有一。而人臣之位极矣。尚书国之理本。公悉更之。中书朝之枢密。公亟掌之。休声与偕。升降数四。守正而见逐者一。遇坎而左迁者二。其馀总戎于外。为国作藩。所平除者。惟幽并秉节钺而巳。至若三登左右丞相。三作中书令。唐兴巳来。朝佐莫比。盖圣贤之运有会。师臣之道欲行。人虽求多。我每馀地。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365948'>馨香之发。敷闻自久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365948_comment'></div>宜其翊戴圣后。师范百寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365948_comment'></div>功烈过于如神。德声出于咸一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365948_comment'></div>此固与版筑崛起。屠钓作合之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365948_comment'></div>亦云异也。公志玄远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365948_comment'></div>而性高亮。未尝自异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365948_comment'></div>会节乃有立。何所不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365948_comment'></div>体道以为宗。既定国于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365948_comment'></div>亦保身之大雅。其于经理代务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365948_comment'></div>杂以军国。决事如流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365948_comment'></div>应物如响。纷纶辐辏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365948_comment'></div>其犹指掌。及夫先圣微旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365948_comment'></div>稽古未传。缺文必补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365948_comment'></div>坠礼咸甄。与经籍为笙簧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365948_comment'></div>于朝廷为粉泽。固不可详而载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365948_comment'></div>始公之从事。实以懿文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365948_comment'></div>而风雅陵夷。巳数百年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365948_comment'></div>时多吏议。摈落文人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365948_comment'></div>庸引雕虫。沮我胜气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365948_comment'></div>邱明有耻。子云不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365948_comment'></div>乃未知宗匠所作。王霸尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365948_comment'></div>及公大用。激昂后来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365948_comment'></div>天将以公为木铎矣。斯文岂丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365948_comment'></div>而今也则亡。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365948_comment'></div>克生以辅时。而臣道不究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365948_comment'></div>致用以利物。而人将安仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365948_comment'></div>上抚床以念往。下辍相而哀至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365948_comment'></div>复见之于公焉。太常议行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365948_comment'></div>谥曰文贞。二十年秋八月甲申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365948_comment'></div>迁窆于万安山之阳。燕国夫人元氏祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365948_comment'></div>夫人故尚书右司员外郎武陵公赠幽州都督讳怀景之女也。动为柔范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365948_comment'></div>皆可师训。及公之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365948_comment'></div>连姻帝室。虽处荣盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365948_comment'></div>若非在已。内执谦下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365948_comment'></div>外睦亲疏。古之贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365948_comment'></div>未始兼有。开元十九年三月壬戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365948_comment'></div>薨于东都康俗里第。享年六十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365948_comment'></div>长子均。中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365948_comment'></div>次曰垍。驸马都尉卫尉卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365948_comment'></div>季曰椒。符宝郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365948_comment'></div>泣血在疚。皆我之有后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365948_comment'></div>呜呼。元堂永閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365948_comment'></div>何事春秋。幽篆斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365948_comment'></div>亦云不朽而巳。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365948_comment'></div>天有密命。滋液百宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365948_comment'></div>时无大贤。谁与明道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365948_comment'></div>我公允叶。我德孔昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365948_comment'></div>翰飞戾天。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1365948", 1365948, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>羽仪</span>清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365948_comment'></div>功遂身谢。名由实美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365948_comment'></div>言而有立。古无不死。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　此间，九龄因老母年高体衰，曾数乞归养，玄宗未允，然深勉其孝心，迁其弟九皋、九章官近州里，适时归宁，九龄复上谢状以表感戴。作品：《谢两弟移官就养状》<div id='poem_1365894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢两弟移官就养状</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_2_1365894_comment'></div>岂堪国用。日月私照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365894_comment'></div>谬掌纶言。犬马以地近见矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365894_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1365894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　此间，九龄因老母年高体衰，曾数乞归养，玄宗未允，然深勉其孝心，迁其弟九皋、九章官近州里，适时归宁，九龄有诗寄两弟。作品：《二弟宰邑南海见群雁南飞因成咏以寄》<div id='poem_22870' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年12月</a>　本月，还西京。年末岁寒，有敕投降奚等书。作品：《敕投降奚等书》<div id='poem_1365759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕投降奚等书</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365759")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365759'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365759'>敕新来投降奚等。汝本小蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365759_comment'></div>不自存立。顷年依我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365759_comment'></div>稍得安全。而常持两端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365759_comment'></div>遽即背叛。忘恩负义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365759_comment'></div>岂是人心。今者闻汝复归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365759_comment'></div>亦应知过。仍缘困蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365759_comment'></div>未免嫌疑。汝若诚能洗心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365759_comment'></div>永以寄命。便令处置汝等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365759_comment'></div>当须一一听从。即舍往愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365759_comment'></div>更期来效。官赏诸事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365759_comment'></div>皆如旧日。各宜自勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365759_comment'></div>勿不知恩。比严寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365759_comment'></div>汝等部落百姓并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365759_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1365759_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　是年在工部侍郎、集贤院学士副知院事兼知制诰任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年1月1日</a>　此日，奉拟岁初处分德音敕文。作品：《敕岁初处分德音》<div id='poem_1365732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕岁初处分</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365732")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365732'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365732'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365732_comment'></div>天地以大德生群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365732_comment'></div>圣人以大宝守万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365732_comment'></div>古者受命之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365732_comment'></div>谓之承天之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365732_comment'></div>明有所代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365732_comment'></div>夫岂徒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365732_comment'></div>若道无钦崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365732_comment'></div>命不永保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365732_comment'></div>帝实临汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365732_comment'></div>人曷戴君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365732_comment'></div>朕所以每期庶乎合于仁覆之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365732_comment'></div>夫宓羲神农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365732_comment'></div>黄帝尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365732_comment'></div>或诛而不怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365732_comment'></div>或教而不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365732_comment'></div>彼亦何为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365732_comment'></div>独臻于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365732_comment'></div>朕自有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365732_comment'></div>二纪及兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365732_comment'></div>虽未能画衣以禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365732_comment'></div>亦未尝刑人于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365732_comment'></div>而政犹舛駮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365732_comment'></div>俗尚浇漓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365732_comment'></div>当是为理之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365732_comment'></div>未返于本耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365732_comment'></div>凡人岂不仁于父母兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365732_comment'></div>不欲于饮食衣服乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365732_comment'></div>而卒被无孝友之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365732_comment'></div>不温饱之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365732_comment'></div>其故何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365732_comment'></div>盖未闻义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365732_comment'></div>不识善道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365732_comment'></div>或任小智而为诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365732_comment'></div>或见小利而苟得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365732_comment'></div>致远则穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365732_comment'></div>继之以暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365732_comment'></div>已而身受戮诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365732_comment'></div>家不相保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365732_comment'></div>愚妄之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365732_comment'></div>类多自陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365732_comment'></div>讼狱之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365732_comment'></div>恒由此作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365732_comment'></div>吁可悲乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365732_comment'></div>亦在教之不明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365732_comment'></div>盖刑罚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365732_comment'></div>不获已而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365732_comment'></div>天下黔黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365732_comment'></div>皆朕赤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365732_comment'></div>以诚告示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365732_comment'></div>其或知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365732_comment'></div>何必用威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365732_comment'></div>然后致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365732_comment'></div>先务仁恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365732_comment'></div>宁不怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365732_comment'></div>且五常循行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365732_comment'></div>岂须深识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365732_comment'></div>六亲和睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365732_comment'></div>何待丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365732_comment'></div>自宜勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365732_comment'></div>以副所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365732_comment'></div>刑措不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365732_comment'></div>道在于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365732_comment'></div>今献岁之吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365732_comment'></div>迎气伊始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365732_comment'></div>敬顺天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365732_comment'></div>无违月令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365732_comment'></div>所由长吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365732_comment'></div>可举旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365732_comment'></div>诸有妪伏孕育之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365732_comment'></div>蠢动生植之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365732_comment'></div>慎无杀伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365732_comment'></div>致令夭伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365732_comment'></div>九土异宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365732_comment'></div>三农在候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365732_comment'></div>聚众兴役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365732_comment'></div>妨时害功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365732_comment'></div>特宜禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365732_comment'></div>以助春事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365732_comment'></div>至若家有征镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365732_comment'></div>人或孤茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365732_comment'></div>物向阳和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365732_comment'></div>此独忧悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365732_comment'></div>良可悯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365732_comment'></div>亦宜所由随事优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365732_comment'></div>盖不体仁无以为长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365732_comment'></div>不知道无以用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365732_comment'></div>故道者众妙之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365732_comment'></div>而心者万事之统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365732_comment'></div>得其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1365732", 1365732, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>要会</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365732_comment'></div>义可以兼济于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365732_comment'></div>失其指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365732_comment'></div>生不能自全于已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365732_comment'></div>故我元元皇帝著道德经五千文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365732_comment'></div>明乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_94_1365732", class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365732_comment'></div>去道弥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365732_comment'></div>违天和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365732_comment'></div>生人怨心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365732_comment'></div>朕甚厌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365732_comment'></div>所不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365732_comment'></div>各励精一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365732_comment'></div>共兴元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365732_comment'></div>俾苍生登于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365732_comment'></div>天下还于淳朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365732_comment'></div>岂远乎哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365732_comment'></div>行之可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365732_comment'></div>其老子道德经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365732_comment'></div>宜令士庶家藏一本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365732_comment'></div>仍劝习读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365732_comment'></div>使知指要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365732_comment'></div>每年贡举人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365732_comment'></div>量减尚书论语一两道策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365732_comment'></div>准数加老子策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365732_comment'></div>俾敦崇道本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365732_comment'></div>附益化源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365732_comment'></div>亦宜家置一本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365732_comment'></div>每须三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365732_comment'></div>以识朕怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_134_1365732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年2月</a>　本月，上表奉贺衢州进古铜器。作品：《贺衢州进古铜器》<div id='poem_1365884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
