id='poem_content_1365884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365884'>右。伏见衢州所进瑞鱼铭等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365884_comment'></div>神物瑰奇。形制纯古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365884_comment'></div>鱼为龙象。既彰受命之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365884_comment'></div>铭作龟文。更表<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365884", 1365884, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>锡年</span>之永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365884_comment'></div>河图旧事。无以加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365884_comment'></div>臣叶赞休明。屡承福应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365884_comment'></div>忝惟拜庆倍百恒情。伏望宣付史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365884_comment'></div>传之不朽。无任喜跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365884_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年2月</a>　本月，有授皇甫翼加阶制文。作品：《授皇甫翼等加阶制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　本年三月前，为侍中兼吏部尚书裴光庭画像作赞并序。作品：《侍中兼吏部尚书裴公画赞并序》<div id='poem_1365934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>侍中兼吏部尚书裴公画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365934")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365934_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365934'>元圣有作。大贤将其命。良弼有二。侍中是其一。所从龙虎。实感风云。我之裴公。道与上合。义深体国。策在忠主。亦既致于尧舜。不惟比于管乐。至于执人柄。振天纲。丹青帝图。金玉王度。虽古之作合。谓之有开。未始闻也。夫事可法。道可度。威可畏。仪可象。赫喧中来。精英外发。故工绘其事。所以见盛德之形容。士颂其功。所以知和气之导达。五事曰貌。一以作恭。七声成文。六乃为颂。俾凡今之人。色斯而睹奥。听之而知理。水有方折。辨和氏之价焉。山为具瞻。表师尹之重焉。赞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365934'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365934'>赫喧人望，时为国纪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365934'>伟量川渟，高标岳峙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365934'>磊落成节，精明入理。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365934'>倬哉辅臣，式是多士。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365934'>丹青炳发，俨如至止。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365934_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365934'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1365934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　有除韩休黄门侍郎平章事制文。作品：《除韩休黄门侍郎平章事制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年闰3月1日</a>　有敕十道朝集使，令其勤子自励，务在农桑，因地制宜，富民有教。作品：《敕处分十道朝集使》（之二）<div id='poem_1365726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕处分十道朝集使</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年闰3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365726")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365726'>敕十道及朝集使等。信赏以劝能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365726_comment'></div>刑罚以惩恶。谓之二柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365726_comment'></div>所以一人。朕念彼黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365726_comment'></div>比遭水旱。而赋役不等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365726_comment'></div>浮惰相仍。且无缉宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365726_comment'></div>渐用凋弊。所以慎择长吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365726_comment'></div>兼命使臣。宠数所加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365726_comment'></div>亦云不薄。智能自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365726_comment'></div>岂是末图。政之殊尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365726_comment'></div>永用虚伫。且郡县所理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365726_comment'></div>黎庶是切。善为政者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365726_comment'></div>防于未然。均其有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365726_comment'></div>省其徭役。事事有豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365726_comment'></div>早为之所。虽遭岁恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365726_comment'></div>固亦人安。况在丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365726_comment'></div>不能招辑。遂使户多虚挂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365726_comment'></div>人苦均摊。务欲削除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365726_comment'></div>更成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365726", 1365726, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>诡故</span>。已逃者未必为削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365726_comment'></div>为奸者因此便除。一启其端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365726_comment'></div>岂胜其弊。向若州有明牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365726_comment'></div>县有良宰。而精心缉理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365726_comment'></div>岂若是乎。卿等至州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365726_comment'></div>将朕此意。优柔慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365726_comment'></div>各令用心。招抚流庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365726_comment'></div>补缀居业。使免助逃之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365726_comment'></div>是为救弊之先。此不存心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365726_comment'></div>更知何理。且刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365726_comment'></div>专任不轻。自有非违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365726_comment'></div>将何率励。至如亲识游客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365726_comment'></div>凭恃威权。嘱托下寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365726_comment'></div>摇动狱讼。或差遣不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365726_comment'></div>致令损失。或处分有乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365726_comment'></div>便至烦扰。兼有不肃诸吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365726_comment'></div>唯只自谨一身。奸豪盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365726_comment'></div>无所畏惧。是虚荷荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365726_comment'></div>徒增禄秩。此而可容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365726_comment'></div>孰为尸旷。并委诸道条察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365726_comment'></div>具状奏闻。今甘泽以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365726_comment'></div>农桑为重。不急之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365726_comment'></div>先己勒停。宜更申明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365726_comment'></div>勿妨春事。诸处百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365726_comment'></div>贫寠者多。虽有陇亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365726_comment'></div>或无牛力。劝率相助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365726_comment'></div>令其有秋。所系囚徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365726_comment'></div>速令决断。无令冤滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365726_comment'></div>致有妨夺。𩻴寡茕独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365726_comment'></div>征镇之家。倍须抚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365726_comment'></div>勿有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1365726", 1365726, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>科唤</span>。朕所悬爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365726_comment'></div>惟待贤能。若政举一州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365726_comment'></div>惠施一县。使者廉问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365726_comment'></div>必以状闻。既能副于朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365726_comment'></div>亦当待以不次。诚可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365726_comment'></div>岂食言哉。并即好去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365726_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1365726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年闰3月8日</a>　此日，加正议大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　是年春，又敕十道朝集使，令其尽职守，务以农桑为重，以谋善政。作品：《敕处分十道朝集使》（之四）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　幽州副总管郭英杰讨契丹阵亡后，九龄有敕老将薛泰书，命其与王忠嗣等合谋，共讨叛藩。作品：《敕薛泰书》<div id='poem_1365742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕薛泰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365742")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365742'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365742'>敕薛泰。朕抚育降奚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365742_comment'></div>每事过厚。衣食供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365742_comment'></div>数年于兹。而禽兽无知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365742_comment'></div>不怀恩信。相率种落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365742_comment'></div>一时<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365742", 1365742, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>叛亡</span>。此于国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365742_comment'></div>譬犹蚊䖟耳。无所惮惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365742_comment'></div>惟恶恶心。总是乱阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365742_comment'></div>私相招诱。若不扑灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365742_comment'></div>何以示威。卿可率所统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365742_comment'></div>与纪思诲王忠嗣等计会进讨。卿既身在边镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365742_comment'></div>深练兵权。进退动静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365742_comment'></div>惟变所适。敌则预料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365742_comment'></div>奇出临时。会在审量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365742_comment'></div>不可轻举。气候渐暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365742_comment'></div>卿及将士已下并得如宜。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365742_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年4月1日</a>　此日，再敕十道朝集使，令其以亿兆为忧，妥善处理好括户问题，杜绝竞进，务于政成。作品：《敕处分十道朝集使》（之三）<div id='poem_1365726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕处分十道朝集使</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年闰3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365726")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365726'>敕十道及朝集使等。信赏以劝能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365726_comment'></div>刑罚以惩恶。谓之二柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365726_comment'></div>所以一人。朕念彼黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365726_comment'></div>比遭水旱。而赋役不等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365726_comment'></div>浮惰相仍。且无缉宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365726_comment'></div>渐用凋弊。所以慎择长吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365726_comment'></div>兼命使臣。宠数所加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365726_comment'></div>亦云不薄。智能自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365726_comment'></div>岂是末图。政之殊尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365726_comment'></div>永用虚伫。且郡县所理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365726_comment'></div>黎庶是切。善为政者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365726_comment'></div>防于未然。均其有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365726_comment'></div>省其徭役。事事有豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365726_comment'></div>早为之所。虽遭岁恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365726_comment'></div>固亦人安。况在丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365726_comment'></div>不能招辑。遂使户多虚挂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365726_comment'></div>人苦均摊。务欲削除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365726_comment'></div>更成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365726", 1365726, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>诡故</span>。已逃者未必为削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365726_comment'></div>为奸者因此便除。一启其端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365726_comment'></div>岂胜其弊。向若州有明牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365726_comment'></div>县有良宰。而精心缉理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365726_comment'></div>岂若是乎。卿等至州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365726_comment'></div>将朕此意。优柔慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365726_comment'></div>各令用心。招抚流庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365726_comment'></div>补缀居业。使免助逃之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365726_comment'></div>是为救弊之先。此不存心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365726_comment'></div>更知何理。且刺史县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365726_comment'></div>专任不轻。自有非违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365726_comment'></div>将何率励。至如亲识游客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365726_comment'></div>凭恃威权。嘱托下寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365726_comment'></div>摇动狱讼。或差遣不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365726_comment'></div>致令损失。或处分有乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365726_comment'></div>便至烦扰。兼有不肃诸吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365726_comment'></div>唯只自谨一身。奸豪盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365726_comment'></div>无所畏惧。是虚荷荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365726_comment'></div>徒增禄秩。此而可容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365726_comment'></div>孰为尸旷。并委诸道条察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365726_comment'></div>具状奏闻。今甘泽以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365726_comment'></div>农桑为重。不急之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365726_comment'></div>先己勒停。宜更申明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365726_comment'></div>勿妨春事。诸处百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365726_comment'></div>贫寠者多。虽有陇亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365726_comment'></div>或无牛力。劝率相助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365726_comment'></div>令其有秋。所系囚徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365726_comment'></div>速令决断。无令冤滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365726_comment'></div>致有妨夺。𩻴寡茕独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365726_comment'></div>征镇之家。倍须抚存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365726_comment'></div>勿有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1365726", 1365726, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>科唤</span>。朕所悬爵秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365726_comment'></div>惟待贤能。若政举一州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365718_comment'></div>征赋以归。河西节度大使原州都督庆王潭河东节度大使太原牧棣王洽河北节度大使幽州大都督鄂王涓等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365718_comment'></div>性皆中和。行无外饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365718_comment'></div>教以诗礼。能渐义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365718_comment'></div>虽已列于封圻。竟未畴于井赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365718_comment'></div>顷以孝友之习。且在深宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365718_comment'></div>服用之间。亦从御府。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年5月</a>　本月，有贺侍讲徧赐衣物状。作品：《贺侍讲徧赐衣物状》<div id='poem_1365876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年5月21日</a>　奉拟皇太子纳妃敕文。作品：《敕皇太子纳妃》<div id='poem_1365722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕皇太子纳妃</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年5月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365722")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365722'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365722'>敕。礼有谨于初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365722_comment'></div>义亦重其本。凡是姻媾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365722_comment'></div>且犹正于人伦。况在元良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365722_comment'></div>更将承于宗祀。皇太子鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365722_comment'></div>储副是属。仁孝自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365722_comment'></div>爰从吉辰。式备嘉礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365722_comment'></div>上事下继。君子重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365722_comment'></div>言告言归。朕岂无慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365722_comment'></div>非独在予之庆。宜申与众之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365722_comment'></div>应天下囚徒。死罪特宜免死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365722_comment'></div>配流岭南远处。流罪降至徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365722_comment'></div>徒已下罪并宜释放。其造伪头首勾合知情受伪人等罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365722_comment'></div>虽徒流仍便隶为百姓。至彼勿许东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365722_comment'></div>诸道征行人家及𩻴寡茕独。委州县长官检校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365722_comment'></div>矜放差科。使安其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365722_comment'></div>中间有不支济者。量事赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365722_comment'></div>仍量助其营种。长安万年两县百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365722_comment'></div>及今月当上彍骑卫士杂匠掌闲幕士驾士工人乐人供膳主膳官马主食<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作角）</span>弓等。并免其家今年地税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365722_comment'></div>三卫细引飞骑万骑监门长上及礼生有职掌者。各减一年劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365722_comment'></div>在京文武官九品以上。见在京外官因公使及当上在京新除五品以上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365722_comment'></div>外官未辞并致仕官朝朔望者。各赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365722_comment'></div>东宫官九品以上诸司。缘礼会祇供官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365722_comment'></div>更加勋一转。五礼使兵部尚书兼中书令萧嵩特封徐国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365722_comment'></div>礼会使黄门侍郎同中书门下平章事韩休特与三品。妃礼会使少府监冯绍正赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365722_comment'></div>诸副使及判官。更加勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365722_comment'></div>礼官傧者夹侍官及孔目官使典主旌节等。选日优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365722_comment'></div>仗内马家内侍省给使教坊音声人。缘太子礼会祇供者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365722_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。皇太子舅尚辇奉御赵回进特与三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365722_comment'></div>仍改三品官。前右武卫骑曹赵某<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>特与五品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365722_comment'></div>仍改与五品官。皇太子侍读侍书等各加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365722_comment'></div>皇太子谕德潘萧特与五品。太子妃兄通事舍人辥愿特与五品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365722_comment'></div>仍改与五品官。兄吏部常选辥某特与五品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365722_comment'></div>仍与六品官。今日应预会官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365722_comment'></div>各节级给赐物。即宜领取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365722_comment'></div>宴会者所以宣其情。颁锡者所以将其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365722_comment'></div>公卿百辟。庶知朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365722_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1365722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1365722'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365722_0'>⑴ 集作迥进一作向遵</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1365722_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年5月27日</a>　检校中书侍郎，遂有谢状。作品：《谢中书侍郎状》<div id='poem_1365895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365895'>右。臣谬迹书府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365895_comment'></div>兼司<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365895", 1365895, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>纶翰</span>。思力浅近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365895_comment'></div>无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365895", 1365895, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>发明</span>。圣恩不以不才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365895_comment'></div>却赐荣奖。拔擢非次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365895_comment'></div>荷跃惟深。但中书近密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365895_comment'></div>参掌不易。岂臣微贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365895_comment'></div>所堪忝窃。拜命之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365895_comment'></div>伏用惭惶。不胜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1365895", ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　秋末，有敕幽州节度张守珪书，对其履新，期待嘱托有加。作品：《敕幽州节度张守珪书》（之一）<div id='poem_1365765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365765' class='poemTitle class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365765_comment'></div>诚可残灭。适闻契丹及奚等并力合谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365765_comment'></div>同破凶丑。卿亦继进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365765_comment'></div>相与成功。此之一捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365765_comment'></div>使其丧气。然斗防困兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365765_comment'></div>诱备羸师。兵家之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365765_comment'></div>慎在终始。卿是宿将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365765_comment'></div>当自明之。若见可则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365765_comment'></div>务须灵敏。固在临事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365757_comment'></div>辅车相依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365757_comment'></div>奚既破伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365757_comment'></div>殆无遗噍。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　本年冬驾还西京后,九龄奉敕前往安国观等处行香,在观中得见玄宗为宁王李宪、故惠宜太子李业和代国金仙公主所写的《一切道经》四本,遂上状请付史馆,玄宗并依所请。作品：《上为宁王写一切经请宣付史馆状》<div id='poem_1365863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上为宁王写一切经请宣付史馆状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365863")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365863'>右。臣奉敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365863_comment'></div>今日于安国观行香。伏见天恩为宁王及故惠宣代国金仙公主共写一切道经四本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365863_comment'></div>伏以睿恩友爱。情深天属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365863_comment'></div>生成之德。无隔存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365863_comment'></div>利益之资。方宏道要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365863_comment'></div>诸经毕缮。景福云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365863_comment'></div>称赞兹日。功用有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365863_comment'></div>教义是先。诚所感庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365863_comment'></div>臣无任欣戴之至。望宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365863_comment'></div>奉状以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365863_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　本年冬,服阕后,玄宗恩赐衣物并授九皋殿中丞、九章太子司议郎,九龄即有谢状。作品：《谢赐衣物状》《谢两弟授官状》<div id='poem_1365902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐衣物状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365902")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365902'>右。高力士宣敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365902_comment'></div>赐臣衣及器物等。臣九龄不孝苟存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365902_comment'></div>企及礼制。天恩以忝枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365902_comment'></div>赐问再临。衣服珍器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365902_comment'></div>殊常宠锡。臣有何力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365902_comment'></div>可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365902", 1365902, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>叨滥</span>。渥泽至深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365902_comment'></div>诚效已竭。惟有微命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365902_comment'></div>不知所图。无任感戴惶悚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365902_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢两弟授官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365901")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365901'>右。伏奉昨二十日恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365901_comment'></div>授臣弟九皋殿中丞九章太子司议郎。臣私门积衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365901_comment'></div>殃罚如昨。日月逾迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365901_comment'></div>礼及外除。弟九皋等加以常才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365901_comment'></div>比服哀疚。瞻望未远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365901_comment'></div>缟练犹存。非常之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365901_comment'></div>一朝总集。惭惶哽咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365901_comment'></div>罔识言次。不知微命馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365901_comment'></div>何以上报大造。载悲载惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365901_comment'></div>五情飞越。不胜感戴战慄之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365901_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　玄宗欲加朔方节度使牛仙客尚书衔或实封,九龄坚执不可,林甫乘间进言,玄宗终封仙客。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年11月</a>　十一月,玄宗偏听谗言,欲废太子李瑛,九龄力谏不可。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　林甫再进谗言,玄宗渐疏九龄。九龄以省中必奉学识为高,贬斥了李林甫引为户部侍郎的萧炅,拟引中书侍郎严挺之为相,玄宗賜以尺诗,寓言警示,九龄退省感懼,遂上谢状。作品：《谢赐尺诗状》<div id='poem_1365899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐尺诗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365899")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365899'>右。今日高力士宣敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365899_comment'></div>赐臣等御制诗并<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365899", 1365899, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>宝尺</span>。伏以尺者纪度之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365899_comment'></div>宜丽天文。诗者律吕之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365899_comment'></div>是生节物。圣恩下逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365899_comment'></div>天旨旁流。因物寓言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365899_comment'></div>以言垂象。臣虽瞽陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365899_comment'></div>伏见宸衷。窃谢良工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365899_comment'></div>徒秉刀尺。终期死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365899_comment'></div>取配钧衡。而未副所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365899_comment'></div>退省知罪。臣等不胜负荷感惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365899_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　本年罢相前,对卢象、包融等颇加提携,擢卢象为左补阙，引包融为集贤殿学士、大理司直。又对李泌器重有加,并结为小友。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　复有谢弟授官状。因九龄为严挺之开脱,玄宗累积前事,以裴耀卿、九龄为阿党,二十七日并罢知政事,充左右丞相。作品：《谢弟授官状》<div id='poem_1365910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢弟授官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365910")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365910'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365910'>臣伏以圣恩非常。拔臣以无能受任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365910_comment'></div>岁月渐久。涓涘无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365910_comment'></div>取招毁议。有累圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365910_comment'></div>臣前面陈。诚以请罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365910_comment'></div>陛下不以赐责。又加过恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365910_comment'></div>特以殊荣。猥沾臣弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365910_comment'></div>弥速旷官之谤。且重非才之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365910_comment'></div>累延公器。宠及私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365910_comment'></div>颠覆是忧。陨越无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365910_comment'></div>不胜悚惧荷戴之至。谨奉状陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365910_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365910_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　东光县令谢混为政暴虐,九龄令监察御史张晓往按之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　罢相后,九龄有庭梅咏诗,流露其“孤危”、“飘荡”之预感。作品：《庭梅咏》<div id='poem_22769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　本年春,有咏燕诗,流露其激流勇退之意。作品：《咏燕》<div id='poem_22755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_22913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22913'>卜居旧何所，休浣尝来兹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22913'>轩盖有迷复，丘壑无磷缁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22913'>感物重所怀，何但止足斯。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22913'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_22913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年4月</a>　四月,渤海国遣其臣公伯计来献鹰鹘,九龄有鹰鹘图赞序。作品：《鹰鹘图赞序》<div id='poem_1365931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹰鹘图赞序</a><span class='authorDate'>（737年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365931")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365931'>鸟之鸷者。曰鹰曰鹘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365931_comment'></div>鹰也者。名扬于尚父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365931_comment'></div>义见于诗。鹘也者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365931_comment'></div>迹隐于古人。史阙其载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365931_comment'></div>岂昔之多识。物亦有遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365931_comment'></div>将今而嘉生。材无不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365931_comment'></div>为所呼之变。与所记之不同者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365931_comment'></div>然于羽族之中。绝有豪杰之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365931_comment'></div>气感刚悍。体侔铦锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365931_comment'></div>顾视之间伟如也。夫授以劲翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365931_comment'></div>意不群飞。资其利觜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365931_comment'></div>义在鲜食。生有自然之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365931_comment'></div>用无可抑之势。古之言武士法吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365931_comment'></div>齐名比义者。以其严若郅都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365931_comment'></div>飞若李广。委质于所事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365931_comment'></div>报功于所养。不惮摧翼以亏勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365931_comment'></div>不立垂枝以屈节。是鸟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365931_comment'></div>向之拟议。不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365931_comment'></div>夫鸾与凤将感于仁。所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365931_comment'></div>鸡与鹤犹较其德。彼何有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365931_comment'></div>况其馀虽飞虽鸣。凡者怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365931_comment'></div>肉非登俎。才非下鞲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365931_comment'></div>威力不敌。群噪无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365931_comment'></div>然后知二禽之为用。众鸟之绝伦者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365931_comment'></div>故君子韪其然。工人图其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365931_comment'></div>以象武备。以彰才美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365931_comment'></div>虽未极其天姿。有以见其风骨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365931_comment'></div>昔支遁道林常养名马。自云重其神骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365931_comment'></div>斯图也。非彼人之徒欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365931_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1365931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　因周子谅事件所牵,二十日左迁荆州大都督府长史。先所置陈、许、豫、寿等州屯田亦废。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
韶关

class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22853'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_22853_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪王司马宴王少府东阁序</a><span class='authorDate'>（717年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365922")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365922'>夫道行与废命也。非谋之不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365922_comment'></div>命通与塞时也。岂力之为弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365922_comment'></div>古之君子。推其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365922_comment'></div>养其和。仲尼得之以弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365922_comment'></div>傅说因之以版筑。至若诗有怨刺之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365922_comment'></div>骚有愁思之文。求之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365922_comment'></div>匪云大雅。王六官志其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365922_comment'></div>司马公引而申之。谪居何心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365922_comment'></div>不欲贾生之投吊。穷愁非我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365922_comment'></div>安用虞卿之著书。尝以风月在怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365922_comment'></div>江山为事。簿领何废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365922_comment'></div>形胜不辜。既好乐而无荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365922_comment'></div>亦上同而不混。迨乎倚层阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365922_comment'></div>凭华轩。川泽清明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365922_comment'></div>上悬秋景。岑岭回合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365922_comment'></div>下带溪流。联草树而心摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365922_comment'></div>际烟氛而目尽。兹邦枕倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365922_comment'></div>是日登临。岂子虚之过诧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365922_comment'></div>诚仲宣之信美。物色起殊乡之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365922_comment'></div>谁则无情。而道术得异人之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365922_comment'></div>吾方有遣。于是旨酒时献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365922_comment'></div>清谈閒发。歌沧浪以放言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365922_comment'></div>咏蟋蟀而伤俭。盖古人之作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365922_comment'></div>岂异于斯。盍赋诗以扬其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365922_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1365922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=717&endYear=717')">717年9月14日</a>　此日，作有文。作品：《为王司马祭甄都督文》《为王司马祭妻父文》<div id='poem_1365960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王司马祭甄都督文</a><span class='authorDate'>（717年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1365960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365960'>维开元五年岁次丁巳九月丁酉朔十四日庚戌。某官谨以清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365960_comment'></div>祭于广州都督甄公之灵。惟公禀气异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365960_comment'></div>为国良臣。资忠秉义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365960_comment'></div>奋翼跃鳞。富贵自取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365960_comment'></div>声名益震。故能北拥旄于元朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365960_comment'></div>南仗节于朱垠。行部无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365960_comment'></div>卧理斯属。棠阴在听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365960_comment'></div>䪥歌成曲。下流是仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365960_comment'></div>长涂反促。始望雨而随车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365960_comment'></div>遽惊风而转烛。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365960_comment'></div>甫兹岁首。彤襜载辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365960_comment'></div>今也秋季。丹旐言归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365960_comment'></div>既寒来而暑往。将物改而人非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365960_comment'></div>驷马不驭。双雁空飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365960_comment'></div>对平生之气象。咏宿昔之音徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365960_comment'></div>燕越兮地眇。胡山兮路微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365960_comment'></div>奠肴觞之在席。感徒御以沾衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365960_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365960_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1365960_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王司马祭妻父文</a><span class='authorDate'>（717年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=717&endYear=717')">717年</a>　秋与王履震有广州之游。作品：《与王六履震广州津亭晓望》<div id='poem_22728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与王六履震广州津亭晓望</a><span class='authorDate'>（717年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_22728'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22728'>明发临前渚，寒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作潮）</span>来净远空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22728'>水纹天上碧，日气海边红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22728'>景物纷为异，人情赖此同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22840'>江间稻正熟，林里桂初荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22840'>鱼意思在藻，鹿心怀食苹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22840'>时哉苟不达，取乐遂吾情。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22824'>通籍微躯幸，归途明主恩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22824'>匪唯徇行役，兼得慰晨昏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22824'>是节暑云炽，纷吾心所尊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22824'>海县且悠缅，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_22824", 22824, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>山邮</span>日骏奔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22824'>徒知恶嚣事，未暇息阴论。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22824'>峣武经陈迹，衡湘指故园。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22824'>水闻南涧险，烟望北林繁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22824'>远霭千岩合，幽声百籁喧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22824'>阴泉夏犹冻，阳景昼方暾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22824'>懿此高深极，徒令梦想存。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22824'>盛明期有报，长往复奚言。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22824'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_22824_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='62ac7581101c4f7894c2f98a54deccf8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62ac7581101c4f7894c2f98a54deccf8");'><span id='62ac7581101c4f7894c2f98a54deccf8_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=719&endYear=719')">719年</a>　北还途中，有诗。作品：《南阳道中作》<div id='poem_22903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_22903'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22903'>登郢属岁阴，及宛懵所适。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22903'>复闻东汉主，遗此南都迹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22903'>佳气蔼厥初，霸图纷在昔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22903'>兹邦称贵近，与世尝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22903", 22903, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>薰赫</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22903'>遭遇感风云，变衰空草泽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22903'>不识邓公树，犹传<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_22903", 22903, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_22903", 22903, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>闉阇</span>，荆榛翳阡陌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22903'>事去物无象，感来心不怿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22903'>怀古对穷秋，兴言伤远客。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22903'>眇默遵岐路，辛勤弊行役。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22903'>云雁号相呼，林麇走自索。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22903'>顾忆徇书剑，未尝安枕席。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22903'>岂暇墨突黔，空持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_22903", 22903, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>辽豕白</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22903'>迷复期非远，归欤赏农隙。<div -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a01fd81ae0c44150859f946ddfd97a95_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a01fd81ae0c44150859f946ddfd97a95");'><span id='a01fd81ae0c44150859f946ddfd97a95_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>，46岁</div><div id='a01fd81ae0c44150859f946ddfd97a95' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>　为中书舍人。春正月，随玄宗自洛阳北巡潞州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='db19f6ce0c4546acaad16f39c77374be_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("db19f6ce0c4546acaad16f39c77374be");'><span id='db19f6ce0c4546acaad16f39c77374be_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=725')">724-725年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='db19f6ce0c4546acaad16f39c77374be' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年12月13日</a>　此日，加守中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年闰12月</a>　本月在洛阳撰有文。作品：《惠庄太子哀册文并序》<div id='poem_1365954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惠庄太子哀册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年闰12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365954")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365954'>维开元十二年岁次甲子十二月丁巳朔二十四日庚辰。司徒申王薨于行在所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365954_comment'></div>册谥惠庄太子。旋殡于寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365954_comment'></div>粤闰十二月二十七日壬午。将陪葬于桥林之柏城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365954_comment'></div>黼幕宵布。羽纛宿设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365954_comment'></div>西序启攒。南首成列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365954_comment'></div>皇帝深天伦之戚。崇后储之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365954_comment'></div>拟容卫于青宫。申孔怀于朱邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365954_comment'></div>爰命史氏。稽于令则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365954_comment'></div>无俾直书。不彰遗德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365954_comment'></div>词臣曰。昊天有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365954_comment'></div>先后受之。分王子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365954_comment'></div>藩卫京师。克荷成宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365954_comment'></div>罔弗肃祇。懿哉明哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365954_comment'></div>诞惟神粹。宣慈日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365954_comment'></div>孝友天至。道则吻合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365954_comment'></div>迹无自异。性则生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365954_comment'></div>学兼时习。易微书远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365954_comment'></div>诗言礼立。德必有邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365954_comment'></div>善如不及。贵而能损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365954_comment'></div>量固难挹。方伯出镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365954_comment'></div>召南取斯。司徒入掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365954_comment'></div>郑武其宜。义之所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365954_comment'></div>政乃克施。物留遗爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365954_comment'></div>事著成规。西夏息人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365954_comment'></div>东征叶卜。炜炜同辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365954_comment'></div>皇皇改服。疾搆中路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365954_comment'></div>凶传左毂。宁不慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365954_comment'></div>奄钟斯酷。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365954_comment'></div>昔在冲眇。具惟兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365954_comment'></div>四国并封。五王均体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365954_comment'></div>游必连骑。居则同邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365954_comment'></div>各承爱于含饴。俱受经于置醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365954_comment'></div>既荏苒而云迈。属殷忧之将启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365954_comment'></div>实定祸于萧墙。遂继明于云陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365954_comment'></div>虽隔深宫之卫。常洽家人之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365954_comment'></div>曷殂谢以痛心。感平生而流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365954_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。爰择茂典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365954_comment'></div>追崇上嗣。表先圣之元良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365954_comment'></div>申友于之褒异。纷卤簿以徒设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365954_comment'></div>俨文物而空备。彼神仪之如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365954_comment'></div>乃群悲之所萃。周礼从祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365954_comment'></div>汉茔是陪。先远日而选吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365954_comment'></div>会同盟以送哀。夜漏尽兮暗室启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365954_comment'></div>庭燎残兮晓挽催。按三校而徐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365954_comment'></div>将一去而不回。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365954_comment'></div>背朱门兮迟迟。驰白骥兮骙骙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365954_comment'></div>野苍茫而助惨。风萧飋而增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365954_comment'></div>翩翩兮素盖。寂寂兮画帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365954_comment'></div>遵旧途而何有。览陈迹以如疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365954_comment'></div>面都邑兮不入。待陵寝兮有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365954_comment'></div>惟光仪之永閟。与昭代而长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365954_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。潜清晖于幽穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365954_comment'></div>召鸿名于美迹。将在皇储之史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365954_comment'></div>岂伊诸侯之策。播遗芳于兰桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365954_comment'></div>传不朽于金石。谅纪言之在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365954_comment'></div>嘉德音之无斁。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365954_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1365954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>　本年前后，还为故襄州刺史靳恒撰有遗爱碑并序。作品：《故襄州刺史靳公遗爱碑并序》<div id='poem_1365938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故襄州刺史靳公遗爱碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365938")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365938_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365938'>江汉閒州以十数。而襄阳为大。旧多三辅之豪。今则一都之会。故在晋称南雍。在楚为北津。厥繇哤杂。亦云难理。而前此领郡。鲜能安人。或宽或猛。或拘或抗。迹多弗类。俗亦弗宁。是以天子念与我之理。而公受烦卿之寄矣。公名恒。字子济。其先某人也。祖帅。幽州长史。父礼庭。奉天讨监察御史。世不苟合。义在难进。虽无充量之位。而有积善之烈矣。公性持重。有器望。即温而厉。居敬而。度量可以轨物。德义可以服人。而先王遗言。率由好学。君子行道。必本忠恕。浚源水洁。厉翼云翔。故一举为拾遗。已有远致。三入为御史。侃然正色。当时知音。谓且大用。而尚书理本。郎官选才。亟践诸曹。克压群议。及再典大郡。遂佐益州。摄御史丞。都督西南军事。原轸超将。岂惟上德。翁归中立。实兼文武。先是兵连蛮徼。岁转军储。扰我公私。费以巨亿。公乃急其所病。思有以易之。建大田于云南。罢馈粮于巴蜀。向之踰重阻。冒毒瘴。负担以踣毙。垂耳于剽掠者。每十有五六。及公底绩。尽境赖全。至于是邦也。政实有素。今也惟行。不违其方。以索其极。莫不教之诲之。优之柔之。从者善之。否则威之。先德后刑。端本肇末。物知所劝。事则有经。率训者众多。变薄为厚。感惠者深远。既和且均。夫然后人斯耻格。庭少诤讼。参佐閒拱。属城晏如。其始也一年而政成。其终也三年而颂兴。爱之如父母。畏之如神明。开元十二年。以理迹尤异。廉使上达。天子嘉之。稍迁陕州刺史。暨解印去郡。攀车盈途。或愿借无缘。而人吏遮道。或瞻望弗及。而老幼啼呼。如是者五里已终朝。十日乃出界。而皆有言曰。舍我何之。及闻公之丧。哀可知矣。市为之罢。舂以之辍。惠爱之结深。古今之感一。盖为仁由已。而遗德在人者。其若是乎。郡中士大夫。与门生故吏。聚族而议撰德。是以刻石立纪。彼鲖阳之陋。堕泪成碑。此岘山之绩。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365938'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365938'>英英靳公，宣哲秉彝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365938'>为我髦士，作人元龟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365938'>倜傥大节，磊落<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365938", 1365938, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>瑰词</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365938'>人亦有言，天实资之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365938'>御史直绳，郎官高选。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365938'>动必兼遂，能皆再践。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365938'>纠遏邦慝，弥纶事典。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365938'>遂及我人，化流樊沔。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365938'>激厉素风，抑扬善政。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365938'>约纪为法，急人所病。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1365938'>物故推诚，事匪忘敬。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365938'>感被于下，仁明在咏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365938'>举德不鲜，涉道载深。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365938'>穆然清风，莫其遗音。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1365938'>繄公既没，厥迹可寻。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1365938'>勒石是图，以慰氓心。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1365938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1365938'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365938_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>　约本年，在洛阳作有序，姑系于此。作品：《送幽州王长史赴军序》<div id='poem_1365927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送幽州王长史赴军序</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365927")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365927'>渔阳。我之巨镇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365927_comment'></div>慎选军佐。敷求<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365927", 1365927, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>国良</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365927_comment'></div>以王公能。有命汝往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365927_comment'></div>底其耕战之事。介于将吏之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365927_comment'></div>则已声籍天庭。气雄辽碣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365927_comment'></div>鹰扬有日。马首欲东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365927_comment'></div>自名卿大夫。与时髦懿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365927_comment'></div>莫不激其节而重其迈。结轸连袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365927_comment'></div>携壶抱琴。留饮极于郊歧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365927_comment'></div>望美延于朔裔者。不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365927_comment'></div>仲月暄矣。阳时<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1365927", 1365927, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>贲若</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365927_comment'></div>植物之发芳香。行人之感意气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365927_comment'></div>不曰群萃。岂怀安于鹿豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365927_comment'></div>不曰垂堂。已载驰于原隰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365927_comment'></div>孰不知西笑之美。况伊岁华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365927_comment'></div>东征之勤。兼彼戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365927_comment'></div>盖乐不遑舍。君人之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365927_comment'></div>义不顾私。志士之为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365927_comment'></div>今之作者。闻而休之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365927_comment'></div>各赋诗一章。以志其善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365927_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1365927_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_6_1365921_comment'></div>博闻多识之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365921_comment'></div>自开元肇建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365921_comment'></div>以迄于今。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1365921_comment'></div>以为候彼神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365921_comment'></div>事虽千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365921_comment'></div>传于方士。<div id='poem_sentence_26_1365921_comment'></div>去华务实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365921_comment'></div>且有后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365921_comment'></div>增其学秩。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年4月</a>　在中书舍人任。时张说甚重文学之士，九龄与韦述、许景先、袁晖、赵冬曦、孙逖、王翰等常游其门。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年9月13日</a>　在中书舍人任。此日潞州献瑞应图，玄宗命唤取蕃邸旧僚，问其实事，然后修图，九龄为此撰序。作品：《圣应图赞并序》<div id='poem_1365933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣应图赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年9月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365933")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365933_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365933'>臣闻启圣者天也。宜有以觉悟。受命者圣也。必有以明徵。故神不言而可知。时将至而先兆。当陛下龙潜上党也。或托类于云物。或效灵于卜筮。意者天之丁宁垂象。唯恐后时。又以潞水之泓深。山鹿之捷走。驰骑是获。厉流不濡。非力所能。以明或跃。乾之上体。时在九四。神道幽赞。圣期密迩。自后而占。何著明其若此。盖天福海内。地降圣迹。以瑞非常之后。以决如神之策。至于再三。明必信耳。有郡掾崔弼。时其从行。见龙骑先驰。谓河流可涉。亦既数步。遽己灭顶。不沈也。安足以验飞。无凡也。于何以昭圣。事来自久。命常维新。臣不胜至愿。谨为圣应图。遂献赞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365933'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365933'>龙之或跃，泉有何深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365933'>神亦成象，化为背禽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365933'>淩厉是获，明命则忱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365933'>如彼从掾，焉能不沈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365933_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365933'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1365933_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=726&endYear=726')">726年</a>　还东都复命后，制授冀州刺史。作品：《使还都湘东作》<div id='poem_22890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年11月</a>　本月，从祀后土汾阴，奉撰赦书，玄宗览而嘉之，誉其有王佐之才。作品：《后土赦书》<div id='poem_1365839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后土赦书</a><span class='authorDate'>（732年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365839'>门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365839_comment'></div>昔者巡狩所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365839_comment'></div>柴瘗斯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365839_comment'></div>盖取诚享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365839_comment'></div>以遵告类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365839_comment'></div>朕恭承祖宗之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365839_comment'></div>获主神祗之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365839_comment'></div>夙夜祗畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365839_comment'></div>不敢荒宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365839_comment'></div>故勒兵朔陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365839_comment'></div>先展义于汾社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365839_comment'></div>回旆脽上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365839_comment'></div>遂有事于郊坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365839_comment'></div>王者父事天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365839_comment'></div>母事地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365839_comment'></div>汉氏祈谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365839_comment'></div>未始正名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365839_comment'></div>周礼降神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365839_comment'></div>乃为徼福而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365839_comment'></div>朕以天命之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365839_comment'></div>子道为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365839_comment'></div>惟兹精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365839_comment'></div>在乎敦孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365839_comment'></div>庶蒙福于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365839_comment'></div>期永康于兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365839_comment'></div>是以率由旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365839_comment'></div>敬恭明祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365839_comment'></div>严配之诚既展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365839_comment'></div>奠献之礼又终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365839_comment'></div>且春秋之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365839_comment'></div>大事在祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365839_comment'></div>斋祭之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365839_comment'></div>庶品维祺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365839_comment'></div>岂独在予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365839_comment'></div>而有斯庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365839_comment'></div>可大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365839_comment'></div>自开元二十年十一月二十一日昧爽已前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365839_comment'></div>大辟罪已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365839_comment'></div>罪无轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365839_comment'></div>已发觉未发觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365839_comment'></div>已结正未结正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365839_comment'></div>系囚见徒常赦所不免者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365839_comment'></div>咸赦除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365839_comment'></div>官人犯赃及有罪被推者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365839_comment'></div>本罪虽原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365839_comment'></div>不得更令却上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365839_comment'></div>仍别与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365839_comment'></div>自先天已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365839_comment'></div>有杂犯流移人等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365839_comment'></div>并配隶人等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365839_comment'></div>各量移近处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365839_comment'></div>左降官未经量移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365839_comment'></div>及经量移未复本资者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365839_comment'></div>奏听进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365839_comment'></div>天下遭损免州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365839_comment'></div>应损户成<span class='inlineComment2'>（诏令作减）</span>一分已上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365839_comment'></div>及供顿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365839_comment'></div>无出今年地税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365839_comment'></div>如已徵纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365839_comment'></div>听折来年地税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365839_comment'></div>逋租悬调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365839_comment'></div>贷粮种子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365839_comment'></div>欠负官物在百姓腹内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365839_comment'></div>并宜放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365839_comment'></div>其不损处<span id='poem_sentence_116_1365839_comment'></div>内外文武官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365839_comment'></div>三品以上赐爵一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365839_comment'></div>四品己下各加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365839_comment'></div>致仕官三品已上赐物七十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365839_comment'></div>四品五品各五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365839_comment'></div>行从蕃客鸿胪安置陪位见大礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365839_comment'></div>宜赐物五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365839_comment'></div>节级分付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365839_comment'></div>南北衙应宿卫斋宫官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365839_comment'></div>及左右厢知兵马虞候总管已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365839_comment'></div>及判官别奏兼孔目官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365839_comment'></div>更加勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365839_comment'></div>前资官选日稍优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365839_comment'></div>白身人有资劳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365839_comment'></div>简选之日优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365839_comment'></div>无资荫者赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365839_comment'></div>南北衙行从三卫飞骑万骑引驾细引及监门直长主帅黄衣长上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365839_comment'></div>各赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365839_comment'></div>仍各赐物五段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365839_comment'></div>两营弩<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作弓）</span>手六番并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365839_comment'></div>宜各赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365839_comment'></div>物五段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365839_comment'></div>仍量折番役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365839_comment'></div>诸卫彍骑及兵角弓手官马主掌闲幕士驾士供膳士供膳主习驭工人乐人杂户官户白身有职掌人合行从人等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365839_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365839_comment'></div>物三段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365839_comment'></div>其斋郎既是见任官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365839_comment'></div>准坛上坛下有职掌官例处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365839_comment'></div>执弹三卫及礼生赞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365839_comment'></div>各减二年劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365839_comment'></div>无劳可减者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365839_comment'></div>选日稍优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365839_comment'></div>流外行署从者各赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365839_comment'></div>有职掌者各赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365839_comment'></div>供顿州刺史同陪位官例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365839_comment'></div>始末专知顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365839_comment'></div>官各与一中上考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365839_comment'></div>蒲州刺史宝鼎县官同升坛官处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365839_comment'></div>管坛一乡百姓给复二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365839_comment'></div>蒲州侍老等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365839_comment'></div>准太原潞州例降一等处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365839_comment'></div>武德初功臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365839_comment'></div>每有大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365839_comment'></div>必存追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365839_comment'></div>业参运始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365839_comment'></div>义合赏延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365839_comment'></div>其子孙沈翳无在朝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365839_comment'></div>宜令勘实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365839_comment'></div>即与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365839_comment'></div>唐<sup id='poem_sentence_172_1365839_comment'></div>有亡没者优赠一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1365839_comment'></div>仍与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1365839_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_218_1365839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1365839'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1365912_comment'></div>赐臣紫骝马一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365912_comment'></div>伏以恩覃不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365912_comment'></div>宠遇非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365912_comment'></div>有忝股肱之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365912_comment'></div>频奉渥洼之赐。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年2月19日</a>　此日,奏置十道采访处置使,玄宗允纳,复有敕文。作品：《敕置十道使》<div id='poem_1365729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365729'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365729'>敕。岁比不登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365729_comment'></div>人或流亡。言念菜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365729_comment'></div>朕用疚怀。而牧宰是寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365729_comment'></div>惠养犹缺。黎元为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365729_comment'></div>赋敛未均。当宁思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365729_comment'></div>良所于邑。且十连为率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365729_comment'></div>六察分条。周汉以还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365729_comment'></div>事有因革。帝王之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365729_comment'></div>义在随时。其天下诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365729_comment'></div>宜依旧逐要便置使。令采访处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365729_comment'></div>若牧宰无政。不能纲理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365729_comment'></div>吏人有犯。所在侵渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365729_comment'></div>及物土异宜。人情不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365729_comment'></div>差科赋税。量事取安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365729_comment'></div>朕所责成。贵在简要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365729_comment'></div>其馀常务。不可横干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365729_comment'></div>其使宜令中书门下即简择奏闻。朕将亲览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365729_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1365729_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年2月19日</a>　此日，有敕授卢绚等十道使文。作品：《敕授十道使》<div id='poem_1365730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365730' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_1_1365730_comment'></div>心必遍于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365730_comment'></div>自古良牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365730_comment'></div>福犹润于京师。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365730_comment'></div>朝散大夫检校御史中丞关内道宣慰赈给使上柱国卢绚等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365730_comment'></div>任寄已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365730_comment'></div>声实兼茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365730_comment'></div>咸贯通于理道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365730_comment'></div>益纯固于公心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365730_comment'></div>或华发不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365730_comment'></div>或白圭无玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365730_comment'></div>可以范仪郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365730_comment'></div>康济黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365730_comment'></div>间岁已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365730_comment'></div>数州失稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365730_comment'></div>颇致流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365730_comment'></div>能勿殷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365730_comment'></div>吏又不畏不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365730_comment'></div>人或不安不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365730_comment'></div>诚须矫过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365730_comment'></div>必在仗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365730_comment'></div>而前此使车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365730_comment'></div>不无殷鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365730_comment'></div>事皆掣肘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365730_comment'></div>务欲总权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365730_comment'></div>小有举于毫发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365730_comment'></div>大莫振于纲领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365730_comment'></div>本不条察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365730_comment'></div>却用烦苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365730_comment'></div>永言所期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365730_comment'></div>岂云自弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365730_comment'></div>今既各膺重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365730_comment'></div>允谓通才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365730_comment'></div>以蠲疾苦之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365730_comment'></div>当叶大中之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365730_comment'></div>若令行一道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365730_comment'></div>利及万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365730_comment'></div>朕所设官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365730_comment'></div>以待能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365730_comment'></div>朝之优秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365730_comment'></div>必归令誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365730_comment'></div>言可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365730_comment'></div>宜副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365730_comment'></div>可依前件。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1365730_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年3月</a>　在洛阳，有应制十道采访使及朝集使诗。作品：《奉和圣制送十道采访处置使及朝集使》<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　正月所赐官宅增修完毕,什物齐备,九龄以为过于弘敞,有奢侈和贪冒之嫌,恳请朝廷收回,玄宗御批不允,并命择日移入。作品：《让赐宅状》<div id='poem_1365906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365906' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365906_comment'></div>臣之俸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365906_comment'></div>实为丰厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365906_comment'></div>足办私室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365906_comment'></div>今崇其甲第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365906_comment'></div>更使增修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365906_comment'></div>其如物议何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365906_comment'></div>其如公道何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365906_comment'></div>望并却令官收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365906_comment'></div>无任惶惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1365906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年3月</a>　三月,初知政事。奏请放私铸钱,以缓通货短缺之弊,玄宗意欲采纳试行，后遭众人訾议而被迫放弃。作品：《议放私铸钱敕》<div id='poem_1365737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕议放私铸钱</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365737")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365737'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365737'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365737_comment'></div>布帛不可以尺寸为交易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365737_comment'></div>菽粟不可以杪勺贸有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365737_comment'></div>故古之为钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365737_comment'></div>将以通货币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365737_comment'></div>盖人所作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365737_comment'></div>非天实生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365737_comment'></div>顷者耕织为资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365737_comment'></div>乃稍贱而伤本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365737_comment'></div>磨铸之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365737_comment'></div>却以少而致贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365737_comment'></div>顷虽官铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365737_comment'></div>所入无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365737_comment'></div>约工计本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365737_comment'></div>劳费又多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365737_comment'></div>公私之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365737_comment'></div>给用不赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365737_comment'></div>永言其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365737_comment'></div>岂无变通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365737_comment'></div>往者汉文之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365737_comment'></div>已有放铸之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365737_comment'></div>虽见非于贾谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365737_comment'></div>亦无费于贤君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365737_comment'></div>况古往今来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365737_comment'></div>时异事变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365737_comment'></div>反经之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365737_comment'></div>安有定耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365737_comment'></div>终然固拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365737_comment'></div>必无足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365737_comment'></div>且欲不禁私铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365737_comment'></div>其理如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365737_comment'></div>公卿百僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365737_comment'></div>详议可否。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年3月</a>　本月,拟有处分新除河南府密县县令张稷等人的敕文。作品：《敕处分县令》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年3月</a>　本月，又有敕牧宰处分选入等文。作品：《敕处分选人》<div id='poem_1365736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_11_1365736_comment'></div>声绩有称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365736_comment'></div>即当待以不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365736_comment'></div>信斯言之可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365736_comment'></div>并于朝堂坐食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365736_comment'></div>食讫好去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1365736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年4月</a>　夏四月,北庭都护刘涣谋反被诛后,九齡连敕安西都护王斛斯和西州都督张待宾等入,通报情况,嘉勉其忠义守边,并令其严防突骑施窥隙。作品：《敕安西节度王斛斯书》《敕西州都督张待宾书》<div id='poem_1365744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕西州都督张待宾书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span
