id='poem_sentence_0_1365744_comment'></div>累得卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365744_comment'></div>一一具知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365744_comment'></div>刘涣凶狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365744_comment'></div>自取诛灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365744_comment'></div>远近闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365744_comment'></div>莫不庆快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365744_comment'></div>卿诚深疾恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365744_comment'></div>初屡表闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365744_comment'></div>边事动静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365744_comment'></div>皆尔用意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365744_comment'></div>即朕无忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365744_comment'></div>夏初渐热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365744_comment'></div>卿及将士官僚百姓已下并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365744_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365744_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　五月,谏相李林甫。作品：《奏劾林甫》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　五月,奉诏简校覆讫两京都城在押囚徒。时有“张公口案”之誉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　致敕北庭将士百姓,对北庭将士百姓同心尽力、一举荡平逆贼刘涣,予以嘉并。作品：《敕北庭将士百姓等书》<div id='poem_1365750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕北庭将士百姓等书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365750")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365750'>敕北庭将士部落及百姓等。忠义所感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365750_comment'></div>在臣子而固然。凶恶必诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365750_comment'></div>虽鬼神而亦尔。逆贼刘涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365750_comment'></div>不意含气有此狂愚。忽于夷涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365750_comment'></div>坐生逆节。奸谋虽起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365750_comment'></div>狡数自穷。诱人不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365750_comment'></div>欺天斯甚。由是忠义奋发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365750_comment'></div>凶丑就擒。虽则奴庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365750_comment'></div>何足比数。然则荒徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365750_comment'></div>亦云除恶。皆是卿等同心尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365750_comment'></div>向国输忠。能协人鬼之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365750_comment'></div>不贻戎狄之笑。朕每以嘉叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365750_comment'></div>无忘于心。所云有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365750_comment'></div>皆巳优赏。惩恶劝善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365750_comment'></div>实在于兹。夏中甚热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365750_comment'></div>卿并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365750_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　致敕伊吾军使张楚宾等,对北庭将士百姓同心尽力、一举荡平逆贼刘涣,予以嘉并。作品：《敕伊吾军使张楚宾书》<div id='poem_1365746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕伊吾军使张楚宾书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365746'>敕伊州刺史伊吾军使张楚宾。近得卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365746_comment'></div>知沙陁入界。此为刘涣凶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365746_comment'></div>处置狂疏。遂令此蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365746_comment'></div>暂有迁转。今刘涣伏法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365746_comment'></div>远近知之。计沙陁部落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365746_comment'></div>当自归本处。卿可具宣朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365746_comment'></div>以慰其心。兼与盖嘉运相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365746_comment'></div>取其稳便。丰草美水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365746_comment'></div>皆在北庭。计必思归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365746_comment'></div>从其所欲也。卿可量事安慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365746_comment'></div>仍勿催迫。处置了日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365746_comment'></div>具以状闻。夏中盛热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365746_comment'></div>卿及将士百姓已下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　命张楚宾妥善处理因刘涣狂疏而引起的沙陀部迁转问题。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　得王斛斯表,知勃律国王苏没谨忙因输诚于唐而遭贼寇侵袭,遂致敕予以慰问,并授其兄及莤领已下官荣,另有物品赏赐。作品：《敕勃律国王书》<div id='poem_1365827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕勃律国王书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365827")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365827'>敕勃律国王苏没谨忙。得王斛斯表卿所与斛斯书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365827_comment'></div>知卿忠赤输诚。闻有外贼相诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365827_comment'></div>执志无二。又闻被贼侵寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365827_comment'></div>颇亦艰虞。能自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365827", 1365827, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>支持</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365827_comment'></div>且得退散。并有杀获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365827_comment'></div>朕用嘉之。卿兄麻来兮及首领已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365827_comment'></div>各量与官赏。具如别敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365827_comment'></div>今赐物三百匹。银盂缶银盘各一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365827_comment'></div>卿及首领以下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365827_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365883_comment'></div>以嘉麦有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365883_comment'></div>陛下躬执劳事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365883_comment'></div>率先兆庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365883_comment'></div>皇太子以下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365883_comment'></div>继美圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365883_comment'></div>臣闻勤于稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365883_comment'></div>必有来麰之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365883_comment'></div>著在春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365883_comment'></div>则非他谷之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365883_comment'></div>伏惟陛下致敬宗庙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365883_comment'></div>则千亩在御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365883_comment'></div>禁园测候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365883_comment'></div>则万宇皆丰。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1365883_comment'></div>式精造物之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365883_comment'></div>人谣在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365883_comment'></div>天意可鉴。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年5月</a>　是月,又有谢敕赐麦面状。作品：《谢敕赐麦面状》<div id='poem_1365896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_26_1365896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年6月</a>　六月,护密国王真檀还蕃之际,九龄敕其宜扬国命、慰抚远人,善讨突骑施,力保西陲安全,张守珪大破契丹后,九龄有贺状。作品：《敕护密国王书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年6月</a>　六月,护密国王真檀还蕃之际,九龄敕其宜扬国命、慰抚远人,善讨突骑施,力保西陲安全,张守珪大破契丹后,九龄有择日告庙敕。作品：《择日告庙敕》<div id='poem_1365741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕择日告庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365741")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365741'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365741'>敕。边境为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365741_comment'></div>莫甚于林胡。朝廷是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365741_comment'></div>几烦于将帅。车徒屡出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365741_comment'></div>刍粟载劳。使燕赵黎氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365741_comment'></div>略无宁岁。而山戎种落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365741_comment'></div>常为匪人。近有野心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365741_comment'></div>穷而归我。曾是怀附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365741_comment'></div>每所抚柔。而不变鸮音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365741_comment'></div>辄为兽搏。幽州节度使副大使张守圭等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365741_comment'></div>乘閒电发。表里奋讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365741_comment'></div>积年逋逃。一朝剪灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365741_comment'></div>则东北之祲。便以廓清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365741_comment'></div>河朔之人。差宽征戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365741_comment'></div>此皆上凭九庙之略。下仗群帅之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365741_comment'></div>今其凯旋。敢不以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365741_comment'></div>宜择吉日告九庙。所司准式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365741_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365741_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　因薛王李业染疾不愈,玄宗为之忧虑而改容发,九龄请将此状宜付史馆。作品：《薛王有疾上忧变容发请付史馆》<div id='poem_1365853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辥王有疾上忧变容发请宣付史馆状</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365853")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365853'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365853'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365853_comment'></div>臣等伏见邠王守礼等表并答制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365853_comment'></div>以辥王业有疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365853_comment'></div>圣情轸虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365853_comment'></div>宿夕之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365853_comment'></div>容发遂变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365853_comment'></div>又寻绎致倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365853_comment'></div>假寝通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365853_comment'></div>因获异方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365853_comment'></div>顿解危惙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365853_comment'></div>诚陛下友爱之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365853_comment'></div>冠于皇王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365853_comment'></div>急难之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365853_comment'></div>达于神道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365853_comment'></div>所以诸王陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365853_comment'></div>愿书竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365853_comment'></div>然犹让此归美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365853_comment'></div>推而不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365853_comment'></div>圣德谦冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365853_comment'></div>固难名于广大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365853_comment'></div>臣子之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365853_comment'></div>敢忘义于昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365853_comment'></div>况臣等近侍轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365853_comment'></div>倍百恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365853_comment'></div>望以邠王等状宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365853_comment'></div>谨录状奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365853_comment'></div>伏听敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1365853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年7月</a>　七月初,因薛王李业卒,玄宗悲而损膳,九龄奏请复膳。作品：《薛王薨上损膳请复膳状》<div id='poem_1365854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辥王薨上损膳请复膳状</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365854")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365854'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365854'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365854_comment'></div>未经旬时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365854_comment'></div>惨恤相次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365854_comment'></div>圣情友爱之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365854_comment'></div>属此天伦之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365854_comment'></div>伏闻寝膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365854_comment'></div>有改乎常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365854_comment'></div>臣等下情不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365854_comment'></div>夙夜惶灼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365854_comment'></div>伏愿抑损恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365854_comment'></div>冲用道心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365854_comment'></div>以承宗社之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365854_comment'></div>以慰臣庶之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365854_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365854_comment'></div>臣等不胜倍百恒情之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365854_comment'></div>谨奉状以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365854_comment'></div>死罪谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365854_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　得王斛斯表,知風宾国王示好于唐,九龄遂致敕嘉勉。作品：《敕罽宾国王书》<div id='poem_1365829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕罽宾国王书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365829")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365829'>敕罽宾国王。得四镇节度使王斛斯所翻卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365829_comment'></div>具知好意。然事在绝域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365829_comment'></div>不可预图。卿若诚心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365829_comment'></div>任彼量度。事遂之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365829_comment'></div>必有重赏。朕每于远国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365829_comment'></div>未尝有所食言。想亦知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365829_comment'></div>勿致疑也。秋初尚热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365829_comment'></div>卿及首领以下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365829_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365829_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　新罗国使者金信忠还归之际,九龄致敕金兴光国王,对年来两国协谋共讨渤海之事多加赞赏,并对金志廉等使者不幸染疾殂逝深表悼惜。作品：《敕新罗王金兴光书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年7月25日</a>　此日,受遣充河南开稻田使,教河南数州种水稻,以广屯田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年8月</a>　八月,九齡受遣于许、豫、陈、亳等州置水屯闭。返往之间仍频理朝务。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　西南蛮大首领蒙归义等来朝贡,还蕃之际,九龄敕其凡事有预,保境安民。作品：《敕西南蛮大首领》（之一）<div id='poem_1365831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕西南蛮大首领蒙归义书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365831")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365831'>敕西南蛮大帅特进蒙归义及诸酋首领等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365831_comment'></div>卿近在边境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365831_comment'></div>不比诸蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365831_comment'></div>率种归诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365831_comment'></div>累代如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365831_comment'></div>况卿等更效忠赤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365831_comment'></div>朕甚知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365831_comment'></div>顷者诸酋之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365831_comment'></div>或有携贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365831_comment'></div>相率自讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365831_comment'></div>恶党悉除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365831_comment'></div>即日蕃中应且安帖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365831_comment'></div>然则地临外境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365831_comment'></div>亦须有预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365831_comment'></div>人无远虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365831_comment'></div>必有近忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365831_comment'></div>卿可思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365831_comment'></div>岂虚语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365831_comment'></div>所有蕃中事意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365831_comment'></div>使者具知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365831_comment'></div>比秋凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365831_comment'></div>卿及百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365831_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1365831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　与此同时,又致敕安南首领蠹仁哲等。作品：《敕安南首领蠹仁哲书》<div id='poem_1365835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕安南首领爨仁哲等书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365835")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365835'>敕安南首领岿州刺史爨仁哲潘州刺史潘明威獠子首领阿迪和蛮大鬼主孟谷误姚州首领左威卫将军爨彦徵将军昆州刺史爨嗣绍黎州刺史爨曾戎州首领右监门卫大将军南州刺史爨归王南宁州司马威州刺史都大鬼主爨崇道升麻县令孟耽卿等。虽在僻远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365835_comment'></div>各有部落。俱属国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365835_comment'></div>并识王化。比者时有背叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365835_comment'></div>似是生梗。及其审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365835_comment'></div>亦有事由。或都府不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365835_comment'></div>处置有失。或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365835", 1365835, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>朋雠</span>相嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365835_comment'></div>经营损害。既无控告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365835_comment'></div>自不安宁。兵戈相防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365835_comment'></div>亦不足深怪也。然则既渐风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365835_comment'></div>亦当颇革蛮俗。有须陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365835_comment'></div>何不奏闻。蕃中事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365835_comment'></div>可具言也。今故令掖庭令安道训往彼宣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365835_comment'></div>并令口具。有不稳便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365835_comment'></div>可一一奏闻。秋中巳凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365835_comment'></div>卿及百姓并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365835_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　西南羁縻州刺史,督其革变陋俗、平安相处,并遣掖庭令安道训前往宣问、口具。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　九月,有敕突厥芯伽可汗书,对其承顺忠信,厚加赞赏,并致祝福。作品：《敕突厥芯伽可汗书》<div id='poem_1365801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕突厥苾伽可汗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365801")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365801'>敕突厥苾伽可汗。比数有信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365801_comment'></div>知彼平安。良足慰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365801_comment'></div>自为父子。情与年深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365801_comment'></div>中閒往来。亲缘义合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365801_comment'></div>虽云异域。何殊一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365801_comment'></div>边境之人。更无他虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365801_comment'></div>甚善甚善。此是儿可汗能为承顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365801_comment'></div>副朕之所亲厚。人閒恩好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365801_comment'></div>无以过之。长保此心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365801_comment'></div>终享福禄。子孙万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365801_comment'></div>岂独在今。比秋气渐冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365801_comment'></div>卿及平章事首领部落并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365801_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　往返督办水屯的旅途中,有宿淮阳亭口号诗,抒发其辛劳为国的情怀。作品：《旅宿淮阳亭口号》<div id='poem_22795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22795' class='poemTitle class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22795")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22795_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22795'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5429, "poem_allusion_22795")'>劳者歌</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22795'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22795'>日暮荒亭上，悠悠旅思多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22795'>故乡临桂水，今夜渺星河。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22795'>暗草霜华发，空亭雁影过。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22795'>兴来谁与晤，劳者自为歌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22795'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22795'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(22795)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年10月</a>　十月,有敕剑南节度使王昱书,告知其吐蕃请和、近与结约等事,并敕其柔远怀来,妥善处置翻附诸蛮事宜,固其归化之心。作品：《敕剑南节度使王昱书》<div id='poem_1365803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕剑南节度王昱书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365803")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365803'>敕剑南节度使益州长史王昱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365803_comment'></div>近得卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365803_comment'></div>知蒙归义等效命出力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365803_comment'></div>自讨西蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365803_comment'></div>彼持两端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365803_comment'></div>宜其残破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365803_comment'></div>苟非生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365803_comment'></div>定是输忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365803_comment'></div>亦卿等指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365803_comment'></div>更张远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365803_comment'></div>诸部所请朝贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365803_comment'></div>及蒙归义等立功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365803_comment'></div>并委卿料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365803_comment'></div>若合行赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365803_comment'></div>岂有不来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365803_comment'></div>时尚炎蒸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365803_comment'></div>路且修阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365803_comment'></div>邮传之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365803_comment'></div>公私可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365803_comment'></div>亦云重劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365803_comment'></div>非是有惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365803_comment'></div>想卿临事思其所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365803_comment'></div>缘蛮落初宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365803_comment'></div>当须计议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365803_comment'></div>若欲入奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365803_comment'></div>亦任暂来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365803_comment'></div>春晚极暄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365803_comment'></div>卿比如宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365803_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365803_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　是年冬,有观御制喜雪篇陈诚状。作品：《观御制喜雪篇状》<div id='poem_1365904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观御制喜雪篇陈诚状</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365904")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365904'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365904_comment'></div>臣等适见工部侍郎侍讲学士陈希烈所蒙恩赐圣制雪篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365904_comment'></div>伏以圣惟无作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365904_comment'></div>作则应天地和阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365904_comment'></div>斯之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365904_comment'></div>言微利溥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365904_comment'></div>旨远思深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365904_comment'></div>于彼苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365904_comment'></div>焉知帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365904_comment'></div>臣闻食者万姓之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365904_comment'></div>雪为五谷之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365904_comment'></div>兆且见于祈年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365904_comment'></div>律既和于言志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365904_comment'></div>圣心昭感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365904_comment'></div>天瑞合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365904_comment'></div>岂比夫汉咏白云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365904_comment'></div>但嗟欢乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365904_comment'></div>周歌黄竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365904_comment'></div>徒事巡游而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365904_comment'></div>臣等仰望昭回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365904_comment'></div>莫知远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365904_comment'></div>幸均生植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365904_comment'></div>同是沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365904_comment'></div>况臣忝在枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365904_comment'></div>无能翼亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365904_comment'></div>闻罪巳之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365904_comment'></div>若寘冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365904_comment'></div>循忘躯之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365904_comment'></div>冀益涓尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365904_comment'></div>伏诵圣文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365904_comment'></div>无任喜惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365904_comment'></div>臣等诚欢诚恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365904_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1365904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　冬有谢赐御书喜雪篇状。作品：《谢赐御书喜雪篇状》<div id='poem_1365905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐御书喜雪篇状</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365905")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365905'>右。臣前伏见圣制喜雪篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365905_comment'></div>奉状称庆。已特蒙赐本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365905_comment'></div>今日高力士又宣赐臣林甫臣某各一本。丽天之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365905_comment'></div>或冀传诵。垂露之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365905_comment'></div>难有偏沾。则不知元造曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365905_comment'></div>宸豪俯逮。鸾凤斯降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365905_comment'></div>云雨载均。愚臣何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365905_comment'></div>叨此殊赐。是知君臣之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365905_comment'></div>义感不一。子孙之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365905_comment'></div>传宝无穷。而未知此生何以上答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365905_comment'></div>臣等不胜感戴。伏望许臣等进食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365905_comment'></div>以申微诚。虽萐每摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365905_comment'></div>而野芹徒献。岂云尧禹之膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365905_comment'></div>冀达臣子之情。幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365905_comment'></div>谨奉状以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365905_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　又应太仆卿判梁州持节河西节度使兼陇右群牧都使支度营田使、陇右采访处置使摄御史大夫牛仙客之请托,为其父牛意撰碑铭。作品：《大唐赠使持节泾州诸军事泾州刺史牛公碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1365941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐赠使持节泾州诸军事泾州刺史牛公碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365941")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365941_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365941'>夫志道莫先于无欲。福善莫大于有后。始而晦迹。终不近名。非道德之合欤。生我劳臣。立于远绩。非善庆所致欤。所谓伊人。其在牛公者矣。公讳意。字某。其先子姓。实始殷后。有牛父者。则宋之大夫。允裔蕃衍。人物更盛。邯为护羌校尉。崇为陇西主簿。遂家陇上。是称冠族。其后因官安定。爰处鹑觚。今为郡人。亦既重代矣。公之族祖。有奇章公者。隋室宗臣。风流笃厚。典章损益。百代可知。天下称之。地灵斯在。大父通。秉志高尚。守道不携。当时交辟。辞疾不起。父会。弱龄早代。有才无禄。公夙遘闵凶。终鲜兄弟。性具纯至。孝思罔极。幼以孑立。志不违邦。与道为徒。求仁自我。不屑轩冕。考槃丘园。虽云屡空。晏如也。六郡自古五方杂错。负力怙利。上气好武。人庶相放。风俗不纯。及公冲和。其返真朴。外以义行格物。内以默致颐神。不饰智以惊愚。不弃同而即异。有恒其德。无斁于人。邻落为之变风。狼戾以之率化。公既浮云不义。介石惟一。或劝之仕。但笑而不言。飞鸿冥冥。胡可量也。开元六年。随子西征。以就色养。春秋高矣。道茂年衰。魂气其归。贤达共尽。越五月。寝疾终于伏羌之官舍。时年七十有六。冬十一月。归葬于北原。夫人同郡王氏。不享偕老。先是即代。母仪妇德。宋子齐姜。自归于我。宜尔家室。不有配德。曷生此子。有子仙客。为国之良。用商君耕战之图。修充国羌胡之具。出言可复。所计而然。边捍长城。主恩前席。且以子贵之义。有加父存之礼。元泽下逮。素风激扬。阴德所流。大福斯至。十八年。有诏赠泾州长史。二十二年冬。且有后命。赠使持节泾州诸军事泾州刺史。夫人追封太原郡夫人。于戏。存而累仁。没有馀烈。福自昭于元体。道非冀于异时。及其影响同符。宠光如答。虽松楸巳拱。而章绂载华。死如可作。无异会稽之节。生苟为耻。安用雁门之肉。贵与不贵。可不然乎。嗣子银青光禄大夫太仆卿判凉州持节河西节度使兼陇西群牧都使支度营田使陇右采访处置使摄御史大夫陇西县开国子仙客。叩心追远。号天莫逮。以为先美盖阙。后嗣有愧。且泽漏幽壤。得不铭恩。名典本州。岂徒锡羡而巳。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365941'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365941'>陇上多豪，山西好武。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365941'>使君贞独，幼不斯取。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365941'>惟道为徒，与代立矩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365941'>善有馀庆，风亦变古。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365941'>不学而知，不行而至。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365941'>迹有相混，名无自异。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365941'>出入百年，终始一意。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365941'>福流于后，神明其事。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365941'>行止于身，用存元体。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365941'>厥子嘉绩，中朝缛礼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1365941'>邙回垄隧，门重旌棨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365941'>逸人之墓，今同郡邸。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365941'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年11月</a>　十一月,有敕日本国王书,对遣唐使广成等遭遇海难、有国难回深表疚怀,并表示将尽力救遣其幸存者。作品：《敕日本国王书》<div id='poem_1365830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕日本国王书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365830")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365830'>敕日本国王王明乐美御德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365830_comment'></div>彼礼义之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365830_comment'></div>神灵所扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365830_comment'></div>沧溟往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365830_comment'></div>未尝为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365830_comment'></div>不知去岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365830_comment'></div>何负幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365830_comment'></div>丹墀真人广成等入朝东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365830_comment'></div>初出江口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365830_comment'></div>云雾斗暗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365830_comment'></div>所向迷方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365830_comment'></div>俄遭恶风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365830_comment'></div>诸船飘荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365830_comment'></div>其后一船在越州界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365830_comment'></div>其真人广成寻已发归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365830_comment'></div>计当至国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365830_comment'></div>一船飘入南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365830_comment'></div>即朝臣名代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365830_comment'></div>艰虞备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365830_comment'></div>性命仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365830_comment'></div>名代未发之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365830_comment'></div>又得广州表奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365830_comment'></div>朝臣广成等飘至林邑国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365830_comment'></div>既在异国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365830_comment'></div>言语不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365830_comment'></div>并被劫掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365830_comment'></div>或杀或卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365830_comment'></div>言念灾患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365830_comment'></div>所不忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365830_comment'></div>然则林邑诸国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365830_comment'></div>比常朝贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365830_comment'></div>朕已敕安南都护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365830_comment'></div>令宣敕告示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365830_comment'></div>见在者令其送来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365830_comment'></div>待至之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365830_comment'></div>当存抚发遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365830_comment'></div>又一船不知所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365830_comment'></div>永用疚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365830_comment'></div>或已达彼蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365830_comment'></div>有来人可具奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365830_comment'></div>此等灾变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365830_comment'></div>良不可测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365830_comment'></div>卿等忠信则尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365830_comment'></div>何负神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365830_comment'></div>而使彼行人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365830_comment'></div>罹此凶害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365830_comment'></div>想卿闻此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365830_comment'></div>当用惊嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365830_comment'></div>然天壤悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365830_comment'></div>各有命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365830_comment'></div>中冬甚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365830_comment'></div>卿及首领百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365830_comment'></div>今朝臣名代还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365830_comment'></div>一一口具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365830_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1365830_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年12月</a>　十二月,契丹王可突干率部请降,九龄致敕施以训诫和安抚。作品：《敕契丹王据埒可突干等书》《敕奚契丹并自离二廓清有期状》<div id='poem_1365760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕契丹王据埒可突于等书</a><span class='authorDate'>（734年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365760")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365760'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365760'>敕契丹王据埒及衙官可突于蜀活刺史郁捷等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365760_comment'></div>顺道则吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365760_comment'></div>惟智能图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365760_comment'></div>逆节即凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365760_comment'></div>岂愚所觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365760_comment'></div>如卿顷年背诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365760_comment'></div>实养祸胎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365760_comment'></div>今而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365760_comment'></div>亦犹未晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365760_comment'></div>因是转灾为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365760_comment'></div>因败而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365760_comment'></div>去百死之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365760_comment'></div>保万全之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365760_comment'></div>则昔者之去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365760_comment'></div>何其悖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365760_comment'></div>今兹复来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365760_comment'></div>又何智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365760_comment'></div>皆是卿素有筹略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365760_comment'></div>本于忠诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365760_comment'></div>率先种人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365760_comment'></div>拔于死地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365760_comment'></div>自尔之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365760_comment'></div>更有何忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365760_comment'></div>朕于诸蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365760_comment'></div>未尝负约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365760_comment'></div>况于卿等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365760_comment'></div>更有旧恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365760_comment'></div>闻卿此来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365760_comment'></div>豁然慰意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365760_comment'></div>一则兵革都息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365760_comment'></div>二则君臣如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365760_comment'></div>百姓之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365760_comment'></div>不失耕种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365760_comment'></div>丰草美水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365760_comment'></div>畜牧随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365760_comment'></div>更无外虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365760_comment'></div>且知上策。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1365760_comment'></div>保此永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365760_comment'></div>一无他虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365760_comment'></div>在卿所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365760_comment'></div>何假朕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365760_comment'></div>部落初归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365760_comment'></div>应须安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365760_comment'></div>可与守圭审定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365760_comment'></div>务依蕃部所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365760_comment'></div>想其沃饶之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365760_comment'></div>适彼寒暑之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365760_comment'></div>无令下人有所不惬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365760_comment'></div>冬末寒甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365760_comment'></div>卿与衙官军吏刺史已下及部落百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365760_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1365760_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　又致敕护密国王真檀,对其忠赤保国、抗御敌寇的举动甚为嘉叹,并表问候。作品：《敕护密国王书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　贺上仙公主灵应状疑亦上于本年，姑系于此。作品：《贺上仙公主灵应状》<div id='poem_1365889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365889' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365889'>右。臣等伏承今月八日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365889_comment'></div>上仙公主灵座有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365889", 1365889, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>祥风</span>瑞虹之应。爰至启殡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365889_comment'></div>乃知尸解。又承特禀清虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365889_comment'></div>薄于滋味。素含真气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365889_comment'></div>自不食盐。洎于迁神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365889_comment'></div>更标奇迹。伏惟圣系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365889_comment'></div>本于道源。妙有所钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365889_comment'></div>灵异必降。不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365889_comment'></div>何得幼而能悟。性与非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365889_comment'></div>适来以时。且契于元运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365889_comment'></div>超然而蜕。复升于丹箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365889_comment'></div>杳冥虽远。髣像如存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365889_comment'></div>则知仙路有归。慈念已释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365889_comment'></div>理绝今古。事昭闻见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365889_comment'></div>况臣等亲侍轩墀。幸闻仙解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365889_comment'></div>无任感慰之至。伏望宣付史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365889_comment'></div>以昭灵异。仍望宣示百官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365889_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1365889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年1月</a>　为中书令。正月,有贺诛奚贼可突干状。作品：《贺诛奚贼可突干状》<div id='poem_1365867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365867'>右。高力士宣示张守圭所上逆贼契丹屈烈及可突于等首级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365867_comment'></div>此等恶稔。丧败将及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365867_comment'></div>故天诱其衷。既降又贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365867_comment'></div>而感义之士。恶其翻覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365867_comment'></div>背恩之贼。已就诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365867_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365867", 1365867, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>幽障</span>廓清。华夷俱静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365867_comment'></div>计其馀噍。永无动摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365867_comment'></div>陛下边任先择。圣谋独断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365867_comment'></div>克禀成命。树此戎功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365867_comment'></div>且知河朔无转输之劳。林胡为赋税之地。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年1月</a>　正月,有敕契丹知兵马中郎李过折书。作品：《敕契丹知兵马中郎李过折书》<div id='poem_1365800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365800' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365800_comment'></div>已知才略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365800_comment'></div>一此行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365800_comment'></div>十倍所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365800_comment'></div>既立殊勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365800_comment'></div>又成大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365800_comment'></div>何其壮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365800_comment'></div>可突于狡算翻覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365800_comment'></div>人面兽心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365800_comment'></div>事其酋长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365800_comment'></div>不忠不义。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365800_comment'></div>专持两端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365800_comment'></div>随事向背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365800_comment'></div>而屈烈愚蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365800_comment'></div>与之同恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365800_comment'></div>卿比观变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365800_comment'></div>实为远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365800_comment'></div>诛元凶而存一蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365800_comment'></div>行权宜而合正道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365800_comment'></div>所全者大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365800_comment'></div>所虑实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365800_comment'></div>今诸部怗然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365800_comment'></div>皆卿之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365800_comment'></div>且顷者携叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365800_comment'></div>又甚崎岖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365800_comment'></div>羊马不保于孳生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365800_comment'></div>田畴不安于耕种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365800_comment'></div>寄命山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365800_comment'></div>并力干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365800_comment'></div>总由顽凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365800_comment'></div>致此劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365800_comment'></div>向若无卿此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365800_comment'></div>信彼所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365800_comment'></div>以疲弊之残人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365800_comment'></div>当骁雄之巨众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365800_comment'></div>彼则朝夕奔命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365800_comment'></div>此方岁月攻守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365800_comment'></div>而众寡不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365800_comment'></div>歼灭有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365800_comment'></div>赖卿先见之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365800_comment'></div>遽为转祸之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365800_comment'></div>以救万人之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365800_comment'></div>以成万代之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365800_comment'></div>岂独大功。<div id='poem_sentence_48_1365800_comment'></div>异姓封王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365800_comment'></div>以旌厥庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365800_comment'></div>且有后命。<div id='poem_sentence_53_1365800_comment'></div>百姓既知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365800_comment'></div>想当安怗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365800_comment'></div>卿可与张守圭量事处置。<div id='poem_sentence_58_1365800_comment'></div>爱同赤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365800_comment'></div>惟其所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365800_comment'></div>随事抚存。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　奉撰籍田之制。作品：《籍田制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　奉撰籍田赦书。作品：《籍田赦书》<div id='poem_1365840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>藉田赦书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365840")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365840'>门下。昔者受命为君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365840_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365840", 1365840, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>体元立极</span>。未有不谨于礼而能见教于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365840_comment'></div>朕其庶乎有惭作者。方册存而可举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365840_comment'></div>旧章绝而复寻。自古所行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365840_comment'></div>无一而废。将以上乞灵于宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365840_comment'></div>下蒙福于黎元。朕兹精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365840_comment'></div>天实降鉴。今嗣岁初吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365840_comment'></div>农事将起。礼有先于耕藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365840_comment'></div>义缘奉于粢盛。是所严祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365840_comment'></div>敢不敬事。故躬载耒耜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365840_comment'></div>亲率公卿。以先万姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365840_comment'></div>遂终千亩。谓敦本之为小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365840_comment'></div>何布泽之更深。宜有顺于发生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365840_comment'></div>俾无偏于行惠。可大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365840_comment'></div>自开元二十三年正月十八日昧爽已前。大辟罪无轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365840_comment'></div>已发觉未发觉。已结正未结正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365840_comment'></div>系囚见徒。咸赦除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365840_comment'></div>其犯十恶死罪。不在赦限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365840_comment'></div>自馀死罪。特宜配流岭南远恶处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365840_comment'></div>官典犯赃本犯。至死贬与岭南远恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365840_comment'></div>左降官至流者亦量贬与远。官典配诸军效力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365840_comment'></div>计赃至徒。仍不得重令却上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365840_comment'></div>天下诸州。损免处地税先矜放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365840_comment'></div>其非损免处。有贫乏未纳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365840_comment'></div>并一切放免。京兆河南府秦州百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365840_comment'></div>有诸色勾徵。及逋悬欠负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365840_comment'></div>亦宜放免。其在官典及仓督等腹内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365840_comment'></div>不在免限。天下色役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365840_comment'></div>爰及支用。务令节减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365840_comment'></div>并诸州贡赋。先令中书门下均融减省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365840_comment'></div>宜准前敕。速即条奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365840_comment'></div>损免州税户钱未纳。并七等已上户租先未处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365840_comment'></div>及五色资钱课未纳。灼然不辨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365840_comment'></div>并放至蚕麦秋收已来赎纳。损免州逃兵健儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365840_comment'></div>承前访捉不获。合取籍人充替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365840_comment'></div>自资送装送军。程期逼迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365840_comment'></div>颇亦辛苦。并放至蚕麦已后发遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365840_comment'></div>仍令所司预与军州计会。诸军征行人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365840_comment'></div>并令州县存恤。其行人有父母年七十已上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365840_comment'></div>委本道采访使检责取实。牒报本军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365840_comment'></div>即放还本贯。军司据阙数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365840_comment'></div>募取健儿充替。行人及防丁有身亡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365840_comment'></div>为造棺榇。递还本处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365840_comment'></div>诸州应发遣防丁。去本贯一千里已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365840_comment'></div>比来除正课之外。给一丁充资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365840_comment'></div>多不济办。宜更量与资助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365840_comment'></div>两京城内今年所有诸杂夫役。并宜免放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365840_comment'></div>应须使役。以诸色钱和雇取充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365840_comment'></div>农桑是时。不得妨夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365840_comment'></div>州县长官。倍加劝课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365840_comment'></div>孝子顺孙。义夫节妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365840_comment'></div>旌表门闾。𩻴寡茕独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365840_comment'></div>不能自存。量加优恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365840_comment'></div>天下侍老。百岁已上版授上州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365840_comment'></div>九十中州刺史。七十已上上州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365840_comment'></div>其九十以上。所由仍量给酒肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365840_comment'></div>各令存问。亚献皇太子鸿赐物二千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365840_comment'></div>终献庆王潭赐物一千匹。邠王守礼等各赐物一千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365840_comment'></div>忠王浚已下各赐物三百匹。夹侍正衣进圭捧圭汝阳郡王淳等各赐物二百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365840_comment'></div>皇太子夹侍正衣等各赐物一百匹。裴耀卿张九龄李林甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365840_comment'></div>自其翊赞。诚有忠益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365840_comment'></div>颁赏以序。等数须优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365840_comment'></div>宜与一子官。仍各赐物三百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365840_comment'></div>二王后各赐物一百匹。长公主公主各与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365840_comment'></div>仍各赐物二百匹。嗣王郡主县主各赐物一百五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365840_comment'></div>在京文武官见任及致仕。并诸色陪位官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365840_comment'></div>一品赐物八十匹。二品七十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365840_comment'></div>三品六十匹。四品五十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365840_comment'></div>五品四十匹。七品六品三十段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365840_comment'></div>八品九品二十段。节度使副大使三都留守京兆尹各一百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365840_comment'></div>四大都督府长史诸道采访使各八十匹。诸赐物应两给者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365840_comment'></div>从一处给。其耕官及侍耕官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365840_comment'></div>各赐勋两转。丞相萧嵩与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365840_comment'></div>仍赐物二百匹。摄九卿诸侯等各与一子出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365840_comment'></div>仍各赐物一百五十匹。侍耕执牛官各赐物一百二十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365840_comment'></div>升坛行事官修礼仪官及刺史判官等。更赐一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365840_comment'></div>应入三品及五品官阶相当。减四考听入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365840_comment'></div>摄司徒信安郡王祎。礼仪官韦绦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365840_comment'></div>既不叙阶。祎与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365840_comment'></div>赐物二百匹。绦与一子出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365840_comment'></div>赐物一百五十匹。其升坛及修礼仪两兼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365840_comment'></div>从一加阶。应与一子官及出身者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365840_comment'></div>若无子。听回与周亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365840_comment'></div>供奉及押阶不升坛。并坛下行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365840_comment'></div>及助耕勒牛官。别敕差中书门下差定人等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365840_comment'></div>泛阶合入三品五品官阶至考未定者。待考定日听叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365840_comment'></div>非待考者赐勋四转。未承别赐者各赐一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365840_comment'></div>知顿使赐物一百匹。修坛场长官屯官撰玉册文官各赐物八十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365840_comment'></div>书玉册官赐物五十匹。管藉田县令赐物六十匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365840_comment'></div>在东京文武官朝集使外官充十道采访使。并判官诸道节度副大使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365840_comment'></div>并诸方通表使诸敕使判官。新除五品已上官未赴任都城畿县令见陪位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365840_comment'></div>三品以上转爵一级。四品已下进一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365840_comment'></div>皇亲诸亲及九庙子孙不入等陪位者。并外文武官九品已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365840_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。诸蕃入朝及贺正蕃客应陪位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365840_comment'></div>共赐物五十匹。节级分付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365840_comment'></div>南北衙行从宿卫斋宫者。及文武官押当有职掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365840_comment'></div>并诸色杂职掌。并应耕公卿从官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365840_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。万骑及飞骑见当上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365840_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。其宿卫斋宫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365840_comment'></div>加赐物三段。仗内坊侍诸色行从人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365840_comment'></div>各赐物三段。彍骑番兵角弓手弩手官马主见当番。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365840_comment'></div>及留帖人掌闲幕士驾士供膳习驭工人乐人见当上有职掌。并庶人应耕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365840_comment'></div>各赐物三段。斋郎礼生赞者行事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365840_comment'></div>并减两年劳。无劳可减者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365840_comment'></div>斋郎放出身。礼生赞者选口稍优与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365840_comment'></div>三卫七色见当番。并流外行署及蕃官见上有职掌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365840_comment'></div>各转一勋。河南洛阳县陪位父老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365840_comment'></div>各赐物五段。近坛百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365840_comment'></div>各免今年杂差科。宗庙致享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365840_comment'></div>务在丰洁。礼经沿革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365840_comment'></div>必本人情。笾豆之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365840_comment'></div>或未能备物。服制之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365840_comment'></div>或有所未通。宜令礼官学士详议具奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365840_comment'></div>朕自临天下。二纪于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365840_comment'></div>不敢荒宁。日加兢业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365840_comment'></div>而灾眚未弭。黎人未康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365840_comment'></div>若有由而然。则在予之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365840_comment'></div>有能直言极谏者。具以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365840_comment'></div>每渴贤良。无忘鉴寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365840_comment'></div>顷虽虚伫。未副旁求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365840_comment'></div>其才有王霸之略。学究天人之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365840_comment'></div>智勇堪将帅之选。政能当牧宰之举者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365840_comment'></div>五品已上清官将军都督刺史各举一人。孝悌力田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365840_comment'></div>乡闾推挹者。本州长官勘实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365840_comment'></div>有才堪应务者。各以名闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365840_comment'></div>致仕官久历清资。始终称著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365840_comment'></div>年渐衰迈。情有可矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365840_comment'></div>量与改职。依前致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365840_comment'></div>宗子中有才行著闻。比尚沈屈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365840_comment'></div>委宗正勘实奏闻。唐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>元年两营立功官任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365840_comment'></div>折冲并改与郎将。郎将改与中郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365840_comment'></div>其亡官失爵。量加收叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365840_comment'></div>五岳四渎。名山大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365840_comment'></div>及自古圣帝明王。忠臣良相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365840_comment'></div>并令所在长官以礼致祭。赦书有所未该者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365840_comment'></div>所司比类奏闻。亡命山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365840_comment'></div>挟藏军器。百日不首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365840_comment'></div>复罪如初。敢以赦前事相告言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365840_comment'></div>以其罪罪之。都城内赐酺三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365840_comment'></div>赦书日行五百里。布告遐迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365840_comment'></div>咸使知闻。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365840_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_141_1365840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1365840'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_129_1365840_0'>⑴ 此处隆字避玄宗讳</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1365840_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　籍田礼毕,适降瑞雪,有贺雪状。作品：《贺雪状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　突厥苾伽可汗逝后,登里(又作“利”)继位,九龄奉拟敕突厥可汗书,对苾伽可汗表示痛悼,并对儿可汗登里重申父子之情。作品：《敕突厥可汗书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　玄宗从叔金吾大将军李佺奉命持节前往突厥吊祭兼营护葬事之际,九龄又奉拟敕突厥登利可汗书一封,表示了要为苾伽可汗建碑立庙、贻范纪功之厚意。作品：《敕突厥登利可汗书》<div id='poem_1365804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕突厥登利可汗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365804")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365804'>敕突厥登利可汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365804_comment'></div>日月流迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365804_comment'></div>将逼葬期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365804_comment'></div>悲慕之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365804_comment'></div>何可堪处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365804_comment'></div>朕以父子之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365804_comment'></div>情与年深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365804_comment'></div>及闻宅兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365804_comment'></div>良以追悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365804_comment'></div>前哥利施颉斤至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365804_comment'></div>所请葬料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365804_comment'></div>事事不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365804_comment'></div>所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365804_comment'></div>将答忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365804_comment'></div>故丧纪之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365804_comment'></div>礼物有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365804_comment'></div>道之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365804_comment'></div>地亦何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365804_comment'></div>今又遣从叔金吾大将军佺持节吊祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365804_comment'></div>兼营护葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365804_comment'></div>佺宗室之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365804_comment'></div>信行所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365804_comment'></div>欲达其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365804_comment'></div>必重其使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365804_comment'></div>以将厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365804_comment'></div>更敦前约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365804_comment'></div>且以为保忠信者可以示子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365804_comment'></div>息兵革者可以训疆场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365804_comment'></div>故遣建碑立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365804_comment'></div>贻范纪功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365804_comment'></div>因命史官正辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365804_comment'></div>朕亦亲为篆写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365804_comment'></div>以固终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365804_comment'></div>想体至怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365804_comment'></div>春初尚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365804_comment'></div>可汗及平章事部落并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365804_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1365804_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　御史大夫李尚隐、太府卿裴伷先因不礼中官,触忤上旨,全赖九龄之庇护而未遭贬斥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　谏相张守珪,反对以名器假人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年2月</a>　二月,因奚、契丹既平,九龄有陈请,欲为东北将吏刊石勒
颂,以纪功德。作品：《请东北将吏刊石
纪功德状》<div id='poem_1365860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请东北将刊石纪功德状</a><span id='poem_sentence_4_1365860_comment'></div>惟欲防御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365860_comment'></div>所谓长策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365860_comment'></div>无出此者。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365860_comment'></div>一举遂平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365860_comment'></div>使迁善者自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365860_comment'></div>为恶者就戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365860_comment'></div>事若不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365860_comment'></div>无息我人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365860_comment'></div>高深未测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365860_comment'></div>及闻凯捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365860_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1365860", 1365860, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>晷候</span>不差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365860_comment'></div>而两蕃遗噍。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365860_comment'></div>卧鼓灭烽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365860_comment'></div>诚自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365860_comment'></div>斯皆陛下睿谋先定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365860_comment'></div>神武非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365860_comment'></div>观变早于<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1365860", 1365860, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>无象</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365860_comment'></div>伏以成功不宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365860_comment'></div>复纪何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365860_comment'></div>请具状宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365860_comment'></div>垂示将来。<div id='poem_sentence_55_1365860_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1365860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　张守珪诣东都献捷,玄宗赋诗宠之,并诏于幽州立碑,以纪其功。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　九龄奉撰开元功德颂。作品：《开元纪功德颂并序》<div id='poem_1365716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开元纪功德颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365716")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365716_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365716'>臣闻蛮夷猾夏。唐虞已然。天之所生。类不可绝。尝有拓境者矣。而固也为患。或有款塞者矣。而必也无亲。是以古之哲王。审其若此。则限以荒服。断非纯臣。不贡不王。武功居后。不庭不率。文德是先。三代所以直道。百蛮所以向化。迨乎春秋之衰。诸侯以力。征伐自出。戎心大启。谋夏乱华。干盟偪好。王纲弛而若缀。天道厌而将革。则有强能攘劫。暴恶交侵。虽杂霸之无成。亦反经之所取。其负力者。乃堑山堙谷。尽境而筑长城。其黩武者。则挽粟飞刍。穷兵以耗中国。又失于下策。而悔在末年。彼王略之不恢。殆千馀载矣。夫有其馀而无豫。思其患而不图。所谓能国。将安贵圣。物岂终否。道非固穷。鉴之者昊天。救之者英主。元命阴骘。畀付神武。我太宗一戎衣而大定。我皇帝再受命而太平。不是古而务文。不非今而忘战。以时变而消息。与天元而合符。日月之所照临。阴阳之所陶冶。凡有在地。莫不禀朔。而东夏郡县。北隙山戎。先是四十年。侵轶数百里。自兹气夺。数以病告。既威攘之不詟。且力制之不可。或朝或否。为虺为蛇。幽鄣未遑以灭烽。边城安得而弛柝。旷日持久。兵连祸挐。率由事边。是无宁岁。二十二年春。乃命右羽林大将军兼御史中丞幽州长史张守圭将中军。都督诸镇。雄名先路。夷裔生风。载驰信臣。继发精卒。戒严有赫。张皇若神。公卿大夫。未始测也。将校部曲。亦莫知也。皇帝方日靖以虑之。乾纲以断之。初决策于九重。已收功于万里矣。二十二年冬十有二月。中贵将命。元戎受律。三军疾雷于不时。二庭丧胆于非意。欲遁则众溃不保。欲拒则兵锋莫当。因而伪降。幸且纾祸。遽图反覆。将肆鸱张。观衅先人。岂伊负我。以间谍而情得。乘猜携而计从。或奇兵以尝。或厚利以啖。无何变作。果自族诛。凶元恶首。鬼惑神诱。假天威而无前。覆鸟巢而何有。于是诸部大骇。率众复归。责以不义之尤。舍其不臣之罪。既服即序。有威且怀。载籍以来。固未之见也。昔我睿宗取句骊于拾遗。今兹圣谋易林胡于反掌。献功有续。后嗣无忘。百王所废之勋。四夷来宾之俗。自我底定。巍乎发皇。其若此也。于是彼节使与群帅。因东师之凯旋。离而族谈。合而公议。以为主上悯一隅之苦。垂不代之略。以计易战。以信去兵。神断自天。虏平不日。且军未血刃。敌免膏原。密承无方之谋。坐致不阵之捷。有征无战。即王者之师欤。而不彰美于吾君。得无臣子之罪。不表圣于帝载。曷称文武之时。乃率其属。至于固请。帝三让德。而曰俞哉。夫曲成万类者天。为而不有。下济兆庶者圣。成而不居。物无谢生于天。虽云至道。人无归功于圣。何以最灵。虽无巳无名。所宜绝于言象。而惟忠与义。固不废于颂述。大雅云。徐方既同。天子之功。又曰。明明天子。令闻不已。其此之谓也。臣再拜顿首。敢献颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365716'>赫赫天威兮被遐荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365716_comment'></div>蠢兹山戎兮不来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365716_comment'></div>命南仲兮整六师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365716_comment'></div>出幽陵兮躏九夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365716_comment'></div>簸赤山兮荡沧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365716_comment'></div>吊无告兮伐有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365716_comment'></div>徒不勤兮车不殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365716_comment'></div>虏震惊兮兵气倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365716_comment'></div>昔负固兮今安在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365716_comment'></div>魁自歼兮裔既平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365716_comment'></div>谋既集兮圣自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365716_comment'></div>我不战兮献戎捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365716_comment'></div>俾厥后兮扬天声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365716_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　九龄奉撰太子李鸿书颂,九龄复有谢状。作品：《谢蒙太子书颂状》<div id='poem_1365900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢蒙太子书颂状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365900'>右。昨者高力士宣恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365900_comment'></div>垂示皇太子书纪功德颂。恭览睿迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365900_comment'></div>实天人之表。幼传楷则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365900_comment'></div>训叶文明。春秋典学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365900_comment'></div>时惟多艺。鸾凤变态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365900_comment'></div>入神妙而难明。俾臣庸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365900_comment'></div>凭篆刻而不朽。微臣之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365900_comment'></div>倍百常情。无任悚戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365900_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1365900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365739'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365739'>敕幽州老人师知礼等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365739_comment'></div>比者林胡翻覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365739_comment'></div>荐岁不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365739_comment'></div>戎马之乡。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月5日</a>　三月五日加金紫光禄大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月9日</a>　九日进封始兴县开国子、食邑四百户。父弘愈追赠为太常卿、广州都督,母卢氏追赠为桂阳郡太夫人,有文祭之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月</a>　玄宗又欲起复授九皋、九章二人京官。九龄恳切辞让,得允所求。作品：《让两弟起复授官状》<div id='poem_1365907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让两弟起复授官状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365907")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365907'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365907'>右。臣昨以两弟身官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365907_comment'></div>状涉隐冒。家且未正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365907_comment'></div>焉能正人。所以陈露奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365907_comment'></div>诚欲自律。今日高力士宣敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365907_comment'></div>令与两弟京官。慈旨优柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365907_comment'></div>感深骨髓。微臣何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365907_comment'></div>叨此殊恩。但臣自罹殃罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365907_comment'></div>才踰年序。忝承重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365907_comment'></div>不敢顾私。而鞠育之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365907_comment'></div>终怀罔极。几筵在远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365907_comment'></div>奠酹不亲。惟有两弟在家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365907_comment'></div>获申情纪。今若恭承恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365907_comment'></div>尽在墨缞。何心何颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365907_comment'></div>可以偷此。陛下每宏教义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365907_comment'></div>必先名节。岂于愚臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365907_comment'></div>无少矜悯。若使九皋等获免罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365907_comment'></div>幸无削除。在臣閤门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365907_comment'></div>已沾殊泽。更令授职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365907_comment'></div>俱远哀次。于臣私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365907_comment'></div>实所不忍。然于朝议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365907_comment'></div>必有喧黩。乞寝成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365907_comment'></div>俯亮愚衷。冀无玷大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365907_comment'></div>岂敢自遂而已。不胜哀荷战惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365907_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1365907_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月</a>　擢王维为右拾遗。拟活孝子张瑝、张琇兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年3月</a>　三月底,有贺御制开元文字音义状。作品：《贺御制开元文字音义状》<div id='poem_1365885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1365885_comment'></div>义微旨远。文省理该。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365885_comment'></div>表隶以训今。存篆以徵古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365885_comment'></div>众释大备。取證于前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365885_comment'></div>片言旁通。去嫌于翻字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365885_comment'></div>信文思之精一。学术之明准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365885_comment'></div>非圣心之善诱。焉降情于豪素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365885_comment'></div>臣等忝居近侍。再忭发蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365885_comment'></div>捧戴之诚。实百<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365885", 1365885, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>恒品</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365885_comment'></div>望令集贤院更写一本。付外流行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365885_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。谨进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365885_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365885_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　朝廷得西域四镇节度使表，知吐蕃与突骑施苏禄可汗暗相交通,即刻引起警觉,九龄拟敕吐蕃赞普书,重申唐蕃姻亲和好之大义。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之一）<div id='poem_1365765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕平卢使乌知义书</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365765")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365765'>敕乌知义。两蕃既巳归我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365765_comment'></div>突厥仍敢犯边。此其不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365765_comment'></div>诚可残灭。适闻契丹及奚等并力合谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365765_comment'></div>同破凶丑。卿亦继进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365765_comment'></div>相与成功。此之一捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365765_comment'></div>使其丧气。然斗防困兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365765_comment'></div>诱备羸师。兵家之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365765_comment'></div>慎在终始。卿是宿将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365765_comment'></div>当自明之。若见可则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365765_comment'></div>务须灵敏。固在临事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365765_comment'></div>难用速言。必图万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365765_comment'></div>不可轻举。巳敕守圭与卿计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365765_comment'></div>可须观衅裁之。秋凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365765_comment'></div>卿及将士巳下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365765_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365765_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　又有敕剑南节度王昱书,命其相机处置西南诸蛮事务。作品：《敕剑南节度王昱书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　与此同时,有敕当州别驾董惩运书,对其要求袭封刺史事加以训诫。作品：《敕当州别驾董惩运书》<div id='poem_1365782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365782' class='poemTitle
