class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365782'>敕当州别驾董惩运。省所奏王昱及严正诲表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365782_comment'></div>具知所缘。卿父往在当州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365782_comment'></div>连年纵酒。既加风疢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365782_comment'></div>行事乖疏。董念封经使具论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365782_comment'></div>王昱始奏停废。皆凭实状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365782_comment'></div>不是冤诬。后自病亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365782_comment'></div>岂可怨诉。所言不直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365782_comment'></div>欲信无凭。卿久袭冠带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365782_comment'></div>复拘法式。宁不知此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365782_comment'></div>犹且有词。至于卿身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365782_comment'></div>合承刺史。比来未授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365782_comment'></div>亦则有由。闻卿少年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365782_comment'></div>未闲抚字。举州之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365782_comment'></div>从此改修。父亡子及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365782_comment'></div>终不失旧。卿表云部落据险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365782_comment'></div>几许无知。亦虑恶人因此扇诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365782_comment'></div>幸无他故。勿取破亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365782_comment'></div>今故令内使往问部落及百姓等。此事虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365782_comment'></div>还自具名状闻。比极暄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365782_comment'></div>卿及部落百姓并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365782_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1365782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　夏初,有敕当悉等州羌首领书,嘱其严勒蕃部、保境安民。作品：《敕当、悉等州羌首领书》<div id='poem_1365783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365783' id='poem_sentence_33_1365783_comment'></div>豫备恶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365783_comment'></div>寇雠纵来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365783_comment'></div>计无所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365783_comment'></div>我之深策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365783_comment'></div>岂不在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365783_comment'></div>卿等荣贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365783_comment'></div>勿忧不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365783_comment'></div>今故令王承训重宣往意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365783_comment'></div>比已热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365783_comment'></div>首领百姓等并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365783_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1365783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年5月</a>　五月,应宗子之请,奉撰龙池圣德颂并进状。作品：《龙池圣德颂》《进龙池圣德颂状》<div id='poem_1365909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进龙池圣德颂状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365909")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365909'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365909_comment'></div>先奉敕令臣撰文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365909_comment'></div>伏以天将启圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365909_comment'></div>地乃出符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365909_comment'></div>历考图箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365909_comment'></div>旷古未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365909_comment'></div>臣学术肤浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365909_comment'></div>且灵命难言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365909_comment'></div>虽已极于愚思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365909_comment'></div>曾未徵于万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365909_comment'></div>猥承恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365909_comment'></div>虚污磨砻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365909_comment'></div>以此惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365909_comment'></div>无宁启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365909_comment'></div>谨随状封进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365909_comment'></div>尘黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365909_comment'></div>伏增<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1365909", 1365909, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>战越</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　夏中,北平王、检校松漠州都督李过折被涅礼所杀,九龄有敕契丹都督涅礼书,责以道义并警示其好自为之。作品：《敕契丹都督涅礼书》<div id='poem_1365761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕契丹都督泥礼书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365761")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365761'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365761'>敕契丹都督泥礼。往者屈烈突于凶恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365761_comment'></div>无心忧矜百姓。背叛于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365761_comment'></div>终日自防。丁壮不得耕耘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365761_comment'></div>牛马不得生养。及依附突厥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365761_comment'></div>而课税又多。部落吁嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365761_comment'></div>卿所见也。李过折因众人之忿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365761_comment'></div>诛顽凶之徒。诸部酋豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365761_comment'></div>相率归我。巳令随事赏赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365761_comment'></div>亦云且得安宁。过折封王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365761_comment'></div>岂直赏功而已。亦为百姓众意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365761_comment'></div>赖其抚存。不知近日巳来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365761_comment'></div>若为非理。亦闻杀害无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365761_comment'></div>棒打又多。众情不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365761_comment'></div>遂致非命。然卿彼之蕃法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365761_comment'></div>多无义于君长。自昔如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365761_comment'></div>朕亦知之。然是卿蕃王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365761_comment'></div>有恶径杀。为此王者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365761_comment'></div>不亦难乎。但恐卿今为王后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365761_comment'></div>人亦常不自保。谁愿作王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365761_comment'></div>卿虽蕃人。是当土豪杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365761_comment'></div>亦须防虑后事。岂取快志目前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365761_comment'></div>过折既亡。卿初知都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365761_comment'></div>百姓诸处分。复得安宁以否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365761_comment'></div>张守圭先拟往彼。亦即令便就处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365761_comment'></div>卿应有官赏。即有处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365761_comment'></div>夏中甚热。卿及首领百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365761_comment'></div>今赐卿锦衣一副。并细腰带七事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365761_comment'></div>至宜领取。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365761_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　因西南边界纠纷,九龄再拟敕吐蕃赞普书,申明朝廷态度。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕吐蕃赞普书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365813")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365813'>皇帝问吐蕃赞普。近窦元礼往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365813_comment'></div>事具前书。赞普后来亦知彼意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365813_comment'></div>朕推心天下。皆合太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365813_comment'></div>况于彼蕃。复是亲娅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365813_comment'></div>仍加结约。盟誓再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365813_comment'></div>以至道言之。此亦仁义不薄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365813_comment'></div>而赞普且犹未信。复是何心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365813_comment'></div>君长大蕃。固不容易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365813_comment'></div>所云去年七月巂州将兵抄掠。兼有诈诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365813_comment'></div>巂州之外。尚隔诸蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365813_comment'></div>既背吐蕃。自行寇抄掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365813_comment'></div>而乃推托于我。何为遥信虚词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365813_comment'></div>且西南群蛮。别是一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365813_comment'></div>既不容于我。亦不专于吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365813_comment'></div>去却不追。来亦不拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365813_comment'></div>乃是两界所有。只合任其所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365813_comment'></div>自数十年来。或叛或附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365813_comment'></div>皆所亲见。岂假<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365813", 1365813, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>缕言</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365813_comment'></div>往者此蛮背恩。侵我边鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365813_comment'></div>昆明即巂州之故县。盐井乃昆明之本城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365813_comment'></div>今复旧疆。何废修筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365813_comment'></div>而云除却。是何道理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365813_comment'></div>且边境备守。彼此常事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365813_comment'></div>今既和好。何有嫌疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365813_comment'></div>至如西自葱岭已来。沿边诸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365813_comment'></div>或地势是要。或水土是好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365813_comment'></div>彼有城镇。亦皆内侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365813_comment'></div>朕既不解广求。更以自益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365813_comment'></div>缘已和好。不可细论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365813_comment'></div>且八叠山筑城置镇。皆入汉界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365813_comment'></div>何曾以此为言。而彼即生词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365813_comment'></div>未知何意。边城委任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365813_comment'></div>当择忠良。无信小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365813_comment'></div>令得閒搆。夏中已热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365813_comment'></div>赞普及平章事部落百姓并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365813_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1365813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　又有敕拓静州首领书,安抚其因处置当州董氏问题而引起的恐慌。作品：《敕拓、静州首领书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　河东节度副使王忠嗣等远经敌境，昼夜勤劳,九龄拟敕予以慰勉。作品：《敕河东节度副使王忠嗣书》《贺依圣料赤山北无贼及突厥要重人死状信安郡王祎承王忠嗣警因牒云赤山有贼》<div id='poem_1365781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕河东节度副使王忠嗣书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365781")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365781'>敕河东节度副使兼代州都督王忠嗣及诸将士等。大叔承庆至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365781_comment'></div>知卿远经贼境。昼夜勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365781_comment'></div>虽不遇凶徒。亦备尽诚效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365781_comment'></div>顷属时暑。士马远来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365781_comment'></div>行李之閒。固应疲顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365781_comment'></div>诸军将等。各须抚养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365781_comment'></div>令其宁息。行回之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365781_comment'></div>当有宴劳。宜令大同军即办宴设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365781_comment'></div>及时慰勉。夏中极热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365781_comment'></div>卿及将士已下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365781_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365781_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺依圣料赤山北无贼及突厥要重人死请宣付史馆状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365870")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365870_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1365870_0'>① 先是信安王祎承王忠嗣警因牒云赤山有贼</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365870'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365870_comment'></div>先得前件牒云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365870_comment'></div>九月三日奚探见贼无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365870_comment'></div>前三日臣等面奉圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365870_comment'></div>料此必安禄山所将之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365870_comment'></div>奚疑是贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365870_comment'></div>便有此牒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365870_comment'></div>臣等当时又奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365870_comment'></div>突厥举国大来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365870_comment'></div>微有输失便去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365870_comment'></div>窃料此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365870_comment'></div>恐其有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365870_comment'></div>陛下又云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365870_comment'></div>必应彼有要重人死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365870_comment'></div>所以即去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365870_comment'></div>今日幽州节度判官监察御史张晓至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365870_comment'></div>云今月十一日从幽州发来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365870_comment'></div>赤山元自无贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365870_comment'></div>奚所见者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365870_comment'></div>正是安禄山下兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365870_comment'></div>又云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365870_comment'></div>契丹有蕃落人走来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365870_comment'></div>云突厥之兵马平章事第一人死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365870_comment'></div>所以狼狈即去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365870_comment'></div>在路每日于帐衙前哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365870_comment'></div>此并圣心悬照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365870_comment'></div>有如目击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365870_comment'></div>臣等亲奉睿算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365870_comment'></div>及此符同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365870_comment'></div>万里无差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365870_comment'></div>不胜惊喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365870_comment'></div>无任踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365870_comment'></div>仍望宣付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1365870_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　秋初,有敕幽州节度张守珪书,命其稳扎稳打,并代为宣示朝旨,安抚涅礼。作品：《敕幽州节度张守珪书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕幽州节度张守圭书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365762")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365762'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365762'>敕幽州节度副大使兼御史大夫张守圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365762_comment'></div>近有降人云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365762_comment'></div>虏骑东下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365762_comment'></div>其数稍众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365762_comment'></div>固宜有以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365762_comment'></div>仍闻两蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365762_comment'></div>亦有应接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365762_comment'></div>当是妄语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365762_comment'></div>终须审观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365762_comment'></div>若保无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365762_comment'></div>便可信任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365762_comment'></div>至于兵马权略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365762_comment'></div>决在一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365762_comment'></div>卿自审量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365762_comment'></div>不可悬料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365762_comment'></div>然虏骑驰突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365762_comment'></div>难与争锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365762_comment'></div>会是乘其气衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365762_comment'></div>然后邀击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365762_comment'></div>一战取灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365762_comment'></div>或在此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365762_comment'></div>顷者泥礼自擅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365762_comment'></div>虽以义责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365762_comment'></div>而未有名位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365762_comment'></div>恐其不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365762_comment'></div>卿可宣示朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365762_comment'></div>使知无他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365762_comment'></div>并便处置讫奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365762_comment'></div>朕当即有处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365762_comment'></div>比秋热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365762_comment'></div>卿及将士已下并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365762_comment'></div>今令赵惠琮一一口具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365762_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1365762_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　边使范正颜带回吐蕃操持两端、意欲边地生事之信息,九龄有敕陇右节度使阴承本书,嘱其严加备守,不得先举。作品：《敕陇右节度阴承本书》<div id='poem_1365785' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365785' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365785?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕陇右节度阴承本书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365785")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365785_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365785'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365785'>敕陇右节度使阴承本。使人范正颜至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365785_comment'></div>省表具知。朕于吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365785_comment'></div>恩信不失。彼心有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365785_comment'></div>操持两端。阴结突骑施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365785_comment'></div>密相来往。事既丑露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365785_comment'></div>却以怨尤。乃云姚巂用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365785_comment'></div>取其城堡。略观此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365785_comment'></div>必欲为恶。必不得先举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365785_comment'></div>但须严备。远加斥堠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365785_comment'></div>察其动静。若形兆已见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365785_comment'></div>驰状以闻。诸处军城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365785_comment'></div>数加戒敕。若不称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365785_comment'></div>速须改换。今年交兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365785_comment'></div>新到陇右。未经戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365785_comment'></div>大须<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365785", 1365785, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>训习</span>。在彼处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365785_comment'></div>委卿裁之。虽有边虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365785_comment'></div>固无忧也。秋初尚热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365785_comment'></div>卿及将士并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365785_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1365785_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年8月5日</a>　八月五日千秋节(玄宗诞辰日),玄宗命诸学士及僧道讲论儒、道、佛教同异,九龄有贺状。作品：《贺论三教状》<div id='poem_1365886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺论三教状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年8月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · id='poem_sentence_2_1365886_comment'></div>理归于一贯。非夫上圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365886_comment'></div>孰探要旨。伏惟陛下道契无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365886_comment'></div>思该元妙。考六经之同异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365886_comment'></div>诠三教之幽赜。将以降照群疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365886_comment'></div>敷化率土。屏浮词于玉殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365886_comment'></div>辑精义于金门。一变儒风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365886_comment'></div>再扬道要。凡百士庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365886_comment'></div>罔不知归。臣等幸侍轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365886_comment'></div>亲承至训。忭跃之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365886_comment'></div>实倍常情。望宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365886_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365886_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　时小旱,是日澍雨,九龄复有贺雨状。作品：《贺雨状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　如所料,吐蕃果发兵欲攻取唐西南边城盐井等处，九龄运筹帷幄,分别有敕隽州都督许齐物和西南蛮大首领蒙归义书,令其稳妥设防,相互为援,无失事宜。作品：《敕隽州都督许齐物书》《敕西南蛮大首领蒙归义书》<div id='poem_1365784' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　顺授铎罗望袭任浪穹州刺史。作品：《敕蛮首领铎罗望书》<div id='poem_1365834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　朝廷得幽州节度使张守珪表,知奚倚官耨云暗结突厥,欲图异谋,奚王李归国临危制变,与松漠都督涅礼等借助唐军的策应与后援,联手大破突厥,内侍刘思贤至省奉宣圣旨,垂示破贼所由,九龄随之上贺破突厥状和贺东北累捷状,并奉拟敕书,对李归国和涅礼等予以彰表慰勉。作品：《敕奚都督李归国书》《敕松漠都督涅礼书》<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365766_comment'></div>卿之忠诚。加以义勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365766_comment'></div>以顺讨逆。自然必胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365869_comment'></div>事皆有预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365869_comment'></div>万全之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365869_comment'></div>永静边隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365869_comment'></div>薄伐之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365869_comment'></div>匪劳中夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365869_comment'></div>凡在黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365869_comment'></div>孰不欣跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365869_comment'></div>臣等忝预枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365869_comment'></div>倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365869_comment'></div>无任庆悦之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1365869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　九龄随之上贺破突厥状,对李归国和涅礼等予以彰表慰勉。作品：《贺破突厥状》<div id='poem_1365868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺破突厥状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365868")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365868'>右。张守圭表奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365868_comment'></div>突厥四万骑。前月二十五日至能讫离山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365868_comment'></div>契丹泥礼等前后斩获俘馘。数逾十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365868_comment'></div>突厥可汗弃甲逃●。奚王李归国及平卢军将等追奔逐北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365868_comment'></div>计日歼灭。更闻奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365868_comment'></div>伏以突厥新立。轻事用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365868_comment'></div>彼之威众。在于一举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365868_comment'></div>又两蕃与其结隙。文搆未深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365868_comment'></div>在于边隅。犹轸天算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365868_comment'></div>陛下料其终始。指授规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365868_comment'></div>知其举种尽来。本自无策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365868_comment'></div>劳师袭远。必合成擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365868_comment'></div>使蕃骑先锋。汉军坚壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365868_comment'></div>坐观成败。自战蛮夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365868_comment'></div>今契丹才交。突厥已破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365868_comment'></div>计其奔北。必至丧亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365868_comment'></div>脱身获全。亦举众皆弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365868_comment'></div>北虏震慑。从此气衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365868_comment'></div>东胡保边。永不携贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365868_comment'></div>宽徭罢柝。自此可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365868_comment'></div>斯皆圣德远覃。皇威遐振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365868_comment'></div>事无遗策。举不失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365868_comment'></div>臣忝迹枢近。亲承睿略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365868_comment'></div>忭跃之至。倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365868_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365868_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1365868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　与此同时,九龄又有论东北等未可轻动状,力主唐军应审慎行事,切勿以一军之利而黩武结怨,为国生患。并望在内侍刘思贤出使东北之际,降书张守珪等必为远图,无得妄动。作品：《论东北军未可轻动状》<div id='poem_1365859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论东北军未可轻动状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365859")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365859'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365859'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365859_comment'></div>高力士宣奉敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365859_comment'></div>张守圭所进送突厥生口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365859_comment'></div>具问知委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365859_comment'></div>故令刘思贤去者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365859_comment'></div>臣等伏以北虏凶狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365859_comment'></div>诚亦难保其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365859_comment'></div>然陛下以恩泽怀柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365859_comment'></div>岁月已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365859_comment'></div>使彼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365859", 1365859, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>豺武</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365859_comment'></div>顿改顽暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365859_comment'></div>以事观察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365859_comment'></div>信然不虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365859_comment'></div>何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365859_comment'></div>昨李佺使回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365859_comment'></div>虏亦具云东下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365859_comment'></div>中间或言难信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365859_comment'></div>至今果如所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365859_comment'></div>即是输诚于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365859_comment'></div>未有他诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365859_comment'></div>且契丹等翻覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365859_comment'></div>或往或来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365859_comment'></div>今其东讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365859_comment'></div>虽未禀命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365859_comment'></div>在于夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365859_comment'></div>亦不可责于常理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365859_comment'></div>若因而屠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365859_comment'></div>亦便除患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365859_comment'></div>陛下先有圣料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365859_comment'></div>以为如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365859_comment'></div>臣等常窃志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365859_comment'></div>固非所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365859_comment'></div>今其来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365859_comment'></div>若契丹等偶胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365859_comment'></div>北虏势衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365859_comment'></div>因而乘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365859_comment'></div>灭其大半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365859_comment'></div>审料必取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365859_comment'></div>始可决行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365859_comment'></div>事若不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365859_comment'></div>而军将妄动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365859_comment'></div>徒结大隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365859_comment'></div>亦以不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365859_comment'></div>为国生患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365859_comment'></div>莫甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365859_comment'></div>臣伏以在边诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365859_comment'></div>苟利一军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365859_comment'></div>便即行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365859_comment'></div>以邀荣赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365859_comment'></div>不思远计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365859_comment'></div>诚是大失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365859_comment'></div>今刘思贤往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365859_comment'></div>望将降书处分守圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365859_comment'></div>必为远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365859_comment'></div>无得妄动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365859_comment'></div>防约诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365859_comment'></div>使知圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365859_comment'></div>纵虏庭闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365859_comment'></div>尤彰天泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365859_comment'></div>未审可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365859_comment'></div>谨录状奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1365859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　分别致敕张守珪和平卢使乌知义,嘱其临机处事,务防困兽之斗,必图万全完胜。作品：《敕幽州节度张守珪书》（之四）《敕平卢使乌知义书》（之一）<div id='poem_1365765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕平卢使乌知义书</a><span class='authorDate'>（733年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365765")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365765'>敕乌知义。两蕃既巳归我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365765_comment'></div>突厥仍敢犯边。此其不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365765_comment'></div>诚可残灭。适闻契丹及奚等并力合谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365765_comment'></div>同破凶丑。卿亦继进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365765_comment'></div>相与成功。此之一捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365765_comment'></div>使其丧气。然斗防困兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365765_comment'></div>诱备羸师。兵家之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365765_comment'></div>慎在终始。卿是宿将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365765_comment'></div>当自明之。若见可则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365765_comment'></div>务须灵敏。固在临事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365765_comment'></div>难用速言。必图万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365765_comment'></div>不可轻举。巳敕守圭与卿计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365765_comment'></div>可须观衅裁之。秋凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365765_comment'></div>卿及将士巳下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365765_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365765_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　又敕奚都督李归国务与涅礼等相为腹背,追袭突厥。作品：《敕奚都督李归国书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕奚都督李归国书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365764")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365764'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365764'>敕奚都督右金吾卫大将军归诚王李归国。朕比闻突厥欲灭卿两蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365764_comment'></div>先敕守圭严为防护。今闻泥礼巳破凶徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365764_comment'></div>仍虑其收合馀烬。复来掩袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365764_comment'></div>卿可与泥礼相为腹背。但突厥不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365764_comment'></div>后患终深。卿可伺其归师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365764_comment'></div>乘其丧气。与诸将计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365764_comment'></div>逐要追袭。时不可失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365764_comment'></div>宜自思之。秋深极冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365764_comment'></div>卿及衙官将士已下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365764_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1365764_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　有让赐蕃口状。作品：《让赐蕃口状》<div id='poem_1365903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让赐蕃口状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_5_1365903_comment'></div>存以至公。矜遂恳诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365903_comment'></div>许归官寺。则上有无偏之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365903_comment'></div>下有无苟之责。无任悃款之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365903_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1365903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　贺御注金刚经状,请御注经内外传授状。作品：《贺御注金刚经状》《请御注经内外传授状》<div id='poem_1365887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺御注金刚经状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365887")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365887'>右。内侍尹凤祥宣敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365887_comment'></div>垂示臣等御注金刚经。但佛法宗旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365887_comment'></div>撮在此经。人閒传习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365887_comment'></div>多所未悟。陛下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365887", 1365887, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>曲垂</span>圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365887_comment'></div>敷演微言。幽关妙键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365887_comment'></div>豁然洞达。虽臣等愚昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365887_comment'></div>本自难晓。伏览睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365887_comment'></div>亦即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1365887", 1365887, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>发明</span>。是知日月既出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365887_comment'></div>天下普照。诚在此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365887_comment'></div>陛下至德法天。平分儒术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365887_comment'></div>道已广度其宗。僧又不违其愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365887_comment'></div>三教并列。万姓知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365887_comment'></div>伏望降出御文。内外传授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365887_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1365887_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请御注经内外传授状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365861")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365861'>右。臣等今日于九龄处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365861_comment'></div>伏见集贤院奉贺御注前件。经墨敕批答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365861_comment'></div>兼九龄说。睿思幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365861_comment'></div>元关洞辟。微言奥旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365861_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365861", 1365861, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>廓然</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365861", 1365861, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>昭畅</span>。臣等<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365861", 1365861, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>近识</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365861_comment'></div>暗于大道。粗闻九龄此传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365861_comment'></div>便若已有所得。欣戴感悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365861_comment'></div>诚不克任。伏惟陛下天纵无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365861_comment'></div>有来斯应。万殊一贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365861_comment'></div>三教同归。伏望降出御本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365861_comment'></div>使内外传授。则冀明积劫之重昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365861_comment'></div>纳群迷于正觉。朝闻夕死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365861_comment'></div>尚不足吝。顾此轻生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365861_comment'></div>于焉何幸。臣等不胜忭跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365861_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365861_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　是时,西突厥族突骑施部落苏禄可汗又欲率部图陷庭州等处,九龄拟敕河西节度使牛仙客书,令其做好攻防准备,并命内侍程元宗前往催遣兵马,一一口具。作品：《敕河西节度使牛仙客书》（之二）《敕河西节度副大使牛仙客书》<div id='poem_1365822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕河西节度副大使牛仙客书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365822")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365822'>敕河西节度副大使太仆卿摄御史大夫牛仙客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365822_comment'></div>突骑施连岁犯边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365822_comment'></div>凶恶如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365822_comment'></div>若不威服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365822_comment'></div>祗长寇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365822_comment'></div>自夏及今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365822_comment'></div>连岁不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365822_comment'></div>疏勒虽解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365822_comment'></div>边城见侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365822_comment'></div>虽无如我何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365822_comment'></div>亦为边所患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365822_comment'></div>终须有计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365822_comment'></div>以挫凶谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365822_comment'></div>卿可于西河诸军州拣练骁雄五千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365822_comment'></div>即赴安西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365822_comment'></div>受王斛斯部分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365822_comment'></div>朕当发遣十八年安西应替五千四百八十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365822_comment'></div>与彼相续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365822_comment'></div>足得成师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365822_comment'></div>若无暂劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365822_comment'></div>何从息甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365822_comment'></div>且此贼狂悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365822_comment'></div>不论信义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365822_comment'></div>直肆凶毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365822_comment'></div>其意巳然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365822_comment'></div>不此加兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365822_comment'></div>以图扑灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365822_comment'></div>使其骄暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365822_comment'></div>岂有宁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365822_comment'></div>巳敕盖嘉运与王斛斯审量事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365822_comment'></div>临时为计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365822_comment'></div>既为卿探访所管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365822_comment'></div>亦宜随要指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365822_comment'></div>兼有别敕发三万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365822_comment'></div>此但声援而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365822_comment'></div>可大张威势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365822_comment'></div>远使震摄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365822_comment'></div>又恐安西资用之乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365822_comment'></div>卿可于凉府将二十万段物往安西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365822_comment'></div>令随事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1365822", 1365822, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>支拟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365822_comment'></div>及充宴赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365822_comment'></div>朕则续支送凉府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365822_comment'></div>冬中甚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365822_comment'></div>卿及将士并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365822_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1365822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　同时,又与别敕令北庭将士,严阵以待,敌此凶寇。作品：《敕北庭将士已下书》<div id='poem_1365748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕北庭将士已下书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365748")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365748'>敕北庭将士瀚海军使盖嘉运已下。逆胡忿戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365748_comment'></div>乘此猖狂。驱率匪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365748_comment'></div>围犯边镇。皆如素虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365748_comment'></div>不出下策。卿等虽在绝境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365748_comment'></div>且据坚城。将士一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365748_comment'></div>莫非义勇。观衅而动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365748_comment'></div>取乱在兹。宜临事筹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365748_comment'></div>无失此便。但苏禄本以奸诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365748_comment'></div>诳诱群胡。无德在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365748_comment'></div>何能有国。今乃驱乌合之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365748_comment'></div>作不义之举。师曲在老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365748_comment'></div>族灭其时。卿可因其不固之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365748_comment'></div>乘其已疲之众。掎角归路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365748_comment'></div>剪灭逋丑。此亦天与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365748_comment'></div>岂直人谋。仍熟料之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365748_comment'></div>取万全也。国之重赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365748_comment'></div>惟待奇功。岂在言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365748_comment'></div>自良图耳。比秋气已冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365748_comment'></div>卿及将士百姓并安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365748_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　同时,又与别敕西州都督张待宾等,严阵以待,敌此凶寇。作品：《敕西州都督张待宾书》<div id='poem_1365749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕西州都督张待宾书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365749'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365749'>敕西州都督张待宾及官吏百姓已下。不虞狂贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365749_comment'></div>拥众多时。彼州军人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365749_comment'></div>素乏器械。闻其悉力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365749_comment'></div>能不悬心。卿等坚守孤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365749_comment'></div>敌此凶寇。亦既久拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365749_comment'></div>终然万全。斯乃义可感幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365749_comment'></div>鬼神相助。妖不胜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365749_comment'></div>氛祲自销。来无所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365749_comment'></div>去无所得。犬羊之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365749_comment'></div>道路埋魂。其于破伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365749_comment'></div>亦云甚矣。向使甲戈有豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365749_comment'></div>士卒且强。蹑彼归途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365749_comment'></div>可无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1365749", 1365749, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>噍类</span>。即令所司支料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365749_comment'></div>以备后来。其有功之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365749_comment'></div>各且据实。以时叙定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365749_comment'></div>当有酬赏。其龙泉寺小堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365749_comment'></div>被其残破。虽巳收拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365749_comment'></div>犹虑损伤。各宜宣慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365749_comment'></div>令得存活。秋气巳冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365749_comment'></div>卿及寮吏百姓巳下并平安好。今赐卿衣一副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365749_comment'></div>至宜领取。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365749_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1365749_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　同时,又与别敕瀚海军使盖嘉运,严阵以待,敌此凶寇。作品：《敕瀚海使盖嘉运书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　因陇右节度阴承本所部兵马备边、修筑城堡,吐蕃赞普顿生疑窦,九龄拟敕予以说明并重申汉蕃旧好。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之四）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　秋冬之际,先妣桂阳君夫人卢氏逝已两年,九龄有状告请回乡以毕大样祭礼,而玄宗倚重正殷,未允所请。作品：《请赴祥除状》<div id='poem_1365908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赴祥除状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365908")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365908'>右。殃衅残生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365908_comment'></div>谬承天泽。无能报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365908_comment'></div>徒废情礼。而日月迅速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365908_comment'></div>祥制有期。在臣私情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365908_comment'></div>哀惧莫主。几筵在远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365908_comment'></div>追慕不亲。一违外除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365908_comment'></div>终身何托。伏望察臣罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365908_comment'></div>俯遂哀恳。假以传乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365908_comment'></div>暂赴来月。道路往复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365908_comment'></div>不出数旬。孝理之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365908_comment'></div>冀知死所。无任悲迫战惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365908_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365908_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年10月</a>　冬十月,玄宗拟于来年正月七日取南路幸西京,因命九龄敕告所司准式,务从节减。作品：《敕幸西京》<div id='poem_1365728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕幸西京</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365728")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365728'>敕。朕所时迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365728_comment'></div>皆顺物情。顷属关辅无年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365728_comment'></div>遽尔东幸。固非为已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365728_comment'></div>将以息人。今百谷既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365728_comment'></div>庶务皆省。而五陵所奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365728_comment'></div>诚在京师。安可更留周南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365728_comment'></div>有阙时荐。宜以来年正月七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365728_comment'></div>取南路幸西京。所司准式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365728_comment'></div>应缘行幸所须。务从节减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365728_comment'></div>所由明为条例。勿使劳烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365728_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　因玄宗对东北边地情况料测如睹,九龄先后三进贺状,并请付史馆纪之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　突骑施苏禄可汗于是年春与吐蕃结盟后,益发蠢蠢欲动,自夏初又与唐交恶,至冬则大举犯边,攻战历涉三年。此间九龄恪尽中枢辅弼之责,心系边关，频繁地致敕安西节度王斛斯、河西节度副大使牛仙客、瀚海军使北庭都护盖嘉运和天山军使张待宾等将领,及时地传达、部署攻防战略,慰勉守边将士。作品：《贺张待宾奏尅捷状》《贺突厥小可汗必是伤死状》《敕四镇节度王斛斯书》（之九）《敕四镇节度王斛斯书》（之十）《敕四镇节度王斛斯书》（之十一）《敕天山军使张待宾书》<div id='poem_1365864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张待宾奏尅捷状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365864")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365864'>右。高力士宣示臣等张待宾表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365864_comment'></div>臣等前因奏事。亲承圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365864_comment'></div>悬料数日当有捷书。及此使至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365864_comment'></div>皆如睿略。但狂胡背诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365864_comment'></div>围逼军州。凶力固已困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365864_comment'></div>边城一无所损。臣等伏料此贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365864_comment'></div>早是破伤。大众远来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365864_comment'></div>踰月乃去。马羸则多死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365864_comment'></div>人苦则计生。本是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1365864", 1365864, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>乌杂</span>之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365864_comment'></div>足徵破亡之渐。此皆皇威远詟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365864_comment'></div>氛祲坐销。岂伊边人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365864_comment'></div>所能自保。臣等幸忝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1365864", 1365864, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>枢近</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365864_comment'></div>承奉圣谟。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1365864", 1365864, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>边捷</span>有符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365864_comment'></div>不胜庆悦。谨奉状陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365864_comment'></div>仍望宣付史馆。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365864_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365864_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺突厥小可汗必是伤死状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365871")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365871'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365871_comment'></div>牛仙童宣敕送前件契丹令问委曲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365871_comment'></div>臣等借问突厥退散所由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365871_comment'></div>其伊吐于被擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365871_comment'></div>将随五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365871_comment'></div>因夜却走回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365871_comment'></div>每日实见突厥诸将皆于衙帐前哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365871_comment'></div>及剺正面是实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365871_comment'></div>㨿此必是小可汗伤死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365871_comment'></div>若其不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365871_comment'></div>不合如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365871_comment'></div>审观伊吐于情状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365871_comment'></div>亦即不敢妄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365871_comment'></div>必其不虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365871_comment'></div>乃是天败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365871_comment'></div>比其归至本处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365871_comment'></div>固应更有馀殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365871_comment'></div>丑虏破●。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365871_comment'></div>必自此始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365871_comment'></div>陛下圣德无远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365871_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1365871", 1365871, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>妖沴</span>自销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365871_comment'></div>不劳师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365871_comment'></div>已清朔漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365871_comment'></div>臣等获奉庙算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365871_comment'></div>不胜忭跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1365871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕天山军使张待宾书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365823")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365823'>敕天山军使张待宾。近知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1365823", 1365823, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>贼下</span>烧此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365823_comment'></div>安然即去。竟无斥堠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365823_comment'></div>来不预知。如此防边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365823_comment'></div>无乃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365823", 1365823, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>疏阔</span>。此一分头抄掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365823_comment'></div>计其数不至多。向若烽燧稍明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365823_comment'></div>复与北庭计会。相与来击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365823_comment'></div>贼可无遗。且边镇统军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365823_comment'></div>俱受朝委。共防患害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365823_comment'></div>何异一家。况在绝漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365823_comment'></div>尤宜相协。巳敕盖嘉运讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365823_comment'></div>可与之筹宜。凶党复来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365823_comment'></div>固须有预。冬中甚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365823_comment'></div>卿及将士并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365823_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1365823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年12月</a>　十二月,因玄宗西幸改期,九龄有状请宣付史馆。作品：《西幸改期请宣付史馆状》<div id='poem_1365862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西幸改期请宣付史馆状</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365862")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365862'>右。臣今日面奉进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365862_comment'></div>西幸有日。般运已去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365862_comment'></div>仍闻京畿百姓。犹有未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365862_comment'></div>倘来岁未熟。下无所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365862_comment'></div>朕虽至彼。复有何情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365862_comment'></div>欲延期至来冬。待看谷麦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365862_comment'></div>卿等商度。以为何似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365862_comment'></div>臣等具奏。洛阳城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365862_comment'></div>虽曰皇都。至于宫苑之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365862_comment'></div>制度本狭。然风土气候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365862_comment'></div>不甚宜人。陛下以万姓为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365862_comment'></div>万姓以陛下为命。亿兆所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365862_comment'></div>诚在圣躬。圣躬若安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365862_comment'></div>何顾小小。陛下遂当宁动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365862_comment'></div>再降德音。苟利于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365862_comment'></div>朕何顾惜。发言恻隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365862_comment'></div>感动神祗。臣等幸闻至言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365862_comment'></div>不觉承睫。圣恩爱育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365862_comment'></div>遂及于此。又敕臣等商量进来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365862_comment'></div>湛恩至德。焉可使朝臣不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365862_comment'></div>圣君鸿名。不可令史官无述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365862_comment'></div>臣望宣圣旨。改用来年十月幸西京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365862_comment'></div>仍望具将本状。遍示朝列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365862_comment'></div>并宣付史官等。臣不胜感戴踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365862_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1365862_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年12月</a>　在洛阳又有谢药状。作品：《谢赐药状》<div id='poem_1365898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365898'>右。高力士宣奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365898_comment'></div>赐臣等鹿角胶丸及<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365898", 1365898, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>驻年</span>面脂。有命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365898_comment'></div>感戴兼至。臣等涓滴无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365898_comment'></div>渥泽日深。多谢股肱之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365898_comment'></div>每惭智力之效。徒承圣恩同体之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365898_comment'></div>更沾御药<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365898", 1365898, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>驻年</span>之锡。事绝希幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365898_comment'></div>礼优常遇。微躯贱貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365898_comment'></div>因大造而载延。捧日承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365898_comment'></div>荷曲成而无极。臣等无任悚戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365898_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1365898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　本年徐浩为九龄所器重,两人结为忘年之交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　本年前后,朔方军节度大使兵部尚书信安郡王李祎大破东突厥凯旋而归,九龄拟敕宴赏朔方将士，姑系于此。作品：《敕处分宴朔方将士》<div id='poem_1365738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365738?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕处分宴朔方将士</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365738'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365738'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365738_comment'></div>朔方军节度大使兵部尚书信安郡王祎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365738_comment'></div>总戎朔陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365738_comment'></div>经略万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365738_comment'></div>赋车籍马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365738_comment'></div>精卒锐兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365738_comment'></div>自其有虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365738_comment'></div>莫不素练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365738_comment'></div>而丑虏背诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365738_comment'></div>偏师致诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365738_comment'></div>谋若有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365738_comment'></div>取如俯拾。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1365738_comment'></div>聊加宴乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365738_comment'></div>各宜坐食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365738_comment'></div>相与尽欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365738_comment'></div>其军将巳下官赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365738_comment'></div>别有处分。<div class='inline'
