· </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365940")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365940_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365940'>夫道遵常习故。盖人拘于凡也。得精亡粗。是天纵于圣也。方圣上之拔太师也。岂藉誉于朝廷哉。径取才于无迹。悬收功于未眹。而终致大用。克成休烈。使祖虚名者。见西子而憎貌。工横议者。闻鲁连而杜口。乃知古谓则哲。惟帝其难。今之得人。遇圣为易。能允明主之鉴。不负真贤之实者。其在正平忠献公乎。公讳光庭。字连城。河东闻喜人也。伯翳之后。与秦同姓。始封于裴。因邑命氏。在魏晋之际。为人物之杰。与琅琊王氏相敌。时人谓之八裴八王。自兹厥后。奕代更盛。大王父定高。周大将军冯翊太守琅琊公。大父仁(此处基字避玄宗讳)隋光禄大夫。追赠持节原州都督。天之既厌隋德矣。见危致命。不亦难乎。谥之曰忠。春秋之义也。父行俭。礼部尚书兼定襄道行军大总管闻喜县公赠太尉。时或有奸王命矣。禁暴安人。不谓重乎。谥之曰宪。尊名之典也。公即太尉公次子。降神元和。含光不耀。越在初岁。巳有老成。虽远大是图。而近识莫悟。学探帝载。何事小名。业综人伦。岂矜一善。弱岁居太尉宪公丧。幼以孝闻。寻补宏文馆学士。神龙初明经擢第。授家令寺丞。转太常丞。加朝散大夫。景龙中以亲累外转。寻入为陕王友。改右卫郎将。丁晋国太夫人忧。柴毁骨立。殆至灭性。服免。起为贝州别驾。未之就也。复除右卫郎。居无何。迁率府中郎。嗟乎。有其道而无其用。不可行也。得其时而不得其志。亦不可行也。公负经纶之器。韬王霸之略。自委洎外台。栖迟下位。出入从事。十数年閒。坦然而自若者何哉。盖知才有所必伸。命有所必与。非苟而巳。开元中。圣上思光禄之休烈。嘉太尉之元勋。是必象贤。其将大受。特拜司门郎中。转兵部。仙台之文。始应列宿。鸿渐之羽。可用为仪。迁鸿胪少卿。以观其能也。是岁天子有事于岱宗。诸侯会朝于行在。执笾豆者。不限于中外。献琛赆者。亦勤于骏奔。莫不来享。无有远近。而执政者以公代晓边事。职在行人。且曰。夷狄豺狼。黩盟阻德。我今有事。戎或生心。我张吾师。有备无患。若何。公曰。不可。夫封禅者。所以告成功也。观乓者。所以威逆命也。云亭苗扈。非一时之事也。受脤执燔。非三代之礼也。天方佑我。光启旧服。憬彼獯鬻。能违天乎。无庸剿人。可以谍告。从之。秋九月。突厥果使其相执失颉利发与其介阿史德暾泥熟来朝。公之谋也。东封还。迁兵部侍郎。圻父之职。夏卿之亚。存而举者。悉以咨之。公于是考遗训。补缺典。饰蒐苗狝狩之礼。详施税稽之赋。颁九畿之政。设九伐之刑。以练国容。以精军实。边鄙不耸。帝用嘉之。既而拜中书侍郎同中书门下平章事兼御史大夫。王言其出。霈乎人有归也。天宪惟明。肃乎人知禁也。寻加银青光禄大夫。换黄门侍郎。俄迁侍中兼吏部尚书宏文馆学士。总百揆之枢辖。酌九流之渊奥。叶文轨之殷。度人神之和。木火象鼎。其惟实餗。山川出云。用作霖雨。时哉之会。无得称焉。先是大化之行。务以元默。遵夫易。旧章在而不议。吏道杂以多端。公于是求革故之实。契随时之义。作执秩以平之。设循资以定之。谨权衡以选之。考殿最以参之。奸回无所措其邪。噂不能介其量。多士动色。群方改瞻。仰之者邈乎如山。窥之者间不容发。或曰。执事无乃惠欤。公曰。大命敢不敬欤。若然。方将致六符于泰阶。驱百姓于仁寿。岂直睥睨先世。纷纶近古。汨而随流。守而勿失云尔哉。二十年冬。上幸河东。祠后土。命公兼左军师。礼毕。赐爵正平男。加光禄大夫。抑人有言曰。树德莫如滋。积仁莫如重。则臧僖之庆。有后于鲁。栾武之德。未绝于人。宜公侯之子孙。必复其始也。公尝读易。至益之屯。与升之渐。乃喟然叹曰。物恶有满而不溢。高而不危者哉。既而居不崇侈。动不踰法。虽百乘之家。万夫之长。冲如也。谓日用不知。存诸方册。何天年未永。瘼此台臣。二十有一年春三月癸卯。遘疾薨于京师平康里之私第。春秋五十八。朝廷哀伤。冕旒震悼。制户部尚书杜暹即殡吊祭。赙物五百段。粟五百石。丧事优厚官供。辍朝三日。丁未。有诏赠太师。谥曰忠献。使左庶子摄鸿胪寺卿李□监护丧事。以某月日。葬我忠献公于闻喜之旧茔。礼也。初知星者言。上相有变。良臣将殁。谓请禳之。公曰。使祸可禳而去。则福可祝而来也。论者多之。以为知命。夫天下之达道有五。所以行之者三。曰忠孝仁。安君忠也。荣亲孝也。周物仁也。此三者有一于身。鲜矣。而公实兼之。且媚于人者。必好其威福。贤于事者。必羞其谤政。公知其然。则以直道匪躬之故。忠莫厚矣。礼为人子。春秋以致享。义于人臣。夙夜以从命。公知其然。则以时告如在之敬。孝莫重焉。夫以衡石之任。陶钧之力。莫不责成于下吏。求备于一人。以故舞文雷同。疑狱岁搆。恬而不改。浸以成风。公知其然。则以信察御物之惠。仁莫加焉。其行已奉公。皆此类也。尝所著述。率于箴规。以为惇叙九族。本枝百代。王者之盛也。而义不可以无训。作瑶山往记维城前轨以讽之。微而彰。志而晦。圣人之举也。道不可以虚行。作续春秋。自战国迄于周隋以统之。臣子之义也。天人之际备矣。非洽闻通理。其孰能与于此乎。宜其存无幸人。殁有遗爱。嗣子稹。京兆府司录事参军。孝实克家。动必中礼。丕承后命。纡天鉴而增华。敢迹前修。琢丰碑而不朽。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365940'>益作舜虞，针分晋土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365940'>庆流八族，德盛三祖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365940'>琅琊象贤，怀文佩武。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365940'>光禄忠烈，杀身报主。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365940'>尚书出将，恢我王略。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365940'>文教内敷，武功外铄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365940'>缁衣之敝，惟公继作。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365940'>用晦而明，处丰思约。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365940'>鸿胪好谋，夏卿称职。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365940'>代天流化，佐皇立极。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1365940'>纳于宪府，好是正直。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365940'>乃宅冢司，谋猷允塞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365940'>尽瘁事国，夙夜在公。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365940'>居无阙政，殁有馀忠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1365940'>天子命我，颂德铭功。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1365940'>日月有既，令闻无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1365940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1365940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　在洛阳又与王斛斯书。作品：《敕安西节度王斛斯书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕安西节度王斛斯书</a><span class='authorDate'>（735年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365755")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365755'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365755'>敕王斛斯。得卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365755_comment'></div>知诸将接勇。亦有克捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365755_comment'></div>是卿指麾。获此凶丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365755_comment'></div>苏禄背德。敢兹寇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365755_comment'></div>自毙犬马之群。我无毫釐之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365755_comment'></div>闻其狼狈。疲羸满道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365755_comment'></div>乘此剪扑。势若摧枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365755_comment'></div>张羲之等虽各行诛。犹恨其少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365755_comment'></div>古之善用兵者。不必在众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365755_comment'></div>能制敌者。会在出奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365755_comment'></div>狂贼此来。真亦送死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365755_comment'></div>众既不整。心且非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365755_comment'></div>乌杂之虏。持久气衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365755_comment'></div>向有奇决。破之必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365755_comment'></div>且如所奏。亦足申威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365755_comment'></div>其将士立功擒杀有状。各据实闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365755_comment'></div>当加优赏。顷来诸军奏请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365755_comment'></div>所患在于不实。将既虚叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365755_comment'></div>人则妄求。如此相蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365755_comment'></div>自然挠法。朕以信示下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365755_comment'></div>以赏劝劳。岂于其閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365755_comment'></div>亦容有诡。故委卿在远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365755_comment'></div>所寄则深。必取诚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365755_comment'></div>勿令致此。冬初已冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365755_comment'></div>卿等及将士以下并平安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365755_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1365755_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　是年为中书令。春初,北庭都护盖嘉运旧疾复发,请入都就医,九龄拟敕回复,言以边事为重,应随时捕捉战机,诛剪贼寇,并告之将专遭医人前往疗疾。作品：《敕北庭都护盖嘉运书》<div id='poem_1365798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕北庭都护盖嘉运书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365798")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365798'>敕北庭都护盖嘉运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365798_comment'></div>近得卿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365798_comment'></div>知旧疾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365798", 1365798, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>发动</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365798_comment'></div>请入都就医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365798_comment'></div>欲遂来表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365798_comment'></div>虑有边要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365798_comment'></div>万一失便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365798_comment'></div>虽悔何追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365798_comment'></div>且苏禄猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365798_comment'></div>方拟肆恶边城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365798_comment'></div>经冬不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365798_comment'></div>西州近复烧屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365798_comment'></div>亦有杀伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365798_comment'></div>想所闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365798_comment'></div>此贼诸头抄掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365798_comment'></div>虏众巳疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365798_comment'></div>亦无能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365798_comment'></div>正可取便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365798_comment'></div>至如西州近者有贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365798_comment'></div>其数无多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365798_comment'></div>烽候若明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365798_comment'></div>密与两军作号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365798_comment'></div>首尾邀击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365798_comment'></div>立可诛剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365798_comment'></div>何为当军自守信贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365798_comment'></div>公行来有损伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365798_comment'></div>去无关键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365798_comment'></div>岂是边镇之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365798_comment'></div>且西庭虽无节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365798_comment'></div>受委固是一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365798_comment'></div>有贼共除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365798_comment'></div>有患相救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365798_comment'></div>万里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365798_comment'></div>何待奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365798_comment'></div>自此之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365798_comment'></div>必须用意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365798_comment'></div>今遣医人将药往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365798_comment'></div>可善自将疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365798_comment'></div>春初馀寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365798_comment'></div>卿及将士并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365798_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1365798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　敕发不久,边使王尚客、曹待仙等至,奏知盖嘉运等穷冬出师绝漠,多有杀获,苏禄遁走,北庭解围,九龄遂有贺状。作品：《贺北庭解围仍有杀获状》《敕贼苏禄遁走状》<div id='poem_1365865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺诛贼状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365865")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365865'>右。盖嘉运奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365865_comment'></div>北庭解围。仍有杀获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365865_comment'></div>苏禄背德。敢此雠天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365865_comment'></div>尽驱犬羊。来犯军镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365865_comment'></div>虽肆凶毒。欲逞其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365865_comment'></div>而边兵无遗镞之费。狂贼有舆尸之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365865_comment'></div>此皆陛下圣武。将士龚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365865_comment'></div>远必<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1365865", 1365865, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>叶谋</span>。动无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365865_comment'></div>能令氛祲。坐自廓清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365865_comment'></div>臣等忝奉密谋。屡承献捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365865_comment'></div>踊跃称庆。倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365865_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365865_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365865_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺贼苏禄遁走状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365874")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365874'>右。高力士宣敕示臣等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365874_comment'></div>曹待宣奏状。知苏禄遁走入山出界者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365874_comment'></div>四镇悬远。比被侵逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365874_comment'></div>将士用命。虽有诛锄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365874_comment'></div>凶党尚多。时有抄掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365874_comment'></div>兵疲矢尽。为弊亦深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365874_comment'></div>今日奔亡。诚是震惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365874_comment'></div>圣威及远。氛沴坐销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365874_comment'></div>又北庭救兵。当时回旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365874_comment'></div>不费军廪。事且无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365874_comment'></div>吐蕃纵实西行。苏禄不得相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365874_comment'></div>其败可必。又无可忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365874_comment'></div>边事且宁。不胜庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365874_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。谨奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365874_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　并再敕盖嘉运,予以慰勉。作品：《贺盖嘉运破贼状》<div id='poem_1365873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺盖嘉运破贼状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365873")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365873'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365873_comment'></div>高力士宣奉敕示臣等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365873_comment'></div>王尚客奏状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365873_comment'></div>知盖嘉运至突厥施店密城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365873_comment'></div>逢贼便斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365873_comment'></div>多有杀获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365873_comment'></div>且凶党大众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365873_comment'></div>见在边城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365873_comment'></div>方拟经春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365873_comment'></div>图为边患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365873_comment'></div>忽闻嘉运此入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365873_comment'></div>复有破伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365873_comment'></div>必其惊忙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365873_comment'></div>当有携散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365873_comment'></div>皆是圣略先定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365873_comment'></div>万里<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1365873", 1365873, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>悬同</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365873_comment'></div>尚客所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365873_comment'></div>合符前者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365873_comment'></div>臣等不胜庆跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1365873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　在守卫西域拨换城之战中，王斛斯所部朱仁惠等将领伤重沦亡,九齡拟敕予以悼惜褒赠,并对其他立功将官予以奖赏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　吐蕃赞普来章又论蛮中地界及抄掠等事,九齡拟敕回复,再申汉蕃连姻结约大义及彼中州图地记之故事,遣责吐蕃侵伐小勃律国和与突骑施相合谋唐碛西之地的不义之举。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕吐蕃赞普书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365814")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365814'>皇帝问赞普自与彼蕃连姻。亦已数代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365814_comment'></div>又与赞普结约。于今五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365814_comment'></div>人使往还。未尝有閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365814_comment'></div>朕以两国通好。百姓获安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365814_comment'></div>子孙已来。坐受其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365814_comment'></div>疆场之事。幸且无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365814_comment'></div>此虽境上有兵。固是存而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365814_comment'></div>在彼边事。与此何殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365814_comment'></div>近得来章。又论蛮中地界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365814_comment'></div>所有本末。前书具言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365814_comment'></div>赞普不体朕怀。乃更傍引远事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365814_comment'></div>若论蛮不属汉。岂复定属吐蕃耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365814_comment'></div>彼不得所即叛来。此不得所即背去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365814_comment'></div>如此常事。何乃固执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365814_comment'></div>复于国家何有。朕岂利之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365814_comment'></div>至如彼中铁柱州图地记。是唐九徵所记之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365814_comment'></div>诚有故事。朕岂妄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365814_comment'></div>所修城壁。亦依故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365814_comment'></div>若不复旧。岂为通和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365814_comment'></div>蛮中抄掠彼人。勘问亦有此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365814_comment'></div>缘其初附。法令未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365814_comment'></div>亦有姚巂边人。奸险求利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365814_comment'></div>或入蛮同盗。亦不可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365814_comment'></div>既与赞普重亲。朕又君临大国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365814_comment'></div>正欲混同六合。岂复侵取一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365814_comment'></div>再三巳论。何乃不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365814_comment'></div>顾惭薄德。良用咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365814_comment'></div>且如小勃律国归朝。即是国家百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365814_comment'></div>前遭彼侵伐。乃是违约之萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365814_comment'></div>朕以结信既深。不顾其小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365814_comment'></div>中閒遣使。曾不形言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365814_comment'></div>赞普何独相尤。而不思巳西之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365814_comment'></div>所存既大。当共成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365814_comment'></div>近闻莽布支西行。复有何故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365814_comment'></div>若与突骑施相合。谋我碛西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365814_comment'></div>未必有成。何须同恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365814_comment'></div>若尔者。欲先为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365814_comment'></div>乃以南蛮为词。今料此情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365814_comment'></div>亦巳有备。近令勒兵数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365814_comment'></div>继赴安西。傥有所伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365814_comment'></div>慎勿为怪也。朕心无所负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365814_comment'></div>事欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1365814", 1365814, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>论平</span>。但国家之所守者信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365814_comment'></div>鬼神之所助者顺。未有背道求福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365814_comment'></div>违约能昌。何况兵众不可当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365814_comment'></div>而又天道所不假。以此求济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365814_comment'></div>不亦难乎。远道所传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365814_comment'></div>多应不实。亦计赞普不合异图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365814_comment'></div>故令人审看。定何缘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365814_comment'></div>待潘息回日。更别具委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365814_comment'></div>今附少物。具如别数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365814_comment'></div>为路远不得多附。春首尚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365814_comment'></div>赞普及公主比如宜也。平章事及首领以下并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365814_comment'></div>今使内常侍窦元礼。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365814_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1365814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　为防突厥报复奚、契丹两蕃,九龄敕平卢使乌知义远加斥候,须有严备,并妥加节度近复归国的渤海、黑水两部,又派白真陁罗前往赐衣一副。作品：《敕平卢使乌知义书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365780' id='poem_sentence_2_1365780_comment'></div>志在报复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365780_comment'></div>复必再来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365780_comment'></div>契丹及奚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365780_comment'></div>岂云王略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365780_comment'></div>顷有没蕃人出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365780_comment'></div>云其见拟东行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365780_comment'></div>蕃汉诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365780_comment'></div>须有严备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365780_comment'></div>实谓得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365780_comment'></div>朕固无忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365780_comment'></div>一任量事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365780_comment'></div>渤海黑水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365780_comment'></div>近复归国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365780_comment'></div>亦委卿节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365780_comment'></div>想所知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365780_comment'></div>春初尚寒。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　随后,又敕突厥登利可汗,劝其不要侵伐奚及契丹诸蕃,当务其大者,应联合夹击突骑施,此乃长策。作品：《敕突厥可汗书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365805' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365805")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365805_comment'></div><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365805_comment'></div>及儿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365805", 1365805, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>绍续</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365805_comment'></div>情意日深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365805_comment'></div>至于国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365805_comment'></div>亦欲无别。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365805_comment'></div>然两蕃既归国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365805_comment'></div>亦即不合侵伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365805_comment'></div>朕既与儿无閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365805_comment'></div>终不以此为怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365805_comment'></div>契丹及奚。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365805_comment'></div>远劳师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365805_comment'></div>兼冒锋镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365805_comment'></div>胜不为武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365805_comment'></div>不胜亦危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365805_comment'></div>以此言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365805_comment'></div>当务其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365805_comment'></div>突骑施本非贵种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365805_comment'></div>出自异姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365805_comment'></div>惟任奸数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365805_comment'></div>诳诱群胡。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1365805_comment'></div>因其荒远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365805_comment'></div>遂得苟存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365805_comment'></div>近日以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365805_comment'></div>敢兹背德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365805_comment'></div>又知儿意亦欲破之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365805_comment'></div>前与先可汗举哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365805_comment'></div>其使不肯就哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365805_comment'></div>当时辞拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365805_comment'></div>彼使具知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365805_comment'></div>儿若总兵西行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365805_comment'></div>朕即出师相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365805_comment'></div>安西瀚海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365805_comment'></div>近已加兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365805_comment'></div>欲以灭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365805_comment'></div>复何难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365805_comment'></div>傥事捷之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365805_comment'></div>羊马土地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365805_comment'></div>总以与儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365805_comment'></div>子女玉帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365805_comment'></div>别有优赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365805_comment'></div>信是长策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365805_comment'></div>可熟思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365805_comment'></div>与儿情亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365805_comment'></div>故言及此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365805_comment'></div>今有少信物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365805_comment'></div>至宜领取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365805_comment'></div>春初尚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365805_comment'></div>儿与平章事首领百姓已下并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365805_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1365805_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年2月</a>　二月,宴新授县令于朝堂,九龄拟敕诫勉。作品：《敕处分县令》（之一）<div id='poem_1365734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕处分县令</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365734'>敕诸县令等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365734_comment'></div>自古致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365734_comment'></div>其在命官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365734_comment'></div>今之所切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365734_comment'></div>莫如守宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365734_comment'></div>朕每属意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365734_comment'></div>尤重此官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365734_comment'></div>有善者虽远必升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365734_comment'></div>无能者纵近必废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365734_comment'></div>惟取才实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365734_comment'></div>非务官资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365734_comment'></div>事亦坦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365734_comment'></div>天下所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365734_comment'></div>而浮竞之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365734_comment'></div>未识朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365734_comment'></div>俾其宰邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365734_comment'></div>便为弃地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365734_comment'></div>或以烦碎而不专意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365734_comment'></div>或以僻远而不畏法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365734_comment'></div>或以徇已而贪婪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365734_comment'></div>于何寄命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365734_comment'></div>朕所以寝兴轸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365734_comment'></div>思以济人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365734_comment'></div>故命吏曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365734_comment'></div>精选才干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365734_comment'></div>卿等各膺推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365734_comment'></div>用简朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365734_comment'></div>若能理化有声。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1365734_comment'></div>智者所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365734_comment'></div>应不至是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365734_comment'></div>各宜勉励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365734_comment'></div>以副勤属。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1365734_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年3月</a>　三月,敕令礼部掌贡人,对科举选入制度作出重大调整。作品：《敕令礼部掌贡人》<div id='poem_1365727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365727' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365727'>敕。每岁举人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365727_comment'></div>求士之本。专典其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365727_comment'></div>宁不重欤。顷年巳来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365727_comment'></div>惟考功郎所职掌。位轻事重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365727_comment'></div>名实不伦。欲尽委长官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365727_comment'></div>又铨选猥积。且六官之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365727_comment'></div>体国是同。况宗伯掌礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365727_comment'></div>宜主宾荐。自今已后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365727_comment'></div>每诸色举人及斋郎等简试。并于礼部集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365727_comment'></div>既众务烦杂。仍委侍郎专知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365727_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1365727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　突骑施苏禄率部遁走后,九龄又先后拟敕北庭经略使盖嘉运、安西都护王斛斯和诸国王叶护城使等,对其慰勉有加,嘱其常须有预，以逸待之。作品：《敕瀚海军使盖嘉运书》（之五）《敕安西节度王斛斯书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕安西节度王斛斯书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365787_comment'></div>遇此狂贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365787_comment'></div>爰自去夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365787_comment'></div>以迄于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365787_comment'></div>攻战相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365787_comment'></div>念甚勤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365787_comment'></div>近者闻在拨换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365787_comment'></div>兵少贼多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365787_comment'></div>朕每忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365787_comment'></div>虑遭吞噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365787_comment'></div>又闻兵势渐合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365787_comment'></div>将士同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365787_comment'></div>父子之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365787_comment'></div>亦不在众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365787_comment'></div>犬羊之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365787_comment'></div>复何能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365787_comment'></div>屡有杀获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365787_comment'></div>固其宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365787_comment'></div>卿等各负忠勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365787_comment'></div>为国忘身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365787_comment'></div>锋镝之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365787_comment'></div>疮痍未免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365787_comment'></div>或致物故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365787_comment'></div>深用哀伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365787_comment'></div>朱仁惠竟致沦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365787_comment'></div>良可悼惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365787_comment'></div>具有褎赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365787_comment'></div>以慰营魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365787_comment'></div>福流子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365787_comment'></div>良亦在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365787_comment'></div>其有频当矢石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365787_comment'></div>每战有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365787_comment'></div>义可成名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365787_comment'></div>勇能抗敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365787_comment'></div>或能出奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365787_comment'></div>以挫凶威。<div id='poem_sentence_39_1365787_comment'></div>自馀战士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365787_comment'></div>尽力边荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365787_comment'></div>计其积劳。<div id='poem_sentence_61_1365787_comment'></div>并依所请讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365787_comment'></div>告身即差使颁送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365787_comment'></div>初春尚寒。<div id='poem_sentence_66_1365787_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　吐蕃使来,仍言境上蛮夷越界筑城,将兵抄掠等事,九龄分别致敕赞普与金城公主,再申维护和好之意,并允公主所请之事。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之五）《敕金城公主书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_20_1365817_comment'></div>贾混之缘此未得独行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365817_comment'></div>待其稍瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365817_comment'></div>亦即遣去。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　渤海遣使来朝,恢复旧好,九龄有敕其王大武艺书,望其勿随突厥攻打奚、契丹两蕃。作品：《敕渤海王大武艺书》（之二）<div id='poem_1365777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365777' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365777'>敕渤海郡王忽汗州都督大武艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365777_comment'></div>不识逆顺之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365777_comment'></div>不知存●之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365777_comment'></div>而能有国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365777_comment'></div>未之闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365777_comment'></div>卿往年背德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365777_comment'></div>已为祸阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365777_comment'></div>近能悔过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365777_comment'></div>不失臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365777_comment'></div>迷复非远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365777_comment'></div>善又何加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365777_comment'></div>朕记人之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365777_comment'></div>忘人之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365777_comment'></div>况此归伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365777_comment'></div>载用嘉叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365777_comment'></div>永祚东土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365777_comment'></div>不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365777_comment'></div>所令大成庆等入朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365777_comment'></div>并已处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365777_comment'></div>各加官赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365777_comment'></div>想具知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365777_comment'></div>所请替人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365777_comment'></div>亦令还彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365777_comment'></div>又近得卿表云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365777_comment'></div>突厥遣使求合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365777_comment'></div>拟打两蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365777_comment'></div>奚及契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365777_comment'></div>今既内属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365777_comment'></div>而突厥私恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365777_comment'></div>欲雠此蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365777_comment'></div>卿但不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365777_comment'></div>何妨有使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365777_comment'></div>拟行执缚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365777_comment'></div>义所不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365777_comment'></div>此是人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365777_comment'></div>况为君道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365777_comment'></div>然则知卿忠赤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365777_comment'></div>动必以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365777_comment'></div>永保此诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365777_comment'></div>庆流未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365777_comment'></div>春晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365777_comment'></div>卿及衙官百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365777_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1365777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年4月</a>　本月,因平卢讨击使安禄山恃勇轻进,为虏所败,张守珪初奏欲斩。九龄适从边使赵堪回复中知其原委,即敕张守珪速按军法处置,以申军威。作品：《敕幽州节度使张守珪书》（之八）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年4月</a>　与此同时,又分别致敕平卢使乌知义及诸将士,令其务以安禄山无谋轻敌为训,重振军威,以补前阙。当张守珪未斩禄山、玄宗又免其死之际,唯九齡坚执固争,其先见之明彪炳史册也。作品：《敕平卢诸将士书》<div id='poem_1365773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365773?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕平卢诸将士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365773")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365773_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365773'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365773'>敕平卢诸军镇将士已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365773_comment'></div>两蕃残贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365773_comment'></div>馀类仅存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365773_comment'></div>朕尝怀抚柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365773_comment'></div>冀其迁善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365773_comment'></div>而数年之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365773_comment'></div>谋叛相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365773_comment'></div>信是枭鸱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365773_comment'></div>固非人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365773_comment'></div>顷者所以列置军镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365773_comment'></div>递为唇齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365773_comment'></div>所虞在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365773_comment'></div>岂欲劳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365773_comment'></div>卿等委身边疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365773_comment'></div>为国展效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365773_comment'></div>遇其反噬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365773_comment'></div>得不讨除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365773_comment'></div>近日安禄山无谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365773_comment'></div>率尔轻敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365773_comment'></div>驰突不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365773_comment'></div>遂损<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1365773", 1365773, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>师徒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365773_comment'></div>择将不良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365773_comment'></div>伤人已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365773_comment'></div>事虽既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365773_comment'></div>义实疚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365773_comment'></div>凡在平卢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365773_comment'></div>其阵亡之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365773_comment'></div>并委张守圭差人吊祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365773_comment'></div>并勘实乡贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365773_comment'></div>具以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365773_comment'></div>悯彼伤魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365773_comment'></div>当有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1365773", 1365773, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>赠饰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365773_comment'></div>兴言悼惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365773_comment'></div>久不能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365773_comment'></div>然此贼比来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365773_comment'></div>削弱已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365773_comment'></div>挼绳系颈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365773_comment'></div>人有其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365773_comment'></div>安禄山之败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365773_comment'></div>缘轻敌太过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365773_comment'></div>勿因此畏愞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365773_comment'></div>致失后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365773_comment'></div>立功成名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365773_comment'></div>荣贵斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365773_comment'></div>各宜勉励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365773_comment'></div>共除凶恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365773_comment'></div>夏初渐热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365773_comment'></div>卿等并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365773_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1365773_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　新罗比岁使来朝贡,累有物故,九龄致敕金兴光国王,对其恭勤忠义深表嘉勉。作品：《敕新罗王金兴光书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365775?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕新罗王金兴光书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365775")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365775'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365775'>敕鸡林州大都督新罗王金兴光。贺正谢恩两使续至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365775_comment'></div>再省来表。深具雅怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365775_comment'></div>卿位总一方。道踰万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365775_comment'></div>托诚见于章奏。执礼存乎使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365775_comment'></div>虽隔沧溟。亦如面会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365775_comment'></div>卿既能副朕虚巳。朕亦保卿一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365775_comment'></div>言念恳诚。每以嗟尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365775_comment'></div>况文章礼乐。粲焉可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365775_comment'></div>德义簪裾。浸以成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365775_comment'></div>自非才包时杰。志合本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365775_comment'></div>岂得物土异宜。而风流一变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365775_comment'></div>乃比卿于鲁卫。岂复同于蕃服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365775_comment'></div>朕之此怀。想所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365775_comment'></div>贺正使金义质及祖荣相次永逝。念其远劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365775_comment'></div>情以伤悯。虽有宠赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365775_comment'></div>犹不能忘。想卿乍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365775_comment'></div>当甚轸悼。近又得思兰表称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365775_comment'></div>知卿欲于浿江寘戍。既当渤海冲要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365775_comment'></div>又与禄山相望。仍有远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365775_comment'></div>固是长策。且蕞尔渤海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365775_comment'></div>久已逋诛。重劳师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365775_comment'></div>未能扑灭。卿每疾恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365775_comment'></div>深用嘉之。警寇安边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365775_comment'></div>有何不可。处置讫因使以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365775_comment'></div>今有少物。答卿厚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365775_comment'></div>至宜领取。春暮已暄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365775_comment'></div>卿及首领百姓并安好。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365775_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1365775_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　渤海王大武艺弟大戊庆等使还之际,九龄再敕大武艺,允其所请之事,并放还大朗雅等人。作品：《敕渤海王大武艺书》（之四）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年6月</a>　六月,在洛阳有贺雨状。作品：《贺雨状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年6月</a>　醴泉人刘志诚为乱伏诛后,又有贺昭陵惩应状。作品：《贺昭陵惩应状》<div id='poem_1365890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺昭陵徵应状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1365890_comment'></div>向臣等说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365890_comment'></div>妖贼刘志诚四日从咸阳北原向南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365890_comment'></div>见昭陵山上有黑云忽起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365890_comment'></div>志诚谓其凶徒云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365890_comment'></div>此云将有暴风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365890_comment'></div>若冲头立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365890_comment'></div>恐有破败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365890_comment'></div>志诚久从军伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365890_comment'></div>颇解杂占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365890_comment'></div>其言未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365890_comment'></div>飘风果至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365890_comment'></div>直冲行首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365890_comment'></div>莫不昏迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365890_comment'></div>众心惊惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365890_comment'></div>不知所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365890_comment'></div>及至便桥之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365890_comment'></div>并即走散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365890_comment'></div>又见父老云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365890_comment'></div>往年权梁山之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365890_comment'></div>将逞不轨。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1365890_comment'></div>彼比至京城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365890_comment'></div>贼还破灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365890_comment'></div>谨参往事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365890_comment'></div>与今同符者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365890_comment'></div>伏以闾阎贼类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365890_comment'></div>窃敢猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365890_comment'></div>而祖宗威灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365890_comment'></div>亦已元鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365890_comment'></div>昔年感召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365890_comment'></div>若命蚩尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365890_comment'></div>今者驱除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365890_comment'></div>更徵风伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365890_comment'></div>所以妖氛自殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365890_comment'></div>狡计莫施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365890_comment'></div>晷刻之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365890_comment'></div>逃形无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365890_comment'></div>此皆神功潜运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365890_comment'></div>昌历无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365890_comment'></div>将俾孙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365890_comment'></div>用昭圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365890_comment'></div>事堪惩恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365890_comment'></div>可以垂后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365890_comment'></div>无任庆悦之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365890_comment'></div>仍望宣付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365890_comment'></div>并示朝列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365890_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365890_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1365890_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　为彻底剿灭契丹叛亡之残孽,朝廷新征万人欲发东北。九龄致敕张守珪应秣马训兵,候时而动。作品：《敕幽州节度张守珪书》（之五）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　时值盛夏,高力士奉赐宰臣白羽扇,九龄感而献赋。作品：《白羽扇赋并序》<div id='poem_1365707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白羽扇赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365707")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365707_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365707'>开元二十四年夏。盛暑。奉敕使大将军高力士赐宰臣白羽扇。某与焉。窃有所感。立献赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365707'>当时而用。任物所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365707_comment'></div>彼鸿鹄之弱羽。出江湖之下方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365707_comment'></div>安知烦暑。可致清凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365707_comment'></div>岂无纨素。彩画文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365707_comment'></div>复有修竹。剖析毫芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365707_comment'></div>提携密迩。摇动馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365707_comment'></div>惟众珍之在御。何短翮之敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365707_comment'></div>而<span class='inlineComment2'>（文粹作与）</span>窃思于圣后。且见持于未央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365707_comment'></div>伊昔皋泽之时。亦有云霄之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365707_comment'></div>苟效用之得所。虽杀身之何忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365707_comment'></div>肃肃白羽。穆如清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365707_comment'></div>纵秋气之移夺。终感恩于箧中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365707_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　安西节度王斛斯上表言及联络大食共破突骑施事,九龄致敕命其坐实行事,力避空言虚报。随后又敕王斛斯据实以报阵亡将士名册,以便追赠官荣,并警示其抓紧屯收粮草,严防突骑施再行袭掠。作品：《敕安西节度王斛斯书》（之五）《敕安西节度王斛斯书》（之六）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　自去年东突厥新可汗登利即位后,朝廷为绍续父子之国的情义,于边境地重开马市,以优赏其民。然登利未明和市之限约,将以往每年交易的三四千匹马,腾升至一万四千余匹,且多有不堪驾驭之劣马。为此,九龄从本年夏末至冬中先后三敕儿可汗登利,申明互市互利之定准和限约,并令内侍赵惠琮前往理谕。作品：《敕突厥可汗书》（之四）《敕突厥可汗书》（之五）《敕突厥可汗书》（之六）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　七月,户部尚书李尚隐入蜀巡按,九龄有诗奉和。作品：《奉和圣制送李尚书入蜀》<div id='poem_22761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制送李尚书入蜀</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22761")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22761'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22761'>眷言感忠义，何有间山川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22761'>徇节今如此，离情空复然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22761'>皇心在勤恤，德泽委昭宣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22761'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_22761", 22761, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>周月</span>成功后，明年或劳还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年8月5日</a>　此日千秋节,群臣皆献宝镜,唯九龄以历代兴替之鉴撰成《千秋金镜录》五卷奉上,玄宗赐书褒美之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年8月7日</a>　此日,突骑施遣大首领胡禄达干来求和,还蕃之际,九龄拟敕毗伽可汗,严正申明言必信,行必果。作品：《敕突骑施毗伽可汗书》<div id='poem_1365806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕突骑施毗伽可汗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年8月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365806")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365806'>敕突骑施毗伽可汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365806_comment'></div>天地有正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365806_comment'></div>鬼神有正主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365806_comment'></div>敢此违犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365806_comment'></div>必有祸殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365806_comment'></div>不信朕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365806_comment'></div>但试看取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365806_comment'></div>可汗虽为君长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365806_comment'></div>实在幽荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365806_comment'></div>阴阳之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365806_comment'></div>偏僻如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365806_comment'></div>纵欲自大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365806_comment'></div>其如天何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365806_comment'></div>往年可汗初有册立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365806_comment'></div>以我国家常为势援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365806_comment'></div>诸蕃闻此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365806_comment'></div>不敢动摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365806_comment'></div>是我有大惠于可汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365806_comment'></div>行阴德于彼国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365806_comment'></div>自尔以后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365806_comment'></div>二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365806_comment'></div>情义相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365806_comment'></div>结为父子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365806_comment'></div>可汗身自不觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365806_comment'></div>岂不知彼之大援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365806_comment'></div>而戎俗少义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365806_comment'></div>见利生心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365806_comment'></div>故阙俟斤入朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365806_comment'></div>行至北庭有隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365806_comment'></div>因此计议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365806_comment'></div>即起异心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365806_comment'></div>何羯达所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365806_comment'></div>即是彼人自告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365806_comment'></div>踪迹已露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365806_comment'></div>然始行诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365806_comment'></div>边头事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365806_comment'></div>未是全失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365806_comment'></div>朕以擅杀彼使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365806_comment'></div>兼为罪责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365806_comment'></div>北庭破刘涣之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365806_comment'></div>仍传首于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365806_comment'></div>可汗纵有怨望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365806_comment'></div>亦合且有奏论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365806_comment'></div>朕若不依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365806_comment'></div>举兵未晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365806_comment'></div>而乃总无来状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365806_comment'></div>即起凶谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365806_comment'></div>侵我西州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365806_comment'></div>犯我四镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365806_comment'></div>连年累月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365806_comment'></div>马死人亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365806_comment'></div>于群胡已闻怨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365806_comment'></div>于国家岂能大损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365806_comment'></div>中閒使哥德都耽及安胡数半泥临河来此求和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365806_comment'></div>朕亦信受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365806_comment'></div>故遣使相逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365806_comment'></div>具宣往意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365806_comment'></div>其后审观形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365806_comment'></div>全是诈欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365806_comment'></div>故密敕半道令回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365806_comment'></div>岂是元心有负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365806_comment'></div>自尔之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365806_comment'></div>侵犯不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365806_comment'></div>可汗有何兵众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365806_comment'></div>遂此凭陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365806_comment'></div>诸国闻此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365806_comment'></div>岂不得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365806_comment'></div>约算已西诸国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365806_comment'></div>未敌我一两大州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365806_comment'></div>可汗亦应先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365806_comment'></div>何烦遂尔为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365806_comment'></div>况安西北庭将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365806_comment'></div>皆是铁石为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365806_comment'></div>可汗具谙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365806_comment'></div>不烦更道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365806_comment'></div>此则承前轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365806_comment'></div>彼自无义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365806_comment'></div>却以我为失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365806_comment'></div>无乃重其过乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365806_comment'></div>可汗向若有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365806_comment'></div>以理论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365806_comment'></div>阙俟斤下羊马数虽稍多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365806_comment'></div>欲为补答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365806_comment'></div>亦何足难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365806_comment'></div>惟费一州庸调酬还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365806_comment'></div>则已大多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365806_comment'></div>而乃无义为雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365806_comment'></div>暴我边镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365806_comment'></div>孤城小堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365806_comment'></div>仓卒见危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365806_comment'></div>大率而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365806_comment'></div>其数非少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365806_comment'></div>彼若计索马价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365806_comment'></div>我亦须得此物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365806_comment'></div>忝是有识之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365806_comment'></div>可不自解思量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365806_comment'></div>又可汗正为寇败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365806_comment'></div>阙伊难如从我界过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365806_comment'></div>葱岭捕获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365806_comment'></div>并物奏来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365806_comment'></div>所有蕃书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365806_comment'></div>具言物数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365806_comment'></div>朕皆送还赞普。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365806_comment'></div>其中一物不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365806_comment'></div>可汗亦以此为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365806_comment'></div>谓言朕留此物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365806_comment'></div>且蕃中贫薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365806_comment'></div>所见不广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365806_comment'></div>银瓶香子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365806_comment'></div>将作珍奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365806_comment'></div>黑毯赤縻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365806_comment'></div>亦为好物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365806_comment'></div>我中国虽在贫下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365806_comment'></div>固不以此为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365806_comment'></div>可汗宜识此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365806_comment'></div>勿妄生词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365806_comment'></div>且阙伊难如越界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365806_comment'></div>可汗复边头作梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365806_comment'></div>如此不捉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365806_comment'></div>更捉何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365806_comment'></div>适是边军明其用命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365806_comment'></div>观可汗求和之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365806_comment'></div>似未有真心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365806_comment'></div>只拟诱引国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365806_comment'></div>乘便取利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365806_comment'></div>如此等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365806_comment'></div>何用为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365806_comment'></div>我国守信如天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365806_comment'></div>终不欺物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365806_comment'></div>谓天无信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365806_comment'></div>物自无知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365806_comment'></div>然于四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365806_comment'></div>终不差也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365806_comment'></div>可汗若遂能为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365806_comment'></div>朕当别有处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365806_comment'></div>三二年内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365806_comment'></div>试看若为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365806_comment'></div>必其自省前非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365806_comment'></div>更思恩旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365806_comment'></div>朕即弃舍大过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365806_comment'></div>父子如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365806_comment'></div>可汗更有何忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365806_comment'></div>百姓皆得安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365806_comment'></div>一任可汗自料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365806_comment'></div>朕亦不复多言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365806_comment'></div>一一在使者口具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365806_comment'></div>秋中渐冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365806_comment'></div>可汗及公主衙官纛官首领百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365806_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_148_1365806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年9月</a>　九月,有贬韩朝宗洪州刺史制。是时,东北剿叛,已见成效,九龄再敕幽州节度使张守珪,督其除恶务尽,用息边甲。作品：《贬韩朝宗洪州刺史制》<div id='poem_1365719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贬韩朝宗洪州刺史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365719")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365719'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365719'>门下。所遣使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365719_comment'></div>将恤人隐。频亦谕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365719_comment'></div>期于悉心。而政或相蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365719_comment'></div>赏或失善。以此致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365719_comment'></div>未尝闻之。朝请大夫荆州大都督府长史兼判襄州刺史事山南道采访处置等使上柱国长山县开国伯韩朝宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365719_comment'></div>亟登清要。爰委条察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365719_comment'></div>宜恭尔职。以副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365719_comment'></div>而乃私其所亲。请以为邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365719_comment'></div>未盈三载。巳至两迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365719_comment'></div>既殊德举。自速官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365719_comment'></div>及令按事。果验非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365719_comment'></div>伤败实多。矫诬斯甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365719_comment'></div>举不为党。岂其然欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365719_comment'></div>事咨于周。则异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365719_comment'></div>不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365719", 1365719, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>自律</span>。何以正人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365719_comment'></div>仍期后效。且示轻贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365719_comment'></div>可使持节都督洪州诸军事守洪州刺史。散官勋封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365719_comment'></div>驰驿赴任。惟知人则哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365719_comment'></div>在予之责已深。而事上竭诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365719_comment'></div>为臣之节当励。其有赏罚不正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365719_comment'></div>枉直失措。陷于比周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365719_comment'></div>隳我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1365719", 1365719, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>纲目</span>。有一于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365719_comment'></div>谁其舍诸。凡今刺举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365719_comment'></div>宜以为戒。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365719_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1365719_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　此间,西北边地,军情又有新变,吐蕃越界与突骑施缔结姻亲之好,并遣莽布支率部西出,进而侵轶军镇、践暴屯田,九龄迅即致敕吐蕃赞普,予以严正警告,并随后派内常侍刘思贤、判官刘明子出使吐蕃,具宣往意,顺慰金城公主。作品：《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之六）《敕吐蕃赞普书》（之七）《敕金城公主书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕吐蕃赞普书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365820")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365820'>皇帝问吐蕃赞普。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365820_comment'></div>比亦觉彼事势有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365820_comment'></div>略加防备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365820_comment'></div>仍未益兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365820_comment'></div>今得安西表来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365820_comment'></div>莽布支率众巳到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365820_comment'></div>今见侵轶军镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365820_comment'></div>并践暴屯苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365820_comment'></div>先知彼有异谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365820_comment'></div>犹未自将至此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365820_comment'></div>且莽布支西出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365820_comment'></div>朕先知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365820_comment'></div>前令问其行由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365820_comment'></div>得报自缘别事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365820_comment'></div>今乃为贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365820_comment'></div>负心如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365820_comment'></div>安西诸军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365820_comment'></div>去此万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365820_comment'></div>仓卒遇敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365820_comment'></div>何暇奏裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365820_comment'></div>既彼交侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365820_comment'></div>必应拒斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365820_comment'></div>倘有伤损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365820_comment'></div>可无相尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365820_comment'></div>军城镇守之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365820_comment'></div>不可刺手就死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365820_comment'></div>事由彼起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365820_comment'></div>深所咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365820_comment'></div>且累代旧亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365820_comment'></div>复新有盟约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365820_comment'></div>彼既欺负天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365820_comment'></div>违犯鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365820_comment'></div>如此用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365820_comment'></div>更知何道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365820_comment'></div>一往边头所备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365820_comment'></div>只缘虑有非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365820_comment'></div>今果如言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365820_comment'></div>防乃不错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365820_comment'></div>突骑施异方禽兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365820_comment'></div>不可以大道论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365820_comment'></div>赞普与其越境相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365820_comment'></div>只虑野心难得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365820_comment'></div>但试相结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365820_comment'></div>久后如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365820_comment'></div>于朕巳然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365820_comment'></div>义则合绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365820_comment'></div>但为誓约在近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365820_comment'></div>亲好又深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365820_comment'></div>彼虽背恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365820_comment'></div>岂我尤效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365820_comment'></div>先令奔问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365820_comment'></div>欲尽旧情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365820_comment'></div>必定为恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365820_comment'></div>别为之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365820_comment'></div>一昨遣内常侍刘思贤送公主封物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365820_comment'></div>并每年国信物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365820_comment'></div>见已临路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365820_comment'></div>适会表来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365820_comment'></div>思贤此行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365820_comment'></div>量其在道迟缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365820_comment'></div>今故令刘思贤判官刘明子先行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365820_comment'></div>具宣往意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365820_comment'></div>秋冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365820_comment'></div>赞普公主及平章事首领百姓并平安好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365820_comment'></div>遣书指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1365820_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365819?labeling=true' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365819'>敕金城公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365819_comment'></div>数有来使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365819_comment'></div>闻彼安宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365819_comment'></div>差慰遥心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365819_comment'></div>想所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365819_comment'></div>柔顺之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365819_comment'></div>既以夙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365819_comment'></div>终始用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365819_comment'></div>贵于无失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365819_comment'></div>惟此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365819_comment'></div>馀不足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365819_comment'></div>所附物并依领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365819_comment'></div>具有还答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365819_comment'></div>并更附少信物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365819_comment'></div>别有委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365819_comment'></div>至宜领取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365819_comment'></div>秋冷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365819_comment'></div>念比何似。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　与此同时或稍后,又分别致敕安西节度使王斛斯、西州都督张待宾和北庭经略使盖嘉运等人,令其同仇敌忾,互为声援,尽敌乃已,并对立功的将士行赏有加。作品：《敕安西节度王斛斯书》（之七）《敕西州都督张待宾书》（之三）《敕北庭经略使盖嘉运书》（之三）<div id='poem_1365791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕安西节度王斛斯书</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365791")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365791'>敕王斛斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365791_comment'></div>吐蕃与我盟约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365791_comment'></div>歃血未乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365791_comment'></div>已生异心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365791_comment'></div>远结凶党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365791_comment'></div>而甘言缓我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365791_comment'></div>欲待合谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365791_comment'></div>连衡若成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365791_comment'></div>西镇何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365791_comment'></div>卿能先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365791_comment'></div>有以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365791_comment'></div>观衅而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365791_comment'></div>适是军法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365791_comment'></div>且屯苗既受践暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365791_comment'></div>军人亦被拘囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365791_comment'></div>如李混之所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365791_comment'></div>不反何谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365791_comment'></div>然则此蕃奸计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365791_comment'></div>颇亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1365791", 1365791, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>阴深</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365791_comment'></div>外示存约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365791_comment'></div>内实伺便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365791_comment'></div>事傥不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365791_comment'></div>即云无负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365791_comment'></div>卿还须知其变诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365791_comment'></div>随事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1365791", 1365791, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>交当</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365791_comment'></div>使其退不得以此为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365791_comment'></div>进不得成其凶计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365791_comment'></div>如此设拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365791_comment'></div>乃为上策若事巳侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365791_comment'></div>兵见交锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365821_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　驾还西京前,有奉和圣制谒元皇帝庙斋诗。作品：《奉和圣制谒元皇帝庙斋》<div id='poem_22896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制谒玄元皇帝庙斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span
