class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22896'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22896'>兴运昔有感，建祠北山巅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22896'>云雷初缔构，日月今悠然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22896'>紫气尚蓊郁，玄元如在焉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22896'>迨兹事追远，轮奂复增鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22896'>洞府香林处，斋坛清汉边。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22896'>吾君乃尊祖，夙驾此留连。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22896'>乐动人神会，钟成律度圆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22896'>笙歌下鸾鹤，芝朮萃灵仙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22896'>曾是福黎庶，岂唯味虚玄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22896'>赓歌徒有作，微薄谢昭宣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22896_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22896'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_22896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　驾还西京前,有奉和圣制贺祥云见状等。作品：《贺祥云状》<div id='poem_1365882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺祥云见状</a><span class='authorDate'>（736年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365882")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365882'>右。臣等伏见道门威仪司马秀表称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365882_comment'></div>今月十日夜。陛下亲临同明殿道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365882_comment'></div>为宗庙苍生祈福。有祥云见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365882_comment'></div>伏惟圣德以精至动天。天意以肸蚃符圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365882_comment'></div>其感甚速。其应岂远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365882_comment'></div>陛下圣敬之深。勤恤所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365882_comment'></div>灵心如答。神道何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365882_comment'></div>自表休期。以介景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365882_comment'></div>生人大赖。天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365882_comment'></div>臣等忝居近侍。倍百恒情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365882_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。伏望宣示史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365882_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年10月2日</a>　此日,扈驾自东都还西京。行前,谏请俟农收毕,待仲冬西幸,玄宗未纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　西行途中,有奉和圣制初出洛城诗。作品：《奉和圣制初出洛城》<div id='poem_22759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_22759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22759'>东土淹龙驾，西人望翠华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22759'>山川祗询物，宫观岂为家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22759'>十月回星斗，千官捧日车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22759'>洛阳无怨思，巡幸更非赊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
汾阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ec1f9e5224714af98922fdc52113e60c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ec1f9e5224714af98922fdc52113e60c");'><span id='ec1f9e5224714af98922fdc52113e60c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年</a>，46岁</div><div id='ec1f9e5224714af98922fdc52113e60c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=723&endYear=723')">723年2月</a>　为中书舍人。本月，随驾自太原南还晋州途中，出汾州雀鼠谷，张说献诗，玄宗和答。九龄与随行群臣苏颋、王丘、袁晖、崔翘、王光庭、席豫、梁升卿、赵冬曦、徐安贞等皆有应制诗。作品：《奉和圣制同二相南出雀鼠谷》<div id='poem_22825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制同二相南出雀鼠谷</a><span class='authorDate'>（723年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22825")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22825'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22825'>设险诸侯地，承平圣主巡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22825'>东君朝二月，南旆拥三辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22825'>寒出重关尽，年随行漏新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22825'>瑞云丛捧日，芳树曲迎春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22825'>舞咏先驰道，恩华及从臣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22825'>汾川花鸟意，并奉属车尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22825'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22825_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
灵宝

-----title
三门峡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fc137231ca2a4e56b0190a0e878eae6b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc137231ca2a4e56b0190a0e878eae6b");'><span id='fc137231ca2a4e56b0190a0e878eae6b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年</a>，47岁</div><div id='fc137231ca2a4e56b0190a0e878eae6b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=724&endYear=724')">724年11月</a>　为中书舍人。扈驾幸东都，沿途有奉和圣制途次陕州作诗。作品：《奉和圣制途次陕州作》<div id='poem_22762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制途次陕州作</a><span class='authorDate'>（724年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22762")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22762'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22762'>驰道当河陕，陈诗问国风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22762'>川原三晋别，襟带两京同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22762'>后殿函关尽，前旌阙塞通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22762'>行看洛阳陌，光景丽天中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22762'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22762_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='70372f551e35440e81b5dcfe6799c6df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("70372f551e35440e81b5dcfe6799c6df");'><span id='70372f551e35440e81b5dcfe6799c6df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年</a>，48岁</div><div id='70372f551e35440e81b5dcfe6799c6df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年10月13日</a>　在中书舍人任。此日玄宗东封泰山行次成皋太宗破窦建德处，感而赋诗，九龄等随侍者有和作。作品：《奉和圣制次成皋先圣擒建德之所》<div id='poem_22828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制次成皋先圣擒建德之所</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年10月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22828")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22828_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22828'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1665, "poem_allusion_22828")'>斩蛇</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22828'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22828'>天命诚有集，王业初惟艰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22828'>剪商自文祖，夷项在兹山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22828'>地识<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1665, "poem_sentence_2_22828")'>斩蛇</span>处，河临饮马间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22828'>威加昔运往，泽流今圣还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22828'>尊祖颂先烈，赓歌安用攀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22828'>绍成即我后，封岱出天关。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22828'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年10月13日</a>　在中书舍人任。此日奉拟《东封赦书》。九龄获加中散大夫，登封之际，谏张说推恩不及百官，希其改易，未果。<div id='poem_1365838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东封赦书</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年10月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365838")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365838'>门下。朕闻天监惟后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365838_comment'></div>后克奉天。既合德以受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365838_comment'></div>亦推恩而复始。厥初作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365838_comment'></div>七十二君。道洽迹著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365838_comment'></div>时至符出。皆用事于介邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365838_comment'></div>升中于上帝。人神之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365838_comment'></div>盖有以塞之。皇王之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365838_comment'></div>固可得而言也。朕接统千岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365838_comment'></div>承光五叶。惟祖宗之德在人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365838_comment'></div>惟天地之灵作主。往有内难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365838_comment'></div>幽赞而集大勋。闻无外虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365838_comment'></div>守成而缵旧服。未尝不乾乾终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365838_comment'></div>思与公卿大夫上下叶心。聿求至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365838_comment'></div>以宏我列圣。其庶几乎馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365838_comment'></div>今九有大宁。群氓乐业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365838_comment'></div>时必敬授而不夺。物亦顺成而无夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365838_comment'></div>懋建皇极。幸致太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365838_comment'></div>洎乃幽遐。率由感被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365838_comment'></div>戎狄不轨。唯文告而来庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365838_comment'></div>麟凤已臻。将觉悟而在薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365838_comment'></div>以故凡百执事。亟言大封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365838_comment'></div>顾惟不德。初欲勿议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365838_comment'></div>伏以先圣储祉。与天同功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365838_comment'></div>荷传符以在今。敢侑神而无报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365838_comment'></div>大节斯在。朕何让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365838_comment'></div>遂奉遵高祖太宗之业。宪章乾封之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365838_comment'></div>时迈东土。柴告岱宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365838_comment'></div>精意上达。肸蚃来应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365838_comment'></div>信宿行事。云物呈祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365838_comment'></div>登降之礼斯毕。严配之诚获展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365838_comment'></div>百神群望。莫不怀柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365838_comment'></div>四方诸侯。莫不来庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365838_comment'></div>斯事天道之介福。邦家之耿光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365838_comment'></div>无穷之休祉。岂独在予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365838_comment'></div>非常之惠泽。宜其逮下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365838_comment'></div>可大赦天下。自开元十三年十一月十三日昧爽已前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365838_comment'></div>大辟罪巳下。罪无轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365838_comment'></div>巳发觉未发觉。已结正未结正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365838_comment'></div>系囚见徒。咸赦除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365838_comment'></div>惟十恶死罪。不在此限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365838_comment'></div>流人未达前所者放还。其有挟藏军器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365838_comment'></div>亡命山泽。百日不首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365838_comment'></div>复罪如初。敢以赦前事相告言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365838_comment'></div>以其罪罪之。内外文武官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365838_comment'></div>三品已上赐爵一等。四品已下加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365838_comment'></div>邠王守礼宁王宪岐王范薛王业各与一子三品官。公主嗣王郡主县主各与一子官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365838_comment'></div>其应文武行从官。加阶之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365838_comment'></div>并赐勋两转。三卫引驾细引黄衣长上飞骑彍骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365838_comment'></div>先有武散官者加两阶。未给武散官者各赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365838_comment'></div>卫士马主戎车主幕士掌闲供膳太常。及仗内音声人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365838_comment'></div>行署及蕃官□□并别敕杂色定名行从人。亦赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365838_comment'></div>缘大礼登山□□□从行事舆脚等官。三品已上特赐一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365838_comment'></div>仍与一子□□□已下特赐一阶。仍赐勋两转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365838_comment'></div>量与进改。其四军别□□山宿卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365838_comment'></div>及诸司上山执当官。三品己上赐爵一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365838_comment'></div>仍与一子出身。四品已下加一阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365838_comment'></div>赐勋两转。亦量与进改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365838_comment'></div>其白身人及行署蕃官放蕃选。其山下升坛行事官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365838_comment'></div>三品已上加爵一等。赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365838_comment'></div>四品已下加一阶。赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365838_comment'></div>选日稍优。诸献官及宿卫斋宫将军率中郎并郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365838_comment'></div>并两京留守诸军节度使。并同升坛例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365838_comment'></div>诸有职守押当非升坛例诸有职人加一阶。选日优量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365838_comment'></div>其加阶应入三品五品人非特赐者。并依十一年三月二十八日敕节限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365838_comment'></div>斋郎礼生见任官前资官已上人。并依资量材与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365838_comment'></div>未出身者放出身。皇亲别敕承恩陪位者亦准此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365838_comment'></div>诸州岳牧。四府长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365838_comment'></div>朝觐陪位者。泛阶之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365838_comment'></div>各赐勋一转。诸方使人及诸州父老宗姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365838_comment'></div>并从家子孙至岳不得陪位者。并赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365838_comment'></div>赐物五段。诸州及兖州道僧至岳见大礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365838_comment'></div>并赐物五段。孔子后褎圣侯量才与处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365838_comment'></div>天下致仕官。各依本品赐一季禄并束帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365838_comment'></div>其陪位者。仍赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365838_comment'></div>诸蕃侯王酋长来会礼者。各加一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365838_comment'></div>至都节级并与赐物。其入朝留在边军人亦准此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365838_comment'></div>其蕃中祗候衙官刺史县令。并赐物及袍带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365838_comment'></div>突厥可汗小杀等诸国王。守护塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365838_comment'></div>岁月朝贡。并宜赐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365838_comment'></div>副使将往。侍老年百岁已上者版授下州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365838_comment'></div>妇人版授郡君。年九十巳上者版授上州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365838_comment'></div>妇人版授县君。年七十巳上者版授县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365838_comment'></div>并妇人版级。量赐粟帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365838_comment'></div>其预见大礼侍老。各别加侍丁一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365838_comment'></div>孝子顺孙。义夫节妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365838_comment'></div>旌表门闾。终身勿事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365838_comment'></div>行人之家。及𩻴寡茕独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365838_comment'></div>并疾病不能自存者。委州县长官倍加存恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365838_comment'></div>诸军行有文武散官已上者加一阶。白身者赐散勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365838_comment'></div>欠负官物逋悬租调。并宜放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365838_comment'></div>其行过州县。供顿劬劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365838_comment'></div>并贴顿百姓。有杂差科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365838_comment'></div>并车马夫役者。并免一年租赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365838_comment'></div>兖州免二年租赋。当顿官人始末不绝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365838_comment'></div>与中上考。仍赐勋一转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365838_comment'></div>朕永惟王业。繄赖旧勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365838_comment'></div>元首股肱。其犹一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365838_comment'></div>自武德已来功臣宰辅。或名存王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365838_comment'></div>遣嗣沈沦。或身无大故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365838_comment'></div>衔屈泉壤。宜令所司访择申理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365838_comment'></div>唐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>元年六月二十六日立功官人。往属艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365838_comment'></div>能尽忠义。今成大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365838_comment'></div>何日忘之。宜各与一子出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365838_comment'></div>无子者任回与周亲之人。有司试策三道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365838_comment'></div>等第收奖。朕躬陟天门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365838_comment'></div>宿斋日观。时属严冬雪后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365838_comment'></div>初夜风寒。朕因露立祈恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365838_comment'></div>誓欲代人当咎。俯仰之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365838_comment'></div>顿息霜飙。奠献之晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365838_comment'></div>变同韶景。诚荷上天垂祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365838_comment'></div>亦赖灵山吐祥。诗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365838_comment'></div>无德不报。宜封太山神为天齐王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365838_comment'></div>礼秩加三公一等。宜令所管崇饰祠庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365838_comment'></div>环山十里。禁其樵采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365838_comment'></div>给近山二十户复。以奉神祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365838_comment'></div>率土之内。赐酺七<span class='inlineComment2'>（英华作五）</span>日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365838_comment'></div>任于村坊内宴乐。不得聚敛烦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365838_comment'></div>其节文有未沾及者。所司比类奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365838_comment'></div>其封祠有数处行事者。从一处叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365838_comment'></div>赦书日行五百里。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365838_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_120_1365838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1365838'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_100_1365838_0'>⑴ 此处隆字避玄宗讳</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1365838_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年11月14日</a>　在中书舍人任。本月甲午，登封毕，玄宗自泰山归经孔子宅。作品：《奉和圣制经孔子旧宅》<div id='poem_22760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和圣制经孔子旧宅</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年11月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22760")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22760'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22760'>孔门太山下，不见登封时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22760'>徒有先王法，今为明主思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22760'>恩加万乘幸，礼致一牢祠。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年11月16日</a>　在中书舍人任。本月丙申，致祭、赋诗，九龄等有和作。作品：《故瀛洲司马参军李府君碑铭并序》<br /></div>

开封
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=725&endYear=725')">725年12月</a>　在中书舍人任。本月自鲁还次梁宋间，九龄等献状贺太阳不亏。作品：《贺太阳不亏状》<div id='poem_1365881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺太阳不亏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（725年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365881")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365881'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365881_comment'></div>今月朔太史奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365881_comment'></div>太阳不亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365881_comment'></div>据诸家历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365881_comment'></div>皆蚀十分已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365881_comment'></div>仍带蚀出者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365881_comment'></div>今日日出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365881_comment'></div>百司瞻仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365881_comment'></div>光景无亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365881_comment'></div>臣伏以日月之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365881_comment'></div>值交必蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365881_comment'></div>算数先定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365881_comment'></div>理无推移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365881_comment'></div>今朔之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365881_comment'></div>应蚀不蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365881_comment'></div>陛下闻日有变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365881_comment'></div>斋戒精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365881_comment'></div>外宽刑政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365881_comment'></div>内广仁惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365881_comment'></div>圣德日慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365881_comment'></div>灾祥自弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365881_comment'></div>若无表应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365881_comment'></div>何谓大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365881_comment'></div>臣等不胜感庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365881_comment'></div>谨奉状陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365881_comment'></div>仍望宣付史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365881_comment'></div>以垂来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1365881_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

南京

id='poem_sentence_9_22836'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1153, "poem_sentence_9_22836")'>桑田</span>东海变，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3452, id='poem_sentence_10_22836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22836'>山虽幕府在，馆岂豫章留。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22836'>水淀还相阅，菱歌亦故遒。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22836'>雄图不足问，唯想事风流。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22836'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_22836_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
当涂
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='174a52d29fe24563808e6055e9564352_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("174a52d29fe24563808e6055e9564352");'><span id='174a52d29fe24563808e6055e9564352_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>，50岁</div><div id='174a52d29fe24563808e6055e9564352' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过当涂，江上遇疾风，有诗。作品：《江上遇疾风》<div id='poem_22887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江上遇疾风</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22887")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22887'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22887'>疾风江上起，鼓怒扬烟埃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22887'>白昼晦如夕，洪涛声若雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22887'>投林鸟铩羽，入浦鱼曝鳃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22887'>瓦飞屋且发，帆快樯已摧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22887'>不知天地气，何为此喧豗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22887'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_22887_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过当涂，江上遇疾风，有寄宣州刺史裴耀卿诗。作品：《江上使风呈裴宣州》<div id='poem_22735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江上使风呈裴宣州耀卿</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22735")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22735'>江路与天连，风帆何淼然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22735'>遥林浪出没，孤舫鸟联翩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22735'>常爱千钧重，深思万事捐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22735'>报恩非徇禄，还逐贾人船。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22735_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江

南昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年6月</a>　本月，亲祭洪州城隍神。作品：《祭洪州城隍神文》<div id='poem_1365958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭洪州城隍神文</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365958")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365958'>维开元十五年岁次丁卯六月朔壬寅十日辛亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365958_comment'></div>中散大夫使持节都督洪州诸军事洪州刺史上柱国曲江县开国男张某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365958_comment'></div>谨以清酌脯醢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365958_comment'></div>祭于城隍神之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365958_comment'></div>恭惟明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365958_comment'></div>懿皆潜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365958_comment'></div>城池是保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365958_comment'></div>民庶是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365958_comment'></div>精灵以秉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365958_comment'></div>正直攸好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365958_comment'></div>忝牧此都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365958_comment'></div>敢忘在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365958_comment'></div>道虽隔于幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365958_comment'></div>事或同于表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365958_comment'></div>今水潦所降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365958_comment'></div>亦惟其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365958_comment'></div>而淫雨不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365958_comment'></div>恐害嘉谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365958_comment'></div>谷者人之所以为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365958_comment'></div>人者神之所以为祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365958_comment'></div>祀不可以为利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365958_comment'></div>义不可以不福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365958_comment'></div>阖境山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365958_comment'></div>能致云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365958_comment'></div>岂无节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365958_comment'></div>愿达精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365958_comment'></div>以时弭灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365958_comment'></div>无或失稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365958_comment'></div>则理人有助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365958_comment'></div>是所望于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365958_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1365958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　又作荔枝赋并序，以寓身世之感。作品：《荔枝赋并序》<div id='poem_1365708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荔枝赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365708")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365708_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365708'>南海郡出荔枝焉。每至季夏。其实乃熟。状甚瑰诡。味特甘滋。百果之中。无一可比。余往在西掖。尝盛称之。诸公莫之知。固未之信。唯舍人彭城刘侯。弱年累迁。经于南海。一闻斯谈。倍复嘉叹。以为甘美之极也。又谓龙眼凡果。而与荔枝齐名。魏文帝方引蒲桃及龙眼相比。是时二方不通。传闻之大谬也。每相顾閒议。欲为赋述。而世务卒卒。此志莫就。及理郡暇日。追叙往心。夫物以不知而轻。味以无比而疑。远不可验。终然永屈。况士有未效之用。而身在无誉之閒。苟无深知。与彼亦何以异也。因道扬其实。遂作此赋。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365708'>果之美者。厥有荔枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365708_comment'></div>虽受气于震方。实禀精于火离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365708_comment'></div>乃作酸于此裔。爰负阳以从宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365708_comment'></div>蒙休和之所播。涉寒暑而匪亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365708_comment'></div>下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>合围</span>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>擢本</span>。傍荫亩而抱规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365708_comment'></div>紫纹绀理。黛缃枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365708_comment'></div>蓊郁霮䨴。环合棽丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365708_comment'></div>如盖之张。如帷之垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365708_comment'></div>云烟沃若。孔翠于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365708_comment'></div>灵根所盘。不高不卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365708_comment'></div>陋下泽之沮洳。恶层崖之崄巇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365708_comment'></div>彼前志之或妄。何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>侧生</span>之见疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365708_comment'></div>尔其勾芒在辰。凯风入律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365708_comment'></div>肇气含滋。芬敷谧溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365708_comment'></div>绿穗靡靡。青英<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>苾苾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365708_comment'></div>不丰其华。但甘其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365708_comment'></div>如有意乎敦本。故微文而妙质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365708_comment'></div>蒂药房而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>攒萃</span>。皮龙鳞以骈比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365708_comment'></div>肤玉英而含津。色江萍以吐日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365708_comment'></div>朱苞剖。明珰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365708_comment'></div>炯然数寸。犹不可匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365708_comment'></div>未玉齿而殆销。虽琼浆而可轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365708_comment'></div>彼众味之有五。此甘滋之不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365708_comment'></div>伊醇淑之无算。非精言之能悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365708_comment'></div>闻者欢而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>竦企</span>。见者讶而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>惊仡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365708_comment'></div>心恚可以蠲忿。口爽可以忘疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365708_comment'></div>且欲神于醴露。何比数于甘橘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365708_comment'></div>援蒲桃而见拟。亦古人之深失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365708_comment'></div>若乃华轩洞开。嘉宾四会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365708_comment'></div>时当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>燠煜</span>。客或烦愦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365708_comment'></div>而斯果在焉。莫不心侈而体忲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365708_comment'></div>信雕盘之仙液。实玳筵之绮缋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365708_comment'></div>有终食于累百。愈益气而理内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365708_comment'></div>故无厌于所甘。虽不贪而必爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365708_comment'></div>沈李美而莫取。浮瓜甘而自退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365708_comment'></div>岂一座之所荣。冠四时而为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365708_comment'></div>夫其贵可以荐宗庙。其珍可以羞王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365708_comment'></div>亭十里而莫致。门九重兮曷通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365708_comment'></div>山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>五峤</span>兮白云。江千里兮青枫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365708_comment'></div>何斯美之独远。嗟尔命之不逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365708_comment'></div>每被销于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>凡口</span>。䍐获知于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1365708", 1365708, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>贵躬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365708_comment'></div>柿何称乎梁侯。梨何幸乎张公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365708_comment'></div>亦因人之所遇。孰能辨乎其中哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365708_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1365708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　是年在洪州有诗。作品：《郡江南上别孙侍御》《在郡秋怀二首》《晨坐斋中偶而成咏》《临泛东湖时任洪州》（郡庭日休暇）《同藄毋学士月夜闻雁》<div id='poem_22794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_5_22914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22914'>休闲倘有素，岂负南山曲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22812'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22812'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(22812)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　本年守洪州后，还拜谒了后汉高士徐穉墓，并亲撰碣铭以表景仰之情。作品：《后汉徴君徐君碣铭并序》<div id='poem_1365945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后汉徵君徐君碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365945")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365945_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365945'>后汉高士徐君。讳稚。字孺子。南昌人也。先生受天元休。含道杰出。生知而上。贯之以一。体资清纯。动适元妙。知道之将废。乃穷而独善。躬耕取资。非力不食。邻落所处。率化无讼。在汉之季。遭时溷浊。不抗迹以庇物。故退栖山林。不苟利以辱身。故进无禄位。五辟宰府。四察孝廉。又举有道。就拜太原太守。皆辞疾不起。延嘉二年。尚书令汝南陈蕃仆射南郡胡广相与上疏。极言先生宜为辅弼。协和人神。汉桓帝犹能安车元纁。备礼徵聘。而竟不屈志。知时之不可支也。然而诸公嘉招。虽不之屑就。及闻薨卒。徒步吊祭。礼有所尚。只鸡不薄。意有所加。生刍为贵。士之感义。实衰世之有补。人而见德。俾后生之可寻。其废中权。行中虑。皆此之类也。昔者夷齐介洁而远去。沮溺野逸而离群。颜阖凿坏以遁逃。接舆狂歌而诡激。此诚作者。或类沽名。夫有所不为。志则偏也。无适不可。用之极也。先生则贬绝在心。而经修于世。纯俭以存戒。博爱以体仁。应物以会通。全巳以归正。汉庭所以宗其德。天下所以服其行。岂与彼数子直径庭而巳哉。灵帝初欲蒲轮聘。会先生以疾终。时年七十二。有子曰季登。笃行孝悌。亦高尚不仕。皇唐开元十五年。予忝牧兹郡。风流是仰。在悬榻之后。想见其人。有表墓之仪。岂孤此地。则先生之德。其可没乎。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365945'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365945'>灵芝无根，醴泉无源。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365945'>角立杰出，先生斯存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365945'>英英先生，德不可名。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365945'>麟出无应，鸿飞入冥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365945'>道高事远，迹陈名劭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365945'>勒石旧邦，以观其妙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365945'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1365945_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　本年登城南楼有诗。作品：《秋晚登楼望南江入始兴郡路》<div id='poem_22909' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　本年独处江城有诗。作品：《郡府中每晨辄见群鹤东飞至暮又行列而返噥唳云路甚和乐焉予愧独处江城常目送此意有所羡遂赋以诗》<div id='poem_22847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡中每晨兴辄见群鹤东飞至暮又行列而返哢唳云路甚和乐焉予愧独处江城常目送此意有所羡遂赋以诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_22847_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22847'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1566, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22847", 22847, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>晓日</span>东田去，烟霄北渚归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22847'>欢呼良自适，罗列好相依。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22847'>远集长江静，高翔众鸟稀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22847'>岂烦仙子驭，何畏野人机。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22847'>却念<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1566, "poem_sentence_5_22847")'>乘轩</span>者，拘留不得飞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22847'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_22847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　本年为毕公撰墓志铭。作品：《故安南副都护毕公墓志铭并序》<div id='poem_1365951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故安南副都护毕公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（727年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365951")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365951_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365951'>公讳某。字某。东平人。四世祖义云。北齐度支郎中青州刺史。曾祖炎。贞观初并州白马府右果毅都尉右卫郎将。祖义。蒲州河东令。坐事左转桂州归义县丞。因家于始安。父诚。举孝廉。高尚不仕。公即孝廉府君之子。禀灵纯茂。姿性开朗。亦既志学。休有令闻。虽在诸生之中。巳有万人之望矣。夫其忠有世。善有元。仁于其亲。友于兄弟。岂尚行所致。其因心而然。公之植身。根萌素厚。掺本制末。何适非宜。故为政之方。所从来远矣。某年初。有御史将命。黜陟幽明。公时盘桓居贞。未有攸往。而使者承式。固才是求。褐衣见召。直绳斯委。乃表公授梧州录事参军。非其好也。先是剽劫在境。行李所病。纲佐无机。逋盗肃然。岁满。授广州浈阳令。事必举。人用稳便。莫不咨嗟。未始见也。寻转韶州司马。其政如初。秩满。丁内忧。公有至性。几于毁灭。庐墓展哀。泣血扶病。有加一等。不惟三年。岭南按察使广州都督兼御史大夫萧璿。彼孝悌之士也。以锡类之故。有嘉德音。于是拔补按察判官。义行相承。终始如一。尤加钦重。特以表闻。敕授新州刺史。属恩州酋帅。日寻干戈。将有式遏。实资明允。后按察使广平郡宋璟以公为五府总管。以甲卒戍焉。虽临之兵威。而开以恩信。俾忿鸷狼戾。化枭为人。广平公深以为能。奏假恩州刺史。俄又真授。夷落大宁。寻加朝散大夫。迁端州刺史。居必致理。莫匪嘉绩。并护之寄。朝选以归。于是加秩中散大夫。拜安南副都护。到官未几。闇忽遂殂。时年六十。某月日庚子。归葬于某山原。公内行无玷。外物不干。文非务华。学皆为巳。所涖数郡。遗爱在人。全已而归。可谓厚矣。有子曰某。衔恤终天。愬哀远日。永惟称伐。存乎幽篆。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365951'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365951'>猗欤毕侯，浚源长流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365951'>受氏于毕，爰自有周。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365951'>彼美系载，实惟孙谋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365951'>贤哲继轨，斯其远猷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365951'>知实内积，行非外诱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365951'>家邦必闻，人伦归厚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365951'>微此令德，夫岂善守。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365951'>亦既从政，厥闻载荣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365951'>邑能讼息，郡用礼成。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365951'>九真副岭，万里扬旌。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365951'>护彼绝域，义忘险艰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365951'>缇律未改，丹旐而还。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=727&endYear=727')">727年</a>　本年祭故李长侍，有文。作品：《祭故李常侍文》<div id='poem_1365957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1365957_comment'></div>谨遣仓曹参军李某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365957_comment'></div>以脯醢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365957_comment'></div>敬祭于故宋国公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365957_comment'></div>惟公代载贤杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365957_comment'></div>天资忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365957_comment'></div>外圭组而虽华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365957_comment'></div>内冰镜而无垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365957_comment'></div>善常不伐。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1365957_comment'></div>五福云欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365957_comment'></div>生涯溘尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365957_comment'></div>精魄何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365957_comment'></div>日欤月欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365957_comment'></div>有荣有凋。<div class='inline' href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365709")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365709_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365709'>臣伏见景寅制书。以开元历握乾符垂示天下。幸甚。其沙门元侃等所言益部耆旧传。洛下闳改颛顼历。推校最为精密。而曰后八百岁。其历差一日。当有圣人定之。到于今。历果有差。圣果有定。诚非常之嘉应。旷代之灵符。不可得而间也。臣诚欢诚喜。臣闻天道先圣而启期。圣人后天而奉时。不当乎天心。不在历数。不登乎圣道。不合元符。元命定而王者应。幽数起而明者察。故洛下闳极其数而知来。耆旧传尚其占而示后。我皇帝无思而感。自然元同。僧元侃等幸会而言。岂云素虑。非人事也。非神道也。天固已储祥以俟时。积分以差日。出入数代。多历年所。畴人极力。不能课其祥。上林杂候。亦莫徵其失。则明天意。以徯圣期。期数未臻。乃藏于密。圣證将至。如应如响。彼幽深之何有。此会通之不谋。所以下叶黄钟。上稽历象。以和六气。以合三光。复其见心。间不容发。斗枢且运。而况于人时。元气巳调。而况于月令。于戏。天下之动。日用不知。昆虫草木。生者自遂。麟凤龟龙。灵者自瑞。蛮夷戎狄。远无不至。山川鬼神。幽罔不洎。此圣人所以定天下之象。通天下之志。而天人之道备矣。昔者河出图。洛出书。自时厥后。符命非一。空文而无应。其殆乎人为。实录而有徵。焉用乎龙负。则洛下闳者。此其神乎。不然。是何见之明也。夫圣有时而不作。物无圣而不睹。仲尼感时于凤鸟。古人叹寿于河清。皆伤于不达。而恨于难见。我后受成命。重光乎文武。累圣而无穷。殊祥而无数。彼哀命之者。曾不得而朝闻。凡今之人。抑何幸而目睹。由是观之。当其来运。唐虞之屋可封。非其有时。孔邱之徒不遇。此千载之会也。万物岂知其谢生于天乎。兆人亦云忘力于帝乎。微臣荷宠灵。扬休命。则臣子之忠。在于尽美。而惟天之大。终莫能名。不胜区区。敢献颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365709'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365709'>于皇惟后，受命于天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365709'>时来于今，兆是厥先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365709'>既定乃日，允叶斯年。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365709'>赫赫光明，应于上元。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365709'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1365709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　在洪州刺史任。春中，给事中严挺之致函九龄，劝其不必汲汲子声名，并约以淡泊无为之言。九龄遂有复函，坦陈全身远害之心迹。作品：《答严给事书》<div id='poem_1365919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答严给事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（729年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365919")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365919'>自出江郡。慰诲累及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365919_comment'></div>情义已积。昆弟无喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365919_comment'></div>人生相知。可谓厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365919_comment'></div>仆方请归养。从此告辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365919_comment'></div>会面无期。所怀当尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365919_comment'></div>故复累而言之耳。凡为前相所厚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365919_comment'></div>岂必恶人耶。仆爰自书生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365919_comment'></div>燕公待以族子。颇以文章见许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365919_comment'></div>不因势利而合。但推奖之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365919_comment'></div>不量不才。引致掖垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365919_comment'></div>有负时议。然则初有超拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365919_comment'></div>岂由本心。嗷嗷之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365919_comment'></div>曾不是察。既不称其服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365919_comment'></div>又加之谗閒。负乘致寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365919_comment'></div>几于不免。当此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365919_comment'></div>若无所容。以孤特之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365919_comment'></div>处背憎之地。自怪既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365919_comment'></div>何幸而全。追想寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365919_comment'></div>恍恍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1365919", 1365919, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>发悸</span>。严子足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365919_comment'></div>不意而然。既而远出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365919_comment'></div>犹有馀衅。巧言潜搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365919_comment'></div>期仆倾危。故使者之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365919_comment'></div>怒于心而色于事。赖于自慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365919_comment'></div>幸且无咎。不者吹毛洗垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365919_comment'></div>求其痕疵。势穷力屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365919_comment'></div>将无控告。未始怯事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365919_comment'></div>有为而然。以故春中有书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365919_comment'></div>薄言求庇。足下犹不谅此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365919_comment'></div>以为汲汲于声名。而乃约以庄生之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365919_comment'></div>博以东山之法。晓导精至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365919_comment'></div>诚故人之情。向之所防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365919_comment'></div>有异来旨。彼二教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365919_comment'></div>忘情灭识。无有缠爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365919_comment'></div>故福至不喜。祸至不忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365919_comment'></div>今仆养亲。岂复割离恩爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365919_comment'></div>直措心于此地哉。正欲惟疾之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365919_comment'></div>全身远害。故虽在小小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365919_comment'></div>敢不兢兢。至如自放身心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365919_comment'></div>虽复懵昧。幸受教于君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365919_comment'></div>亦闻道于古人。岂不能少有所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365919_comment'></div>方复屑屑于毁誉之际也。管仲尝三战三北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365919_comment'></div>而鲍子不以为无勇。以其有亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365919_comment'></div>足下宁不我知。而有此诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365919_comment'></div>且往者不自量力。因缘小技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365919_comment'></div>蹩躠干进。荏苒历年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365919_comment'></div>固以为运属盛明。朝多君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365919_comment'></div>义能容物。而忘其孤陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365919_comment'></div>则不知弊帚之贵。末路多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365919_comment'></div>今专典一州。盖幸遇已甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365919_comment'></div>而平生万事。为寒暑所移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365919_comment'></div>虽忝簪缨。若坠泉壑者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365919_comment'></div>诚耻令名之不副宠章也。昔贾谊才偕管晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365919_comment'></div>言则霸王。名重汉廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365919_comment'></div>官止梁傅。班固犹云未为不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365919_comment'></div>况仆拟非其伦。遇已过彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365919_comment'></div>顾多惭色。岂敢怨而更求欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365919_comment'></div>足下知心。当明义有所在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365919_comment'></div>尊者慈爱诸下。怀宁本乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365919_comment'></div>不欲随官。重有离别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365919_comment'></div>春秋高矣。晨昏久违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365919_comment'></div>仆岂复规规然徼无妄之福。在悔吝之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365919_comment'></div>而迥无所恃。单孑独立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365919_comment'></div>万一蹉跌。或远庭闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365919_comment'></div>朝心不开。暮发尽白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365919_comment'></div>行已五十。独不知命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365919_comment'></div>是以冒死抗疏。乞归侍药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365919_comment'></div>一则洁膳以展下情。二则辞满而无贻忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365919_comment'></div>周易曰。飞鸟遗之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365919_comment'></div>不宜上宜下。盖取此义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365919_comment'></div>亦自卜者审也。顾恨上负明主邱山之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365919_comment'></div>未有涓尘之答。下愧知己契奖之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365919_comment'></div>卒无如言之效。又平生不饰小节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365919_comment'></div>苟取虚名。使吠声之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365919_comment'></div>退有后议。竟未获尽展所有之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365919_comment'></div>以塞罔极之谗。碌碌而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365919_comment'></div>不能不耿耿耳。古人有从所好者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365919_comment'></div>仆亦有心。庶承颜之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365919_comment'></div>放性自适。轩冕之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365919_comment'></div>亦云傥来。林泽之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365919_comment'></div>聊足<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1365919", 1365919, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>散虑</span>。纵绝后望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365919_comment'></div>亦了一生。何必崎岖不平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365919_comment'></div>龃龉求入。然后为得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365919_comment'></div>去矣严子。勉事圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365919_comment'></div>傥存平仲久要之言。无惜诗人金玉之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365919_comment'></div>幸甚。张九龄白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365919_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_85_1365919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　在洪州刺史任。秋，在郡舍南园畦杂树间却步怀想，聊以永日，有诗纪之。作品：《郡舍南有园畦杂树聊以永日》<div id='poem_22849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22849' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　在洪州刺史任。秋，复有秋怀诗。作品：《秋怀》<div id='poem_22908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_22908'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22908'>感惜芳时换，谁知客思悬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22908'>东南起归望，何处是江天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22908'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22908_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　在洪州刺史任。冬，应徐峻、徐峤、徐三兄弟之请，为其父徐坚撰神道碑。作品：《大唐故光禄大夫右散骑常侍集贤院学士赠太子少保东海徐文公神道碑》<div id='poem_1365939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐故光禄大夫右散骑常侍集贤院学士赠太子少保东海徐文公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（729年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365939")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365939_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365939'>夫物之所宗也。莫善乎德行。道之以明也。莫先乎文学。人伦以具体为难。世业以济美为贵。有能兼之者。其东海公乎。公讳坚。字元固。其先东海郯人。永嘉之后。仕业南国。因家吴兴焉。隋氏平陈。徙族入雍。今为冯翊人也。原其伯翳平水土。实佐文命。偃王行仁义。大启徐方。因国保姓。克昌厥后。逮乎汉魏。间出仁贤。十二代祖晋江州刺史顺德侯宁。至五代祖梁直阁将军慈源侯整。整生陈始安太守综。综生隋延州临真令方贵。方贵生唐果州刺史孝德。孝德生唐西台舍人赠礼部尚书齐聃。出入六朝。载祀数百。文武冠冕。存殁光灵。训子克家。谋孙必复。贤风儒行。世有其人。公即尚书府君之元子也。生而浚发。默识经艺。粤自童龀。则善文言。时先府君为沛王侍读。公之岐嶷。声振平台。王闻而延伫。与之谈议。授能赋。博奕惟贤。门客府寮。深所厌服。奄遭不造。十四而孤。祖母金城郡君姜太夫人。念其聪异。诲以志学。公遂刻勉。诣心精微。磅礡九流。激昂三变。景倩幼露。实赖悯孙。令伯大成。抑由祖母。上元中。遭姜太夫人丧。哀几灭性。制则从礼。有感斯绝。无声常泪。服阕。州辟秀才。其年登科。解巾补汾州参军事。部送边糈。至于定襄。军使王本立。素重公才。署为管记。书奏谋算。悉以咨之。坐耀锋铓。未尝肯綮。寻而换云阳尉万年主簿。亲累出为杨府功曹。振鳞将抟。载跃京毂。垂翼远逝。有声东南。俄迁太子文学。时秘阁群籍。大抵讹谬。有敕召学士详定。公实在焉。为之刊缉。卷盈二万。时辈绝倒。服其博达。寻与李峤等撰三教珠英。书成奏御。拜司封员外。寻加朝散大夫。即拜郎中。稍迁给事中。以公代及文史。词不失旧。虽居琐闼。尚比缠牵。遂除中书舍人。君子曰。舜之官人也。二年。敕公修则天圣后实录及文集等绝笔。中宗嘉之。玺书敦慰。赐爵慈源县子。赉物五百段。旌良史也。迁刑部侍郎。加秩银青光禄大夫。转礼部侍郎兼判户部。公久践朝廷。累登省阁。旧章必练。即事无疑。雅不烦文。深得大体。云台高议。以此归之。进封县伯。食邑五百户。兼昭文馆学士。受诏与天竺僧菩提流志译宝积经。及柳冲等同修姓氏系录。三教宝真。万族有伦。亟见成矣。太平公主内秉国权。驸马武攸暨外收人望。命公至第。拒而不行。恶夫佞也。景云初。今上夷乱。主鬯东朝。宫相四员。时难其选。二以宰臣兼领。一则天子故人。任良两宫。实在公矣。遂除右庶子兼崇文馆学士。修史如故。进爵东海郡公。食邑二千户。迁右散骑常侍。以本官兼黄门侍郎。寻而即真。禄赐同三品。爵崇五等。道茂两宫。利君谋身。举代皆誉。又以删定格令。承恩进爵二等。公请回授叔父齐庄。帝用怀之。遂封齐庄为长城县子。天下义士。莫不激昂焉。侍中岑羲。公之姻娅。与其联事。深自危惧。求典閒司。以远祗悔。遂改太子詹事。迨羲祸败。地绝嫌疑。先是不交定王。及此不眤岑氏。见炎莫附。思患预防。信达人也。复以亲累出为绛州。历永蕲棣衢四郡。山川分位。楚夏异齐。公政不易宜。教以因俗。德化归厚。人共由之。开元中。会同京师。迁秘书监。无何。转国子祭酒。皇帝稽古崇训。开堂集儒。以公才学元长。命登首席。遂令集贤殿修撰。又除右常侍。以公为学士。副丞相燕公知院事。绸缪顾问。日月献纳。恩渥尤及。少有其比。上将柴于岱宗。诏公草其仪注。定禋祀之位。广配类之仪。博文约礼。或沿或革。言出而人伏。事立而天从。时议远矣。及礼毕。承恩特加光禄大夫。时置十铨。公在分掌。程不愆素。且无遗才。公既赞相谟。犹从容讽议。大钟必谏。温树不言。启沃尽规。实致君于尧舜。死生有命。空比德于老彭。享年若干。以开元十七年龙集己巳五月丁酉。薨于长安颁政里之私第。圣人震悼。君子称嗟。翌日。有诏褎赠太子少保。赠物若干段。粟若干石。特遣中使内侍伊凤祥吊祭。而别赐布帛若干端匹。俾鸿胪少卿元复监护葬事。官给鼓吹仪仗。太常考行曰文。君子曰。仁而爱人。敏而好学。家有荣业。绍其弓冶。国有大事。修其典章。谥之曰文。不亦宜乎。其年冬甲子。与夫人故南阳郡夫人合葬于万年县之少陵原先茔。礼也。公宽裕有礼。温良能断。智出于象外。枢得其环中。行之积也厚。名之立也大。故起自黄绶。累践赤墀。五省推高。连州得最。事将时并。位与才偕。莫之天阏也。至于升堂入室。探微睹奥。动有礼乐之运。言有雅颂之声。是惟无作。作则万物和而八音备矣。盖尝注史记。修晋书。续文选大隐传。及有文集三十卷。皆资于故实。博于遗训。古今通变。河汉共高。或藏名山。或升天府。亹亹然各得其所。呜呼。文仲殁而其言立。子产终而遗爱存。公则备焉。宜受戬谷。保艾厥后。代代守之。有子曰峻峤嵬等。才以雅著。孝以特闻。学茂高曾之科旨。词雄祖考之风格。备历清贯。皆立能名。三贤德声。方贾氏无愧。累叶儒训。与班门孰多。咸瞿瞿如。皇皇如。昊天不追。终身积痛。求旧撰实。勒诸坟道。仆从述者之后。敬而伸之。乃为铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365939'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365939'>舜命益虞，畴功帝俞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365939'>偃行文教，代集通儒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365939'>光华<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365939", 1365939, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>鼎阀</span>，出入秦吴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365939'>门多长者，君其最乎<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_1365939_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365939'>曾是好学，果行洵美。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365939'>日就鳞成，风积鹏起。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365939'>黄绶覆篑，朱门方轨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365939'>官籍正人，朝称良史<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_1365939_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365939'>三入承明，五迁外郡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365939'>道有出处，心齐喜愠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1365939'>帝思启沃，国尚师训。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365939'>屡献箴规，偏承顾问<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365939_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365939'>居常有异，博而无惑。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365939'>绵蕝孙通，铨衡叔则。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1365939'>为龟为镜，立言立德。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1365939'>胡不慭遗，左右王国<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365939_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1365939'>悼兴冕旒，哀结衣簪。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1365939'>官供羽仗，士惜人琴。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1365939'>巳矣终古，平生德音。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1365939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1365939'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1365939", 1365939, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>松枝挂剑</span>，碑字生金<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365939_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1365939'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1365939_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=729&endYear=729')">729年</a>　在洪州刺史任。为高力士夫人之祖吕处贞撰碑铭。作品：《赠庆王友东平吕府君碑铭》<div id='poem_1365942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐赠庆王友东平吕府君碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（729年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365942")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365942_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365942'>夫官虽序贤。志道者不常有位。才虽屈命。福善者未必无后。子夏文学之达。以为富贵在天。于公决曹之平。则云子孙由我。盖不享当代。生数犹奇。流庆后人。互体乃用。亨之会也。盖有原焉。公讳处贞。字虔求。东平人。曾祖北齐幽州长史府君讳赟。祖隋贯州中正府君讳伽。考渝州清池令府君讳师。昔伯夷佐唐。实典三礼。四岳佐禹。用平九州。虞夏以功而见封。申吕因邑而命氏。惟时厥后。奕代丕承。公正性之有自来。直道之不充诎。嘉勇退之乂德。避近名之未然。越在弱龄。栖迟事外。用光本于藏曜。履行期于灭迹。不远于仁。行之斯至。不苟于义。方之自正。佐一郡而即安。居九夷而匪陋。始不然者。公何掾于东裔哉。起家授元州司户参军。晏如也。言旋初服。遂从所好。外物之槩。不离于风尘。远子之言。惟闻于诗礼。所谓温良淑慎。无竞伊人者欤。天册二年夏四月。遇疾终于家。春秋五十有二。开元十四年冬十一月。葬于邑城西南四里原。夫人北地傅氏祔焉。夫果于立诚。静以俟命。力不足者则不疚。运不至者则不忧。物情之难。及我而易。是以名利众之所欲也。公则澹泊之。德义人之所鲜也。亦克蹈籍之。如此而神不劳。福不流。未之有也。有四子。长曰元知。今左威卫司戈。次曰元悟。中散大夫使持节鄜州诸军事守鄜州刺史。次曰元智。左威卫执戟。次曰元爽。左卫长上。惟元悟至大官。此其教忠有旧。服义无斁。好爵是与。馀庆所贻。入为王门之长。出居邦伯之列。属恩推子贵。名彰身后。事有光于冥漠。德乃发于馨香。三命为大夫。百代称先子。孝理所赐。邦族为荣。开元十七年。有制赠公庆王友。夫人赠河间郡君。异人之符。至是斯验。惟神之鉴。谓之不欺。公之女孙曰东平郡夫人。冠军大将军右监门卫大将军渤海高公之夫人。鄜州刺史之女也。冰玉相辉。椒兰同馥。由福履于君子。与嘉会于善人。齐姜于归。鱼轩华以照路。鄜畤之往。熊戟殷其若雷。有车服而始大。履霜露而追远。于戏。食于旧德。无忝尔之奉先。树之休声。有以见其归美。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365942'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365942'>赫赫我祖，惟师尚父。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365942'>泱泱大风，悠悠终古。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365942'>施于礽裔，宪是文武。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365942'>我美其济，我则斯取。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365942'>虽匪高位，亦惟硕德。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365942'>我王之友，彼夫之特。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365942'>既贞且亮，宜语而默。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365942'>投足皆安，终身不忒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365942'>峨峨积善，以福后人。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365942'>肸蚃家庆，炜煌宗姻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1365942'>瞻彼松槚，锡之丝纶。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1365942'>今也追饰，实为先臣。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1365942'>先臣伊何，宜其有后。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1365942'>志之所尚，义无所苟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1365942'>身虽既没，名岂虚受。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1365942'>立德在兹，亦云不朽。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1365942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1365942'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　任洪州刺史至是年七月。春，有戏题春意诗。作品：《戏题春意》<div id='poem_22733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏题春意</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22733")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22733_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22733'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10818, "poem_allusion_22733")'>朱丝直</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22733'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22733'>一作江南守，江林三四春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22733'>相鸣不及鸟，相乐喜关人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22733'>日守<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10818, "poem_sentence_2_22733")'>朱丝直</span>，年催华发新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22733'>淮阳秪有卧，持此度芳辰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22733'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年4月8日</a>　此日加大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　是年，洪州得白鹿，九龄表献之。作品：《洪州进白鹿表》<div id='poem_1365846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州进白鹿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365846")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365846'>臣闻圣法天则。至理调于元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365846_comment'></div>天表圣则。嘉瑞托于群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365846_comment'></div>将以幽赞王泽。觉悟生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365846_comment'></div>知至德之所感。如虚响之必应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365846_comment'></div>伏见开元神武皇帝陛下道孚神化。体合乾行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365846_comment'></div>品物所资。太和罔不叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365846_comment'></div>图谍所载。殊祥罔不臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365846_comment'></div>故郡国上言。日月相继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365846_comment'></div>臣所部豫章县。某月某日获白鹿一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365846_comment'></div>休气所集。灵质自呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365846_comment'></div>欲效符祉。易为驯狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365846_comment'></div>臣谨按瑞应图云。王者明惠及下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365846_comment'></div>则白鹿见。又按孝经援神契云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365846_comment'></div>王者德至鸟兽。则白鹿见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365846_comment'></div>盖鹿者仙寿之物。实为祯祥之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365846_comment'></div>虽时和岁稔。固不假于羽毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365846_comment'></div>而天意人事。诚欲伸于耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365846_comment'></div>臣不胜感庆之至。谨诣某所奉瑞鹿表进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365846_comment'></div>臣诚欢诚喜顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365846_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　在洪州任上。秋夕望月，有诗。作品：《秋夕望月》《望月怀远》<div id='poem_22783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋夕望月</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22783")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22783'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22783'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_22783", 22783, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>清迥</span>江城月，流光万里同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22783'>所思如梦里，相望在庭中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22783'>皎洁青苔露，萧条黄叶风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22783'>含情不得语，频使桂华空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22783'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22783'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(22783)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_22801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望月怀远</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22801")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_22801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22801'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22801'>海上生明月，天涯共此时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22801'>情人怨遥夜，竟夕起相思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22801'>灭烛怜光满，披衣觉露滋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22801'>不堪盈手赠，还寝梦佳期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22801'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_22801'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(22801)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　在洪州任上。在洪州，又应前任都督赵金穀之请托，为其父故辰州泸溪令赵公撰铭并序。作品：《故辰州泸溪令赵公碣铭并序》<div id='poem_1365946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故辰州泸溪令赵公碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365946")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365946_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365946'>有唐泸溪令晋国赵君。讳某。字某。终于其位。呜呼。鲁史既没。称行者不在兹乎。荀孟以来。论命者亦何谓也。放其言而无苟。作合乃迁。行其志而不回。与权必遂。故道每屈于位。身必后于时。而犹守真不夺。固穷自若。立诚者既独其所善。尚德者徒随而为名。名非欲彰。以美实而自著。位非欲下。以属守而遂卑。此由命而然欤。为自我而然欤。无代无之。而今实续之矣。公太祖旴。北齐河间太守。因家于饶阳。亦既重代。今为饶阳人也。曾祖北齐幽州大总管。大父隋钜鹿大中正府君。烈考范阳令府君。皆累行积庆。以贻于后。正性直道。遂钟于公。公刚洁不群。精明独断。非义所在。不以利污名。非礼所安。不以迹伤教。有立卓尔。童丱而然。既学大成。纷纶博综。将求禄养也。而俯就乡举。寻而明经登科。补太子正字。又改射洪尉。皆以逮亲自乞。执政哀之。遂屈换定襄尉。公欣然而捧檄矣。秩满。转洪洞主簿永城丞。时县宰败类。公止之不可。虽尽同官之心。且急下人之病。义形于色。彼用我雠。此贪而无亲。难与心竞。公刚亦不吐。乃迈力争。迄用上闻。因而坐免。邑中黔庶。莫不咨嗟。求而得仁。退则无愠矣。乃返初服。遨游坟索。精义致用。清风被物。或太守咨访。偃息自若。或诸儒稽疑。废疾皆起。是时中书侍郎河东辥元超。人伦之表也。将命河朔。实举废滞。企我休风。延以殊礼。立谭体要。大见嗟称。以故表闻。其庶乎在帝心。会有阴忌之谮。实为无妄之祸矣。进既曾母致疑。退而贾生投吊。不无故也。以此左迁泸溪丞。公竟不自列。穷则体命。虽在幽闇。鬼神不欺。苟推忠诚。蛮貊何陋。时县无长史。政则我由。未岁月而已成。无溪谷而不悦。互乡自专之子。左言难晓之民。翕然同辞。乞为父母。于是诣阙投疏。至于再三。朝廷允之。则授泸溪令。公聿副诚请。增修德化。乃邹鲁设教。而夷楚变风。迨公迁殂。阖境号慕。古人遗爱。何以加也。遗令戒子留葬洛阳。斯又不恋本达也。有子曰瑝。历官侍御史尚书郎洪州都督。霜露既变。则感念以时。陵谷有迁。而音徽何代。君子所惧。于斯撰德。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365946'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365946'>洛赵侯之德，好是正直。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365946'>令仪令则，不回不忒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365946'>寔邦之选，彼夫之特。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365946'>玉坚而折，膏明自煎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365946'>辰阳于远，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365946", 1365946, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>溆浦</span>回邅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1365946'>下邑巳矣，君子歼旃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1365946'>遗令桐乡，归魂崇芒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1365946'>瞻彼有洛，维水泱泱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1365946'>德音不已，于是扬扬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1365946'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1365946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年7月3日</a>　此日，转桂州刺史，当管经略使、兼岭南按察使、摄御史中丞、借紫金鱼袋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　离洪州，有南还江上作。作品：《至豫章南还江上作》<div id='poem_22738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
