id='poem_sentence_12_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22930'>朝闻循诚节，夕饮蒙瘴疠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_22930'>义疾耻无勇，盗憎攻亦锐。<div id='poem_sentence_14_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_22930'>葵藿是倾心，豺狼何反噬。<div id='poem_sentence_15_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_22930'>履险甘所受，劳贤恧相曳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_22930'>揽辔但荒服，循陔便私第。<div id='poem_sentence_17_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_22930'>嘉庆始获申，恩华复相继。<div id='poem_sentence_18_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_22930'>无庸我先举，同事君犹滞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_22930'>当推奉使绩，且结拜亲契。<div id='poem_sentence_20_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_22930'>更延怀安旨，曾是虑危际。<div id='poem_sentence_21_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_22930'>善谋虽若兹，至理焉可替。<div id='poem_sentence_22_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_22930'>所杖有神道，况承明主惠。<div id='poem_sentence_23_22930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_22930'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_22930_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桂林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f9834ec75cd24d2591a8fa44e79b7ee7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9834ec75cd24d2591a8fa44e79b7ee7");'><span id='f9834ec75cd24d2591a8fa44e79b7ee7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=731')">730-731年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='f9834ec75cd24d2591a8fa44e79b7ee7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　沿桂江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　沿漓水。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=730&endYear=730')">730年</a>　至桂州任所，有祭舜庙文。作品：《祭舜庙文》<div id='poem_1365955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭舜庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（730年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365955")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365955'>维某月朔日。中散大夫使持节都督桂州诸军事守桂州刺史兼当管经略使岭南道按察使摄御史中丞佩紫金鱼袋上柱国曲江县开国男张某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365955_comment'></div>敢昭告于大舜之灵。惟神以大孝而崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365955_comment'></div>以大圣而奋庸。以至公而有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365955_comment'></div>以至均而一海内。故不以荒服之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365955_comment'></div>不以黄屋之尊。巡守而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365955_comment'></div>殂落于此。倦勤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365955_comment'></div>永结于黎庶。惠怀之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365955_comment'></div>长存于寿宫。载祀虽遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365955_comment'></div>威灵如在。今圣朝绍兴至道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365955_comment'></div>悯兹远人。爰遣使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365955_comment'></div>按理边俗。惟神幽鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365955_comment'></div>愿表微诚。若私僻为谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365955_comment'></div>公忠有替。明鉴是殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365955_comment'></div>俾无远图。如悉心在公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365955_comment'></div>惟力是视。当福而不福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365955_comment'></div>为善者惧矣。今至止之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365955_comment'></div>辄诣陈诚。伏惟神道聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365955_comment'></div>亮斯钦畏。愿俯垂冥祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365955_comment'></div>俾输力明时。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365955_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365955_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　任桂州刺史兼岭南道按察使至本年三月。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　春，自桂州任所出巡按察岭南诸州，有自漓水南行诗。作品：《巡按自漓水南行》<div id='poem_22880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>巡按自漓水南行</a><span class='authorDate'>（731年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22880")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22880'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22880'>理棹虽云远，饮冰宁有惜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22880'>况乃佳山川，怡然傲潭石。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22880'>奇峰岌前转，茂树隈中积。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22880'>猿鸟声自呼，风泉气相激。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22880'>目因诡容逆，心与清晖涤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22880'>纷吾谬执简，行郡将移檄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22880'>即事聊独欢，素怀岂兼适。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22880'>悠悠咏靡盬，庶以穷日夕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22880'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_22880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年3月7日</a>　此日，制授守秘书少监兼集贤院学士副知院事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
荆州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79d58d519f1746bb9c91841a1ced4ba4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79d58d519f1746bb9c91841a1ced4ba4");'><span id='79d58d519f1746bb9c91841a1ced4ba4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=739')">737-739年</a>，60-62岁</div><div id='79d58d519f1746bb9c91841a1ced4ba4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年5月8日</a>　五月八日驰抵荆州后,即拟表谢罪,并详述荐周子谅一事之原委。以为绝无私协、坐贬衔冤。表讫,托请河西经略判官所部朝议郎法曹参军苏锐奉陈。作品：《荆州谢上表》<div id='poem_1365843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荆州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（737年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365843")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365843'>臣九龄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365843_comment'></div>伏奉四月十四日制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365843_comment'></div>授臣荆州大都督府长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365843_comment'></div>闻命<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365843", 1365843, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>皇怖</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365843_comment'></div>魂胆飞越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365843_comment'></div>即日戒路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365843_comment'></div>星夜奔驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365843_comment'></div>属小道使多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365843_comment'></div>驿马先少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365843_comment'></div>以今月八日至州礼上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365843_comment'></div>诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365843_comment'></div>臣不即饮气取死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365843_comment'></div>岂敢辄惜馀命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365843_comment'></div>伏念心无党恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365843_comment'></div>死则似同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365843_comment'></div>以此偷生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365843_comment'></div>犹希圣察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365843_comment'></div>臣往年按察岭表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365843_comment'></div>便道赴使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365843_comment'></div>访闻周子谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365843_comment'></div>久经推覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365843_comment'></div>遥即奏充判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365843_comment'></div>寻属臣改官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365843_comment'></div>使亦有替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365843_comment'></div>其后信安郡王祎奏将朔方驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365843_comment'></div>便请授官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365843_comment'></div>臣因其岭外勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365843_comment'></div>因而奏乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365843_comment'></div>事不敢隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365843_comment'></div>未至涉私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365843_comment'></div>然进用非人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365843_comment'></div>诚宜得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365843_comment'></div>但臣特蒙拔擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365843_comment'></div>出自宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365843_comment'></div>陛下所用隐微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365843_comment'></div>惟臣而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365843_comment'></div>伏思报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365843_comment'></div>窃恃圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365843_comment'></div>每于事端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365843_comment'></div>无所防避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365843_comment'></div>智识虽浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365843_comment'></div>罄竭则深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365843_comment'></div>微诚区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365843_comment'></div>义有所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365843_comment'></div>岂复与此私协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365843_comment'></div>以负累圣鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365843_comment'></div>臣虽至顽至愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365843_comment'></div>不至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365843_comment'></div>皇天后土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365843_comment'></div>照臣血诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365843_comment'></div>夙夜烦冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365843_comment'></div>欲辨无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365843_comment'></div>臣闻物有穷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365843_comment'></div>必诉于昊天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365843_comment'></div>人有痛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365843_comment'></div>必呼于父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365843_comment'></div>臣今孤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365843_comment'></div>不乞哀于圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365843_comment'></div>岂蒙恶声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365843_comment'></div>遂衔冤以没代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365843_comment'></div>臣受性愚钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365843_comment'></div>闇于知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365843_comment'></div>禀命舛剥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365843_comment'></div>与此凶会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365843_comment'></div>诚合自死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365843_comment'></div>以谢天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365843_comment'></div>所以侧息苟存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365843_comment'></div>臣为圣朝所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365843_comment'></div>既极荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365843_comment'></div>而一朝至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365843_comment'></div>恐玷明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365843_comment'></div>在臣微生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365843_comment'></div>有若蝼蚁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365843_comment'></div>身名俱灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365843_comment'></div>诚不足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365843_comment'></div>今衅咎则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365843_comment'></div>恩礼犹重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365843_comment'></div>面目有腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365843_comment'></div>夙夜唯忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365843_comment'></div>戴盆望天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365843_comment'></div>岂期上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365843_comment'></div>又未能宣布圣泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365843_comment'></div>少答殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365843_comment'></div>跼蹐兢皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365843_comment'></div>动失次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365843_comment'></div>无任荷惧兢悚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365843_comment'></div>谨附河西经略判官所部朝义郎法曹参军苏锐奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365843_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365843_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1365843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　有登荆州城楼等诗作,抒发其江城自拘、时来易失之优伤和孤愤之情。作品：《登荆州城楼》《登荆州城楼望江二首》<div id='poem_22861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登荆州城楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（737年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22861")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22861_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22861'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4862, "poem_allusion_22861")'>金门</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6547, "poem_allusion_22861")'>宁武愚</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7361, "poem_allusion_22861")'>王陵戆</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22861'>天宇何其旷，江城坐自拘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22861'>层楼百馀尺，迢递在西隅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22861'>暇日时登眺，荒郊临故都。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22861'>累累见陈迹，寂寂想雄图。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22861'>古往山川在，今来郡邑殊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22861'>北疆虽入郑，东距岂防吴。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22861'>几代传荆国，当时敌陕郛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22861'>上流空有处，中土复何虞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22861'>枕席夷三峡，关梁豁五湖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22861'>承平无异境，守隘莫论夫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22861'>自罢<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4862, "poem_sentence_10_22861")'>金门</span>籍，来参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_22861", 22861, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>竹使符</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22861'>端居向林薮，微尚在桑榆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22844'>焚香忏在昔，礼足誓来今。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22844'>灵异若有对，神仙真可寻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22844'>藓驳经行处，猿啼燕坐林。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　又与孟浩然、裴迪等游观古楚遺迹,猎纪南城、泊渚宫、登当阳城楼,聊遣胸中块垒。作品：《郢城西北有大古塚数十观其封域多是楚时诸王而年代久远不复可识唯直西有樊妃塚因后人为植松柏故行路尽知之》<div id='poem_22850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_5_22906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年</a>　又有感遇诗,更为深广地总结和反思了自己的仕宦生涯及人生操守。作品：《感遇十二首》<div id='poem_22804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感遇十二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_22804'>持此谢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_22804", 22804, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>高鸟</span>，因之传远情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22804'>日夕怀空意，人谁感至精。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22929_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22929'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_22929_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年1月</a>　是年在荆州长史任。正月，接玄宗春郊礼成推恩制书，遂上贺赦表，并因所部送永王俸料官当阳县主簿陈琇奉表以闻。作品：《贺赦表》<div id='poem_1365844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（738年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365844")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365844'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365844'>臣言。伏奉今月八日制恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365844_comment'></div>春郊展礼。惟新布泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365844_comment'></div>臣闻古之王政。虽在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365844", 1365844, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>方册</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365844_comment'></div>将崇旧典。必俟圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365844_comment'></div>伏惟开元神武皇帝陛下德合天明。道高帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365844_comment'></div>以为春者发生之气。气者含育之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365844_comment'></div>事乃重于岁始。礼故亲于东郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365844_comment'></div>振绝代之纲。作名王之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365844_comment'></div>布泽行庆。昭德顺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365844_comment'></div>以合阴阳之和。以乘天地之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365844_comment'></div>凡在品汇。莫不昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365844_comment'></div>臣待罪荆南。亦滥承恩赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365844_comment'></div>臣无任欣庆战荷之至。谨因所部送永王俸料官当阳县主簿陈琇奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365844_comment'></div>臣诚欢诚喜顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365844_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1365844_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　钱起至荆州，与九龄有诗唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　夏，司勋员外郎萧诚使荆考课，九龄得会友人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年7月22日</a>　此日，封始兴县开国伯，食邑五百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　秋，与郡司马崔颂有诗唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　宋之望为宋鼎绘写真图，请九龄为赞。依所请，有赞并序。作品：《宋使君写真图赞并序》<div id='poem_1365935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋使君写真图赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（739年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_1365935")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1365935_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1365935'>夫形者。神明之表。而动用之应也。察之苟至。则珠玉虽蕴。光辉必兆于山泉。而眉睫可知。贤达亦徵于骨象。如宋公之天姿森挺。人望俨然。一睹清扬。不俟深鉴。是犹鸡群见鹤。象齿非牛。居然有差。此其殊特者也。声闻如彼。风格又尔。宁有陈平之美。更虞子羽失之耶。虽妄庸之目。素非知公者。偶见斯状。亦已明其瑰异焉。初公举茂才。历长安尉。三为御史。再入尚书郎。色庄以立朝。则百僚所惮。言扬于伏奏。则三台为表。而竟以出守。俄复从边。其故何哉。由抗直之为患也。然公处屯而必行其道。居陋而不改其度。能贞其节。可谓君子哉。才为国而生。命有时而泰。彼宋公修志以俟也。其复可立而须焉。时其族兄曰之望者。亦贾生之谪居。有顾君之画绝。伟公之貌。作为是图。意得神传。笔精形似。因命仆为赞。其词云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1365935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365935'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365935'>宋公卓荦，体标山岳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1365935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365935'>匪石不移，如玉斯琢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1365935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1365935'>被服忠信，规模礼乐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1365935'>望之俨然，允谓高邈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1365935_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1365935'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1365935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　冬，王昌龄贬岭南途中，有诗寄九龄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　卧病期间，有怀始兴南山旧居，企盼归老此处。作品：《始兴南山下有林泉尝卜居焉荆州卧病有怀此地》<div id='poem_22900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22900' class='poemTitle href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22900")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_22900_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_22900'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(284, "poem_allusion_22900")'>过隙</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5693, "poem_allusion_22900")'>履冰</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22900'>出处各有在，何者为陆沈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22900'>幸无迫贱事，聊可祛迷襟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22900'>世路少<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_22900", 22900, onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5693, "poem_sentence_3_22900")'>履冰</span>心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22900'>一跌不自保，万全焉可寻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22900'>行行念归路，眇眇惜光阴。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22900'>浮生如<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(284, "poem_sentence_6_22900")'>过隙</span>，先达已吾箴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22900'>敢忘丘山施，亦云年病侵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_22900'>力衰在所养，时谢良不任。<div id='poem_sentence_8_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_22900'>但忆旧栖息，愿言遂窥临。<div id='poem_sentence_9_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_22900'>云间日孤秀，山下面清深。<div id='poem_sentence_10_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_22900'>萝茑自为幄，风泉何必琴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_22900'>归此老吾老，还当日千金。<div id='poem_sentence_12_22900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_22900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_22900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>　是年在荆州长史。南归前，有送杨道士往天台诗。作品：《送杨道士往天台》<div id='poem_22788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_allusion_22788'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3629, "poem_allusion_22788")'>鬼谷子</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22788'>鬼谷还成道，天台去学仙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22788'>行应松子化，留与世人传。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22788'>此地烟波远，何时羽驾旋？<div id='poem_sentence_2_22788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22788'>当须一把袂，城郭共依然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_22788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>　是年在荆州长史。南归前，赠澧阳韦明府诗。作品：《赠澧阳韦明府》<div id='poem_22809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "poem_allusion_22809")'>武城鸡</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_22809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22809'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22809'>君有百鍊刃，堪断七重犀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22809'>谁开太阿匣，持割<span class='link' -----title
当阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1adb526258a641ce8d13a000362b23ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1adb526258a641ce8d13a000362b23ee");'><span id='1adb526258a641ce8d13a000362b23ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>，62岁</div><div id='1adb526258a641ce8d13a000362b23ee' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　春，巡县至当阳，有登临沮楼诗。作品：《登临沮楼》<div id='poem_22858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_22858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/22858?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登临沮楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（739年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15164, "唐", "张九龄", "poem_title_22858")'>张九龄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_22858_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_22858'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_22858'>高深不可厌，巡属复来过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_22858'>本与众山绝，况兹韶景和。<div id='poem_sentence_1_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_22858'>危楼入水倒，飞槛向空摩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_22858'>杂树缘青壁，樛枝挂绿萝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_22858'>潭清能彻底，鱼乐好跳波。<div id='poem_sentence_4_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_22858'>有象言虽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作难）</span>具，无端思转多。<div id='poem_sentence_5_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_22858'>同怀不在此，孤赏欲如何。<div id='poem_sentence_6_22858_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_22858'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_22858_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
